<?php

defined('_JEXEC') or die('Restricted access');

use Joomla\CMS\Factory;
use Joomla\CMS\Session\Session;
use Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri;

// Include Joomla authentication early, but only after Joomla access guard.
// Uses a __DIR__ lookup first, then falls back to the original relative include path for Sorcerer compatibility.
$authFile = realpath(__DIR__ . '/../joomla-auth.php');
if (!$authFile) {
    $authFile = realpath('../joomla-auth.php');
}
if ($authFile && is_readable($authFile)) {
    include $authFile;
}

// Define Joomla constants only if this file is executed in a context that needs them.
if (!defined('JPATH_BASE')) {
    define('JPATH_BASE', realpath(__DIR__ . '/../..'));
}

if (defined('JPATH_BASE')) {
    $definesFile   = JPATH_BASE . '/includes/defines.php';
    $frameworkFile = JPATH_BASE . '/includes/framework.php';

    if (is_readable($definesFile)) {
        require_once $definesFile;
    }

    if (is_readable($frameworkFile)) {
        require_once $frameworkFile;
    }
}

$app = Factory::getApplication();
$db  = Factory::getDbo();

// SEO values are prepared here but printed later inside the HTML [[head]].
// Do not echo tags before the document starts.
$canonicalUrl  = Uri::getInstance()->toString();
$pathWithQuery = Uri::getInstance()->toString(['path', 'query']);
$href          = 'https://lottoexpert.net' . $pathWithQuery;

/**
 * Single source of truth for the Lottery Game ID.
 * Change this one value, and all lookups will use it.
 */
// ─── DETERMINE GAME ID ──────────────────────────────
// Accept alphanumeric ID from URL. Supported parameter names:
//   ?gameId=145   (current hub links)
//   ?game_id=145  (legacy)
//   ?gid=145      (alias)
//   ?gmCode=145   (LottoExpert game code alias)
$rawId =
    (isset($_GET['gameId'])  ? trim((string) $_GET['gameId'])  : '') ?:
    (isset($_GET['game_id']) ? trim((string) $_GET['game_id']) : '') ?:
    (isset($_GET['gid'])     ? trim((string) $_GET['gid'])     : '') ?:
    (isset($_GET['gmCode'])  ? trim((string) $_GET['gmCode'])  : '');

// Validate: only letters and digits allowed; reject empty or unsafe input.
// Do NOT fall back silently to any default game -- show a safe error instead.
if ($rawId !== '' && preg_match('/^[A-Za-z0-9]+$/', $rawId)) {
    $gameId = $rawId;
} else {
    error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Missing or invalid game ID. rawId=' . preg_replace('/[^A-Za-z0-9_\-]/', '?', substr($rawId, 0, 32)));
    die(htmlspecialchars(
        'No game ID was specified. Please access this page via a valid lottery link (e.g. ?gameId=FL1).',
        ENT_QUOTES,
        'UTF-8'
    ));
}

// Get the current user BEFORE processing the save request
$currUser   = Factory::getUser();
$userGroups = $currUser->groups ?? [];

// Explicit fallback group if no specific rule exists for a game
$defaultGroups = [14];

// Explicit allowed groups per game (no merging, no auto-matching)
$gameGroups = [
    '101' => [10, 12, 13, 14],
  //  '113' => [14],
  //  '801' => [10, 12, 13, 14],
    // Add more as needed…
];

// Pick the right list of allowed groups
if (isset($gameGroups[$gameId])) {
    $allowedGroups = $gameGroups[$gameId];
} else {
    $allowedGroups = $defaultGroups;
}

// Guest check: only allow if group 1 is in allowed groups
if ($currUser->guest && in_array(1, $allowedGroups)) {
    $userIsInAllowedGroup = true;
} else {
    $userIsInAllowedGroup = !empty(array_intersect($allowedGroups, $userGroups));
}

/**
 * SAVE ENTITLEMENT GATE
 * Enthusiast (group 10) can save ONLY on Powerball (gameId 101).
 * Members (group 14) can save anywhere they are allowed to run analysis.
 */
$enthusiastGroupId = 10;   // Enthusiast plan
$powerballGameId   = '101';

$isEnthusiast = in_array($enthusiastGroupId, $userGroups, true);

// Allow save only if analysis is allowed AND (not enthusiast OR Powerball)
$userCanSave = $userIsInAllowedGroup && (!$isEnthusiast || (string)$gameId === $powerballGameId);

/**
 * Retrieve the next upcoming draw_date for a given lottery.
 *
 * @param   string $gameId     The lottery game ID (e.g. '101').
 * @param   object $db         Joomla database object.
 * @param   string $tableName  Resolved table name from config (e.g. '#__lotterydb_fl').
 * @return  string|null        Next draw_date (YYYY-MM-DD) or null if none.
 */

// ─── LOAD GAME SPEC FROM CONFIG FILES ────────────────────────────────────────
// Resolution order:
//   1. lottery_skip_config.json  (regular/jackpot games: US, UK, IE, CA, etc.)
//   2. dailylotteries.json       (daily Pick 3 / Pick 4 style games)
// all_game_rules.xml is consulted only for supplemental game-type metadata.
// tableName is NEVER accepted from URL input.
$configBase = '/home/oscara/web/lottoexpert.net/public_html/';
$foundSpec  = null;

// ── Normalise a lottery_skip_config.json entry into a unified spec ──
function normalizeSkipConfigSpec(array $entry) {
    $lc         = (isset($entry['lotteryConfig']) && is_array($entry['lotteryConfig']))
                    ? $entry['lotteryConfig']
                    : [];
    $hasExtra   = !empty($lc['has_extra_ball']) && isset($lc['num_extra_balls_drawn'])
                    && (int) $lc['num_extra_balls_drawn'] > 0;
    $extraCount = $hasExtra ? (int) $lc['num_extra_balls_drawn'] : 0;
    return [
        'gameId'         => isset($entry['gameId'])                    ? (string) $entry['gameId']                    : '',
        'gameName'       => isset($entry['lotteryName'])               ? (string) $entry['lotteryName']               : '',
        'tableName'      => isset($entry['dbCol'])                     ? (string) $entry['dbCol']                     : '',
        'pickSize'       => isset($lc['num_main_balls_drawn'])         ? (int) $lc['num_main_balls_drawn']            : 0,
        'rangeMain'      => isset($lc['max_main_ball_number'])         ? (int) $lc['max_main_ball_number']            : 0,
        'extraBallCount' => $extraCount,
        'rangeExtra'     => ($extraCount > 0 && isset($lc['max_extra_ball_number']))
                                ? (int) $lc['max_extra_ball_number']
                                : 0,
        'state'          => '',
        'training'       => [],
        '_source'        => 'lottery_skip_config',
    ];
}

// ── Normalise a dailylotteries.json entry into a unified spec ──
function normalizeDailySpec(array $entry) {
    $extraCount = isset($entry['extraBallCount']) ? (int) $entry['extraBallCount'] : 0;
    return [
        'gameId'         => isset($entry['gameId'])    ? (string) $entry['gameId']    : '',
        'gameName'       => isset($entry['label'])     ? (string) $entry['label']     : '',
        'tableName'      => isset($entry['tableName']) ? (string) $entry['tableName'] : '',
        'pickSize'       => isset($entry['pickSize'])  ? (int) $entry['pickSize']     : 0,
        'rangeMain'      => isset($entry['rangeMain']) ? (int) $entry['rangeMain']    : 0,
        'extraBallCount' => $extraCount,
        'rangeExtra'     => ($extraCount > 0 && isset($entry['rangeExtra']))
                                ? (int) $entry['rangeExtra']
                                : 0,
        'state'          => isset($entry['state']) ? (string) $entry['state'] : '',
        'training'       => (isset($entry['training']) && is_array($entry['training']))
                                ? $entry['training']
                                : [],
        '_source'        => 'dailylotteries',
    ];
}

$normalizedGameId = strtoupper(trim((string) $gameId));

// ── Step 1: Search lottery_skip_config.json ──
$skipConfigFile = realpath($configBase . 'lottery_skip_config.json');
if ($skipConfigFile && is_readable($skipConfigFile)) {
    $raw = file_get_contents($skipConfigFile);
    if ($raw !== false) {
        $decoded = json_decode($raw, true);
        if (json_last_error() === JSON_ERROR_NONE && is_array($decoded)) {
            // Games are stored under the "lotteries" key
            $gameMap = (isset($decoded['lotteries']) && is_array($decoded['lotteries']))
                ? $decoded['lotteries']
                : $decoded;
            foreach ($gameMap as $key => $entry) {
                if (!is_array($entry)) {
                    continue;
                }
                $entryId = strtoupper(trim((string) (isset($entry['gameId']) ? $entry['gameId'] : $key)));
                if ($entryId === $normalizedGameId) {
                    $foundSpec = normalizeSkipConfigSpec($entry);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

// ── Step 2: If not found, search dailylotteries.json ──
if (!$foundSpec) {
    $dailyFile = realpath($configBase . 'dailylotteries.json');
    if ($dailyFile && is_readable($dailyFile)) {
        $raw = file_get_contents($dailyFile);
        if ($raw !== false) {
            $decoded = json_decode($raw, true);
            if (json_last_error() === JSON_ERROR_NONE && is_array($decoded)) {
                $dailyList = [];
                if (isset($decoded['dailylotteries']) && is_array($decoded['dailylotteries'])) {
                    $dailyList = $decoded['dailylotteries'];
                } elseif (isset($decoded['lotteries']) && is_array($decoded['lotteries'])) {
                    $dailyList = $decoded['lotteries'];
                } elseif (!empty($decoded) && is_array(reset($decoded))) {
                    $dailyList = $decoded;
                }
                foreach ($dailyList as $entry) {
                    if (!is_array($entry)) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    $rawEntryId = isset($entry['gameId']) ? $entry['gameId']
                        : (isset($entry['game_id']) ? $entry['game_id'] : '');
                    $entryId = strtoupper(trim((string) $rawEntryId));
                    if ($entryId === $normalizedGameId) {
                        $foundSpec = normalizeDailySpec($entry);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

// ── Game not found in any config ──
if (!$foundSpec) {
    error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Game ID not resolved: ' . $gameId . ' (normalized: ' . $normalizedGameId . ')');
    die(htmlspecialchars(
        'Game ID ' . $gameId . ' was not found in any configuration file. ' .
        'Please verify the game ID is registered in lottery_skip_config.json or dailylotteries.json.',
        ENT_QUOTES,
        'UTF-8'
    ));
}

// ── Validate resolved spec ──
$tableName = $foundSpec['tableName'];
if (empty($tableName)) {
    error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Missing tableName for game: ' . $gameId);
    die(htmlspecialchars(
        'Configuration error: tableName is missing for game ID ' . $gameId . '.',
        ENT_QUOTES,
        'UTF-8'
    ));
}
if ((int) $foundSpec['pickSize'] <= 0 || (int) $foundSpec['rangeMain'] <= 0) {
    error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Invalid pickSize or rangeMain for game: ' . $gameId);
    die(htmlspecialchars(
        'Configuration error: invalid pickSize or rangeMain for game ID ' . $gameId . '.',
        ENT_QUOTES,
        'UTF-8'
    ));
}

// ── Derive jurisdiction / state label ──
// Multi-state numeric IDs (Powerball, Mega Millions, etc.)
$multiStateGameIds = ['101', '101D', '113', '113D', '132', '134', '135', '145'];
$isMultiState = in_array(strtoupper((string) $gameId), array_map('strtoupper', $multiStateGameIds), true);

function deriveJurisdiction($gid, $spec, $multiStateIds) {
    if (!empty($spec['state'])) {
        return (string) $spec['state'];
    }
    $upper = strtoupper(trim((string) $gid));
    $prefix2 = substr($upper, 0, 2);
    if (in_array($upper, array_map('strtoupper', $multiStateIds), true)) {
        return 'Multi-State';
    }
    if ($prefix2 === 'UK') { return 'United Kingdom'; }
    if ($prefix2 === 'IE') { return 'Ireland'; }
    // Canadian province prefixes
    $caProvinces = ['BC', 'AB', 'ON', 'MB', 'SK', 'QC', 'NS', 'NB', 'PE', 'NL', 'YT', 'NT', 'NU'];
    if (in_array($prefix2, $caProvinces, true)) { return 'Canada'; }
    return $prefix2;
}

$stateLabel = $isMultiState ? 'Multi-State' : deriveJurisdiction($gameId, $foundSpec, $multiStateGameIds);



// ─── NEW getNextDrawDate() ─────────────────────────────────────
// ─── NEW getNextDrawDate() ─────────────────────────────────────
/**
 * Retrieves the next non-blank next_draw_date, expanding #__ prefix.
 * Returns DATETIME (adds ' 00:00:00' if the source is DATE-only).
 */
function getNextDrawDate($gameId, $db, $tableName) {
    $tbl = $db->quoteName($db->replacePrefix($tableName));
    $q   = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select($db->quoteName('next_draw_date'))
        ->from($tbl)
        ->where($db->quoteName('game_id') . ' = ' . $db->quote($gameId))
        ->where($db->quoteName('next_draw_date') . ' IS NOT NULL')
        ->where($db->quoteName('next_draw_date') . " <> " . $db->quote('0000-00-00'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('next_draw_date') . " <> " . $db->quote('0000-00-00 00:00:00'))
        ->order($db->quoteName('draw_date') . ' DESC')
        ->setLimit(1);
    $db->setQuery($q);
    $val = $db->loadResult();

    // Normalize DATE to DATETIME for inserts downstream
    if (!empty($val) && preg_match('/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/', $val)) {
        $val .= ' 00:00:00';
    }
    return $val ?: null;
}


/**
 * Elite helper functions for secure save handling.
 */
function leIsAjaxRequest(): bool
{
    return isset($_SERVER['HTTP_X_REQUESTED_WITH'])
        && strtolower((string) $_SERVER['HTTP_X_REQUESTED_WITH']) === 'xmlhttprequest';
}

function leJsonResponse(bool $success, string $message, array $extra = []): void
{
    if (!headers_sent()) {
        header('Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8');
    }

    echo json_encode(
        array_merge(
            [
                'success' => $success,
                'message' => $message,
            ],
            $extra
        ),
        JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE
    );

    if (class_exists('Joomla\\CMS\\Factory')) {
        try {
            \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getApplication()->close();
        } catch (Throwable $e) {
            exit;
        }
    }

    exit;
}

function leFailSave($app, string $message): void
{
    if (leIsAjaxRequest()) {
        leJsonResponse(false, $message);
    }

    $app->enqueueMessage($message, 'error');
    $app->redirect(Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    exit;
}

function leSuccessSave($app, string $message, int $savedId = 0): void
{
    if (leIsAjaxRequest()) {
        leJsonResponse(true, $message, ['saved_id' => $savedId]);
    }

    $app->enqueueMessage($message, 'message');
    $app->redirect('/my-dashboard');
    exit;
}

function leCheckCsrfToken(): bool
{
    try {
        if (class_exists('Joomla\\CMS\\Session\\Session')) {
            return (bool) Session::checkToken('post');
        }
    } catch (Throwable $e) {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Session::checkToken failed: ' . $e->getMessage());
    }

    try {
        if (class_exists('JSession')) {
            return (bool) \JSession::checkToken('post');
        }
    } catch (Throwable $e) {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] JSession::checkToken failed: ' . $e->getMessage());
    }

    return false;
}

function leCleanText(string $value, int $maxLength = 120): string
{
    $value = trim(strip_tags($value));
    $value = preg_replace('/\s+/', ' ', $value) ?: '';

    if (function_exists('mb_substr')) {
        return mb_substr($value, 0, $maxLength, 'UTF-8');
    }

    return substr($value, 0, $maxLength);
}

function leCleanNumberList(string $value, int $maxItems, int $maxNumber, bool $allowEmpty = false): string
{
    $value = trim($value);

    if ($value === '') {
        return $allowEmpty ? '' : '';
    }

    // Accept only digits and commas; reject anything else (e.g. injection attempts).
    if (!preg_match('/^[\d,]+$/', $value)) {
        return '';
    }

    $parts = explode(',', $value);
    $clean = [];
    $seen  = [];

    foreach ($parts as $part) {
        $part = trim($part);
        if ($part === '') {
            continue; // skip empty segments from accidental double-commas
        }

        $num = (int) $part;

        if ($num < 1 || $num > $maxNumber) {
            // Skip individual out-of-range numbers instead of rejecting the
            // entire list.  The server still validates the final count below.
            continue;
        }

        if (isset($seen[$num])) {
            continue; // deduplicate silently
        }

        $seen[$num] = true;
        $clean[]    = (string) $num;

        // Check is after appending, so this breaks once we have exactly
        // $maxItems entries (correct truncation, not premature).
        if (count($clean) >= $maxItems) {
            break; // truncate at maxItems instead of rejecting the whole list
        }
    }

    if (!$allowEmpty && count($clean) === 0) {
        return '';
    }

    return implode(',', $clean);
}

function leClampInt($value, int $min, int $max, int $fallback): int
{
    $value = filter_var($value, FILTER_VALIDATE_INT);

    if ($value === false || $value < $min || $value > $max) {
        return $fallback;
    }

    return (int) $value;
}

function leClampFloat($value, float $min, float $max, float $fallback): float
{
    $value = filter_var($value, FILTER_VALIDATE_FLOAT);

    if ($value === false || $value < $min || $value > $max) {
        return $fallback;
    }

    return (float) $value;
}

function leCleanDateTimeForDb(string $value): string
{
    $value = trim($value);

    if (preg_match('/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2} \d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2}$/', $value)) {
        return $value;
    }

    return date('Y-m-d H:i:s');
}


function leCleanDateForDbNullable(string $value): ?string
{
    $value = trim($value);

    if ($value === '') {
        return null;
    }

    if (preg_match('/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/', $value)) {
        return $value . ' 00:00:00';
    }

    if (preg_match('/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2} \d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2}$/', $value)) {
        return $value;
    }

    return null;
}

function leCleanHash(string $value): string
{
    $value = strtolower(trim($value));
    return preg_match('/^[a-f0-9]{64}$/', $value) ? $value : '';
}

function leCleanRunUuid(string $value): string
{
    $value = strtolower(trim($value));
    return preg_match('/^[a-f0-9]{8}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[1-5][a-f0-9]{3}-[89ab][a-f0-9]{3}-[a-f0-9]{12}$/', $value)
        ? $value
        : '';
}

function leGenerateUuidV4(): string
{
    try {
        $data = random_bytes(16);
        $data[6] = chr((ord($data[6]) & 0x0f) | 0x40);
        $data[8] = chr((ord($data[8]) & 0x3f) | 0x80);
        return vsprintf('%s%s-%s-%s-%s-%s%s%s', str_split(bin2hex($data), 4));
    } catch (Throwable $e) {
        return sprintf(
            '%04x%04x-%04x-4%03x-%04x-%04x%04x%04x',
            mt_rand(0, 0xffff),
            mt_rand(0, 0xffff),
            mt_rand(0, 0xffff),
            mt_rand(0, 0x0fff),
            mt_rand(0x8000, 0xbfff),
            mt_rand(0, 0xffff),
            mt_rand(0, 0xffff),
            mt_rand(0, 0xffff)
        );
    }
}


/**
 * Core AI learning handoff helpers.
 * These keep the save pipeline backward-compatible while allowing MyLottoExpert
 * to read richer evidence when the matching optional columns exist.
 */
function leCleanTechnicalKey(string $value, int $maxLength = 64): string
{
    $value = strtolower(trim($value));
    $value = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9_\-\.]/', '', $value) ?: '';
    if (function_exists('mb_substr')) {
        return mb_substr($value, 0, $maxLength, 'UTF-8');
    }
    return substr($value, 0, $maxLength);
}

function leCleanJsonPayload(string $value, int $maxLength = 30000): string
{
    $value = trim($value);
    if ($value === '' || strlen($value) > $maxLength) {
        return '';
    }

    $decoded = json_decode($value, true);
    if (json_last_error() !== JSON_ERROR_NONE || !is_array($decoded)) {
        return '';
    }

    $encoded = json_encode($decoded, JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE);
    return is_string($encoded) ? $encoded : '';
}


/**
 * Simple production save recovery:
 * Pull a clean comma-separated number list from Core AI JSON payloads when the
 * browser submits before the visible hidden CSV fields are populated.
 */
function leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload(string $value, int $maxItems, int $maxNumber): string
{
    $value = trim($value);
    if ($value === '' || strlen($value) > 60000) {
        return '';
    }

    $decoded = json_decode($value, true);
    if (json_last_error() !== JSON_ERROR_NONE || !is_array($decoded)) {
        return '';
    }

    $clean = [];
    $seen  = [];

    $pushNumber = function ($candidate) use (&$clean, &$seen, $maxItems, $maxNumber): void {
        if (count($clean) >= $maxItems) {
            return;
        }
        if (is_array($candidate)) {
            if (isset($candidate['number'])) {
                $candidate = $candidate['number'];
            } elseif (isset($candidate['num'])) {
                $candidate = $candidate['num'];
            } elseif (isset($candidate['value'])) {
                $candidate = $candidate['value'];
            } else {
                return;
            }
        }
        $n = filter_var($candidate, FILTER_VALIDATE_INT);
        if ($n === false || $n < 1 || $n > $maxNumber || isset($seen[$n])) {
            return;
        }
        $seen[$n] = true;
        $clean[] = (string) $n;
    };

    $pushFromList = function ($list) use (&$pushNumber, &$clean, $maxItems): void {
        if (!is_array($list)) {
            return;
        }
        foreach ($list as $item) {
            if (count($clean) >= $maxItems) {
                break;
            }
            $pushNumber($item);
        }
    };

    // Preferred Core AI display payload shape: { numbers:[...], ranked:[{number:...}] }
    if (isset($decoded['numbers']) && is_array($decoded['numbers'])) {
        $pushFromList($decoded['numbers']);
        if (!empty($clean)) {
            return implode(',', $clean);
        }
    }

    // Preferred ranked payload shape: [{rank:1, number:12, ...}, ...]
    if (array_keys($decoded) === range(0, count($decoded) - 1)) {
        $pushFromList($decoded);
        if (!empty($clean)) {
            return implode(',', $clean);
        }
    }

    // Secondary display payload shape: { ranked:[{number:...}] }
    if (isset($decoded['ranked']) && is_array($decoded['ranked'])) {
        $pushFromList($decoded['ranked']);
        if (!empty($clean)) {
            return implode(',', $clean);
        }
    }

    // Final compatibility pass for any nested {numbers:[...]} block.
    foreach ($decoded as $item) {
        if (count($clean) >= $maxItems) {
            break;
        }
        if (is_array($item) && isset($item['numbers']) && is_array($item['numbers'])) {
            $pushFromList($item['numbers']);
        }
    }

    return implode(',', $clean);
}

function leBuildCoreAiPredictionTarget(int $lotteryId, string $gameId, ?string $nextDraw, int $pickSize, int $extraCount): array
{
    $drawDate = '';
    if (!empty($nextDraw)) {
        $ts = strtotime($nextDraw);
        if ($ts !== false && $ts > 0) {
            $drawDate = date('Y-m-d', $ts);
        }
    }

    $canonicalKey = strtolower(trim(implode('-', [
        $lotteryId > 0 ? (string) $lotteryId : '0',
        'core-ai',
        $drawDate !== '' ? $drawDate : 'undated',
        'regular',
    ]), '-'));

    if ($canonicalKey === '') {
        $canonicalKey = '0-core-ai-undated-regular';
    }

    $targetId = 'ptg_' . substr(hash('sha256', $canonicalKey), 0, 40);
    $payload = [
        'prediction_target_id' => $targetId,
        'canonical_key'        => $canonicalKey,
        'game_id'              => $gameId !== '' ? $gameId : null,
        'lottery_id'           => $lotteryId > 0 ? $lotteryId : null,
        'draw_date'            => $drawDate !== '' ? $drawDate : null,
        'draw_session'         => 'regular',
        'timezone_id'          => 'America/New_York',
        'prediction_family'    => 'core_ai',
        'prediction_type'      => 'core_ai_foundation',
        'pick_size'            => $pickSize > 0 ? $pickSize : null,
        'extra_count'          => $extraCount >= 0 ? $extraCount : 0,
    ];

    return [
        'prediction_target_id'     => $targetId,
        'prediction_target_key'    => $canonicalKey,
        'prediction_target_json'   => json_encode($payload, JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE),
        'target_game_id'           => $gameId,
        'target_lottery_id'        => $lotteryId,
        'target_draw_date'         => $drawDate,
        'target_draw_session'      => 'regular',
        'target_timezone_id'       => 'America/New_York',
        'target_prediction_family' => 'core_ai',
        'target_prediction_type'   => 'core_ai_foundation',
        'target_pick_size'         => $pickSize,
        'target_extra_count'       => $extraCount,
    ];
}

function leNormalizeDecimalForHash(float $value, int $precision): string
{
    $out = number_format($value, $precision, '.', '');
    $out = rtrim(rtrim($out, '0'), '.');
    return $out === '' ? '0' : $out;
}

function leBuildClientCanonicalString(array $payload): string
{
    $orderedKeys = [
        'payload_version',
        'run_uuid',
        'game_id',
        'lottery_id',
        'main_numbers',
        'extra_ball_numbers',
        'draws_analyzed',
        'generated_at',
        'latest_draw_date',
        'mode_key',
        'epochs',
        'batch_size',
        'dropout_rate',
        'learning_rate',
        'activation_function',
        'hidden_layers',
        'recency_decay',
        'model_version',
        'tfjs_version',
    ];

    $parts = [];
    foreach ($orderedKeys as $key) {
        $value = isset($payload[$key]) ? (string) $payload[$key] : '';
        $parts[] = str_replace('|', '/', $value);
    }

    return implode('|', $parts);
}

function leGetTableColumns($db, string $tableName): array
{
    static $cache = [];
    $resolved = $db->replacePrefix($tableName);

    if (isset($cache[$resolved])) {
        return $cache[$resolved];
    }

    try {
        $db->setQuery('SHOW COLUMNS FROM ' . $db->quoteName($resolved));
        $rows = $db->loadObjectList();
    } catch (Throwable $e) {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Could not inspect table columns for ' . $resolved . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
        $cache[$resolved] = [];
        return [];
    }

    $columns = [];
    foreach ($rows as $row) {
        if (isset($row->Field)) {
            $columns[(string) $row->Field] = true;
        }
    }

    $cache[$resolved] = $columns;
    return $columns;
}

function leAppendColumnIfExists(array &$columns, array &$values, array $availableColumns, string $column, string $sqlValue): void
{
    if (isset($availableColumns[$column])) {
        $columns[] = $column;
        $values[]  = $sqlValue;
    }
}

/**
 * Core AI first-run schema installer.
 *
 * Your live database prefix is jos9d_. Joomla's #__ prefix is still respected
 * through $db->getPrefix(), with jos9d_ used as a defensive fallback. This
 * function quietly creates the optional learning/evidence columns required for
 * the Core AI -> MyLottoExpert handoff. It is safe to run on every page load:
 * it checks INFORMATION_SCHEMA before each ALTER and never blocks analysis if
 * a hosting permission or duplicate-index race condition occurs.
 */
function leEnsureCoreAiSavedNumberColumns($db): bool
{
    $prefix = '';
    try {
        $prefix = (string) $db->getPrefix();
    } catch (Throwable $e) {
        $prefix = '';
    }

    if ($prefix === '') {
        $prefix = 'jos9d_';
    }

    $rawName = $prefix . 'user_saved_numbers';

    $columnExists = function (string $column) use ($db, $rawName): bool {
        try {
            $db->setQuery(
                'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS'
                . ' WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE()'
                . ' AND TABLE_NAME = ' . $db->quote($rawName)
                . ' AND COLUMN_NAME = ' . $db->quote($column)
            );
            return (int) $db->loadResult() > 0;
        } catch (Throwable $e) {
            error_log('[Core AI] Column check failed for ' . $rawName . '.' . $column . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
            return true;
        }
    };

    $indexExists = function (string $indexName) use ($db, $rawName): bool {
        try {
            $db->setQuery(
                'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.STATISTICS'
                . ' WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE()'
                . ' AND TABLE_NAME = ' . $db->quote($rawName)
                . ' AND INDEX_NAME = ' . $db->quote($indexName)
            );
            return (int) $db->loadResult() > 0;
        } catch (Throwable $e) {
            error_log('[Core AI] Index check failed for ' . $rawName . '.' . $indexName . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
            return true;
        }
    };

    $columnsToAdd = [
        'run_uuid'                   => "CHAR(36) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'analysis_run_uuid'          => "CHAR(36) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'analysis_method_key'        => "VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'core_ai'",
        'analysis_engine_label'      => "VARCHAR(80) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'LottoExpert Core AI'",
        'analysis_track_label'       => "VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Core AI Precision Lock Track'",
        'analysis_source_page'       => "VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'core_ai'",
        'analysis_schema_version'    => "VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1'",
        'game_id'                    => "VARCHAR(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'latest_draw_date'           => "DATETIME NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'mode_key'                   => "VARCHAR(40) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'model_version'              => "VARCHAR(80) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'tfjs_version'               => "VARCHAR(40) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'browser_engine'             => "VARCHAR(190) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'client_result_hash'         => "CHAR(64) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'client_hash'                => "CHAR(64) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'server_validation_hash'     => "CHAR(64) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'result_hash'                => "CHAR(64) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'origin_source'              => "VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT ''",
        'save_intent'                => "VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'prediction_archive'",
        'play_status'                => "VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'archived'",
        'model_family'               => "VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'core_ai'",
        'risk_profile'               => "VARCHAR(40) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'strategy_profile'           => "VARCHAR(40) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'batch_type'                 => "VARCHAR(64) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'batch_uuid'                 => "CHAR(36) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'batch_index'                => "INT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'batch_total'                => "INT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'settings_json'              => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'settings'                   => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'ranked_main_numbers_json'   => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'ranked_extra_numbers_json'  => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'regular_main_numbers_json'  => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'regular_extra_numbers_json' => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'main_display_json'          => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'extra_display_json'         => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'prediction_target_id'       => "VARCHAR(64) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'prediction_target_key'      => "VARCHAR(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'prediction_target_json'     => "MEDIUMTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_game_id'             => "VARCHAR(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_lottery_id'          => "INT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_draw_date'           => "DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_draw_at'             => "DATETIME NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_draw_session'        => "VARCHAR(40) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_timezone_id'         => "VARCHAR(64) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_prediction_family'   => "VARCHAR(30) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_prediction_type'     => "VARCHAR(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_pick_size'           => "INT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'target_extra_count'         => "INT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
        'user_editable'              => "TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1",
        'play_notes'                 => "TEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL",
    ];

    foreach ($columnsToAdd as $column => $definition) {
        if ($columnExists($column)) {
            continue;
        }
        try {
            $db->setQuery('ALTER TABLE ' . $db->quoteName($rawName) . ' ADD COLUMN ' . $db->quoteName($column) . ' ' . $definition);
            $db->execute();
        } catch (Throwable $e) {
            error_log('[Core AI] Could not add column ' . $rawName . '.' . $column . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
        }
    }

    $indexesToAdd = [
        'idx_core_ai_run_uuid'      => ['run_uuid'],
        'idx_core_ai_batch_uuid'    => ['batch_uuid'],
        'idx_core_ai_target'        => ['prediction_target_id'],
        'idx_core_ai_target_draw'   => ['target_game_id', 'target_draw_date'],
        'idx_core_ai_source_family' => ['source', 'model_family'],
        'idx_core_ai_method_key'    => ['analysis_method_key'],
        'idx_core_ai_method_target' => ['analysis_method_key', 'target_game_id', 'target_draw_date'],
        'idx_core_ai_client_hash'   => ['client_result_hash'],
    ];

    foreach ($indexesToAdd as $indexName => $indexColumns) {
        if ($indexExists($indexName)) {
            continue;
        }
        $missingIndexColumn = false;
        foreach ($indexColumns as $idxColumn) {
            if (!$columnExists($idxColumn)) {
                $missingIndexColumn = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if ($missingIndexColumn) {
            continue;
        }
        try {
            $quotedColumns = array_map([$db, 'quoteName'], $indexColumns);
            $db->setQuery('ALTER TABLE ' . $db->quoteName($rawName) . ' ADD INDEX ' . $db->quoteName($indexName) . ' (' . implode(',', $quotedColumns) . ')');
            $db->execute();
        } catch (Throwable $e) {
            error_log('[Core AI] Could not add index ' . $rawName . '.' . $indexName . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
        }
    }

    return true;
}

// First-run learning schema installer for jos9d_user_saved_numbers.
leEnsureCoreAiSavedNumberColumns($db);


// SIMPLE CORE AI SAVE ENDPOINT
// This intentionally mirrors the older working behavior: if completed prediction
// numbers are posted, save them. No client hash, run UUID, or delayed hidden-field
// dependency is required for this batch endpoint.
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['save_set']) && isset($_POST['core_ai_simple_save'])) {
    if (!leCheckCsrfToken()) {
        leFailSave($app, 'Security token expired. Please refresh the page and try again.');
    }

    if (!$userCanSave) {
        leFailSave($app, 'You are not authorized to save predictions for this game.');
    }

    $lotteryRaw = filter_input(INPUT_POST, 'lottery_id', FILTER_VALIDATE_INT);
    $lottery    = ($lotteryRaw !== false && $lotteryRaw !== null) ? (int) $lotteryRaw : 0;
    if ($lottery <= 0) {
        leFailSave($app, 'Invalid lottery ID. Please reload the page and try again.');
    }

    // Keep the important game safety check, but do not use this as a timing/security gate.
    $verifyQuery = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select($db->quoteName('game_id'))
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__lotteries'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('lottery_id') . ' = ' . (int) $lottery)
        ->setLimit(1);
    $db->setQuery($verifyQuery);
    $postedGameId = (string) $db->loadResult();
    if ($postedGameId === '' || strtoupper($postedGameId) !== strtoupper((string) $gameId)) {
        error_log('[Core AI Simple Save] Lottery verification failed. posted=' . $postedGameId . ' resolved=' . $gameId);
        leFailSave($app, 'Lottery verification failed. Please reload the page and try again.');
    }

    $saveMainMax      = (int) ($foundSpec['rangeMain'] ?? 0);
    $saveExtraCount   = (int) ($foundSpec['extraBallCount'] ?? 0);
    $saveHasExtraBall = $saveExtraCount > 0;
    $saveExtraMax     = $saveHasExtraBall ? (int) ($foundSpec['rangeExtra'] ?? 0) : 0;
    if ($saveMainMax <= 0) {
        leFailSave($app, 'Game configuration is missing a valid main number range.');
    }

    $mainNumbers = leCleanNumberList((string) ($_POST['main_numbers'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax, false);
    if ($mainNumbers === '') { $mainNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['simple_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax); }
    if ($mainNumbers === '') { $mainNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['core_ai_snapshot_json'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax); }
    if ($mainNumbers === '') { $mainNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['ranked_main_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax); }
    if ($mainNumbers === '') { $mainNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['main_display_json'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax); }

    if ($mainNumbers === '') {
        error_log('[Core AI Simple Save] Missing main numbers. posted_main=' . substr((string)($_POST['main_numbers'] ?? ''), 0, 200));
        leJsonResponse(false, 'Simple save failed: no prediction numbers were posted.', [
            'debug_code' => 'missing_main_numbers',
            'posted_main_numbers' => substr((string)($_POST['main_numbers'] ?? ''), 0, 200),
            'has_simple_numbers_json' => !empty($_POST['simple_numbers_json']) ? 1 : 0,
            'has_snapshot_json' => !empty($_POST['core_ai_snapshot_json']) ? 1 : 0,
            'has_ranked_main_json' => !empty($_POST['ranked_main_numbers_json']) ? 1 : 0,
            'has_main_display_json' => !empty($_POST['main_display_json']) ? 1 : 0,
        ]);
    }

    $extraNumbers = '';
    if ($saveHasExtraBall && $saveExtraMax > 0) {
        $extraNumbers = leCleanNumberList((string) ($_POST['extra_ball_numbers'] ?? ''), 5, $saveExtraMax, true);
        if ($extraNumbers === '') { $extraNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['simple_extra_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 5, $saveExtraMax); }
        if ($extraNumbers === '') { $extraNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['ranked_extra_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 5, $saveExtraMax); }
        if ($extraNumbers === '') { $extraNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['extra_display_json'] ?? ''), 5, $saveExtraMax); }
    }

    $source = 'ai_prediction';
    $label = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['label'] ?? ''), 140);
    if ($label === '') { $label = 'LottoExpert Core AI Prediction - ' . date('M j, Y'); }

    $countRaw = filter_input(INPUT_POST, 'draws_analyzed', FILTER_VALIDATE_INT);
    $count = ($countRaw !== false && $countRaw !== null && (int)$countRaw >= 0) ? (int)$countRaw : 0;
    $generatedAt = leCleanDateTimeForDb((string) ($_POST['generated_at'] ?? ''));

    $epochs = leClampInt($_POST['epochs'] ?? null, 1, 2000, 200);
    $batchSize = leClampInt($_POST['batch_size'] ?? null, 1, 512, 32);
    $dropout = leClampFloat($_POST['dropout_rate'] ?? null, 0.0, 0.8, 0.2);
    $lr = leClampFloat($_POST['learning_rate'] ?? null, 0.00001, 0.1, 0.001);
    $activationFunctionPosted = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['activation_function'] ?? ''), 20);
    $activationFunctionSaved = in_array($activationFunctionPosted, ['relu','sigmoid','tanh'], true) ? $activationFunctionPosted : 'relu';
    $layers = leClampInt($_POST['hidden_layers'] ?? null, 1, 10, 3);
    $recencyDecay = leClampFloat($_POST['recency_decay'] ?? null, 0.0, 1.0, 0.95);

    $nextDraw = getNextDrawDate($postedGameId, $db, $tableName);

    $columns = [
        'user_id','lottery_id','main_numbers','extra_ball_numbers','source','label',
        'draws_analyzed','generated_at','date_saved','next_draw_date','epochs','batch_size',
        'dropout_rate','learning_rate','activation_function','hidden_layers','recency_decay'
    ];
    $values = [
        (int)$currUser->id,
        (int)$lottery,
        $db->quote($mainNumbers),
        $db->quote($extraNumbers),
        $db->quote($source),
        $db->quote($label),
        (int)$count,
        $db->quote($generatedAt),
        $db->quote(date('Y-m-d H:i:s')),
        $nextDraw !== null ? $db->quote($nextDraw) : 'NULL',
        (int)$epochs,
        (int)$batchSize,
        (float)$dropout,
        (float)$lr,
        $db->quote($activationFunctionSaved),
        (int)$layers,
        (float)$recencyDecay,
    ];

    $availableSaveColumns = leGetTableColumns($db, '#__user_saved_numbers');
    $runUuid = leCleanRunUuid((string) ($_POST['run_uuid'] ?? ''));
    if ($runUuid === '') { $runUuid = leGenerateUuidV4(); }
    $batchUuid = leCleanRunUuid((string) ($_POST['batch_uuid'] ?? ''));
    if ($batchUuid === '') { $batchUuid = $runUuid; }
    $batchType = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['batch_type'] ?? 'core_ai_precision_lock_9_batch'), 64);
    $modeKey = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['mode_key'] ?? 'balanced'), 40);
    $riskProfile = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['risk_profile'] ?? $modeKey), 40);
    $strategyProfile = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['strategy_profile'] ?? $modeKey), 40);
    $batchIndex = leClampInt($_POST['batch_index'] ?? null, 0, 999, 0);
    $batchTotal = leClampInt($_POST['batch_total'] ?? null, 0, 999, 0);

    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'run_uuid', $db->quote($runUuid));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_run_uuid', $db->quote($runUuid));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_method_key', $db->quote('core_ai'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_engine_label', $db->quote('LottoExpert Core AI'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_track_label', $db->quote('Core AI Precision Lock Track'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_source_page', $db->quote('core_ai'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_schema_version', $db->quote('simple-v12'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'game_id', $db->quote((string)$gameId));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'mode_key', $db->quote($modeKey));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'origin_source', $db->quote('core_ai'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'save_intent', $db->quote('prediction_archive'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'play_status', $db->quote('archived'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'model_family', $db->quote('core_ai'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'risk_profile', $db->quote($riskProfile));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'strategy_profile', $db->quote($strategyProfile));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_type', $db->quote($batchType));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_uuid', $db->quote($batchUuid));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_index', (int)$batchIndex);
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_total', (int)$batchTotal);
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'settings_json', !empty($_POST['settings_json']) ? $db->quote(leCleanJsonPayload((string)$_POST['settings_json'], 30000)) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'settings', !empty($_POST['settings_json']) ? $db->quote(leCleanJsonPayload((string)$_POST['settings_json'], 30000)) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'ranked_main_numbers_json', !empty($_POST['ranked_main_numbers_json']) ? $db->quote(leCleanJsonPayload((string)$_POST['ranked_main_numbers_json'], 30000)) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'ranked_extra_numbers_json', !empty($_POST['ranked_extra_numbers_json']) ? $db->quote(leCleanJsonPayload((string)$_POST['ranked_extra_numbers_json'], 16000)) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'main_display_json', !empty($_POST['main_display_json']) ? $db->quote(leCleanJsonPayload((string)$_POST['main_display_json'], 30000)) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'extra_display_json', !empty($_POST['extra_display_json']) ? $db->quote(leCleanJsonPayload((string)$_POST['extra_display_json'], 16000)) : 'NULL');

    $insertQuery = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
        ->columns($db->quoteName($columns))
        ->values(implode(',', $values));
    try {
        $db->setQuery($insertQuery);
        $db->execute();
        $savedId = 0;
        try { $savedId = (int) $db->insertid(); } catch (Throwable $idError) { $savedId = 0; }
        leJsonResponse(true, 'Number set saved successfully.', [
            'saved_id' => $savedId,
            'simple_save' => 1,
            'main_numbers_saved' => $mainNumbers,
        ]);
    } catch (Throwable $e) {
        error_log('[Core AI Simple Save] Insert failed: ' . $e->getMessage());
        leJsonResponse(false, 'Simple save insert failed: ' . $e->getMessage(), ['debug_code' => 'insert_failed']);
    }
}

// PROCESS SAVE PREDICTION SET
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['save_set'])) {
    if (!leCheckCsrfToken()) {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Save rejected: invalid or missing CSRF token.');
        leFailSave($app, 'Security token expired. Please refresh the page and try again.');
    }

    if (!$userCanSave) {
        leFailSave($app, 'You are not authorized to save predictions for this game.');
    }

    $lotteryRaw = filter_input(INPUT_POST, 'lottery_id', FILTER_VALIDATE_INT);
    $lottery    = ($lotteryRaw !== false && $lotteryRaw !== null) ? (int) $lotteryRaw : 0;

    if ($lottery <= 0) {
        leFailSave($app, 'Invalid lottery ID. Please reload the page and try again.');
    }

    // Verify posted lottery_id belongs to the current resolved gameId.
    $verifyQuery = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select($db->quoteName('game_id'))
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__lotteries'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('lottery_id') . ' = ' . (int) $lottery)
        ->setLimit(1);

    $db->setQuery($verifyQuery);
    $postedGameId = (string) $db->loadResult();

    if ($postedGameId === '' || strtoupper($postedGameId) !== strtoupper((string) $gameId)) {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Save rejected: posted lottery_id does not match resolved gameId. posted=' . $postedGameId . ' resolved=' . $gameId);
        leFailSave($app, 'Lottery verification failed. Please reload the page and try again.');
    }

    $saveMainMax      = (int) ($foundSpec['rangeMain'] ?? 0);
    $saveExtraCount   = (int) ($foundSpec['extraBallCount'] ?? 0);
    $saveHasExtraBall = $saveExtraCount > 0;
    $saveExtraMax     = $saveHasExtraBall ? (int) ($foundSpec['rangeExtra'] ?? 0) : 0;

    if ($saveMainMax <= 0) {
        leFailSave($app, 'Game configuration is missing a valid main number range.');
    }

    $source = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['source'] ?? 'ai_prediction'), 40);
    if ($source !== 'ai_prediction') {
        $source = 'ai_prediction';
    }

    $label = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['label'] ?? ''), 140);
    if ($label === '') {
        $label = 'LottoExpert AI Prediction - ' . date('M j, Y');
    }

    $mainNumbers = leCleanNumberList(
        (string) ($_POST['main_numbers'] ?? ''),
        20,
        $saveMainMax,
        false
    );

    // Simple save recovery: batch runs may submit before saveMainNumbers is filled.
    // Recover from the deterministic Core AI snapshot first, then ranked/display JSON.
    if ($mainNumbers === '') {
        $mainNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['core_ai_snapshot_json'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax);
    }
    if ($mainNumbers === '') {
        $mainNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['ranked_main_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax);
    }
    if ($mainNumbers === '') {
        $mainNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['main_display_json'] ?? ''), 20, $saveMainMax);
    }

    if ($mainNumbers === '') {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Simple save rejected: no main numbers in CSV or Core AI JSON payload.');
        leFailSave($app, 'Please run the AI analysis before saving.');
    }

    $extraNumbers = '';
    if ($saveHasExtraBall && $saveExtraMax > 0) {
        $extraNumbers = leCleanNumberList(
            (string) ($_POST['extra_ball_numbers'] ?? ''),
            5,
            $saveExtraMax,
            true
        );
        if ($extraNumbers === '') {
            $extraNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['ranked_extra_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 5, $saveExtraMax);
        }
        if ($extraNumbers === '') {
            $extraNumbers = leRecoverNumberListFromJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['extra_display_json'] ?? ''), 5, $saveExtraMax);
        }
    }

    $countRaw = filter_input(INPUT_POST, 'draws_analyzed', FILTER_VALIDATE_INT);
    $count    = ($countRaw !== false && $countRaw !== null && (int) $countRaw >= 0) ? (int) $countRaw : 0;

    // Accept 0 as a valid sentinel when the client hasn't supplied the count yet.
    // Only reject clearly impossible values (> 1 million rows).
    if ($count < 0 || $count > 1000000) {
        leFailSave($app, 'Invalid draw count. Please reload the page and try again.');
    }

    $generatedAt = leCleanDateTimeForDb((string) ($_POST['generated_at'] ?? ''));

    $epochs = leClampInt($_POST['epochs'] ?? null, 1, 2000, 200);
    $batchSize = leClampInt($_POST['batch_size'] ?? null, 1, 512, 32);
    $dropout = leClampFloat($_POST['dropout_rate'] ?? null, 0.0, 0.8, 0.2);
    $lr = leClampFloat($_POST['learning_rate'] ?? null, 0.00001, 0.1, 0.001);

    $activationFunctionPosted = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['activation_function'] ?? ''), 20);
    $allowedActivations       = ['relu', 'sigmoid', 'tanh'];
    $activationFunctionSaved  = in_array($activationFunctionPosted, $allowedActivations, true)
        ? $activationFunctionPosted
        : 'relu';

    $layers = leClampInt($_POST['hidden_layers'] ?? null, 1, 10, 3);
    $recencyDecay = leClampFloat($_POST['recency_decay'] ?? null, 0.0, 1.0, 0.95);


    // Phase 2: client-side computation integrity metadata.
    // Production batch-save relaxation:
    // Single-run manual saves remain strict. Core AI batch saves can recover a missing
    // browser run UUID/hash because the browser may finish training and populate
    // numbers before the async integrity hash finishes. Server-side authority still
    // validates Joomla token, entitlement, lottery/game match, number ranges, draw
    // count, and draw target before insert.
    $postedBatchTypeForIntegrity = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['batch_type'] ?? ''), 64);
    $isCoreAiBatchSave = in_array($postedBatchTypeForIntegrity, [
        'core_ai_precision_lock_9_batch',
        'core_ai_range_test_9_batch',
        'core_ai_precision_lock_batch',
        'core_ai_batch',
    ], true);

    $runUuid = leCleanRunUuid((string) ($_POST['run_uuid'] ?? ''));
    if ($runUuid === '') {
        $runUuid = leGenerateUuidV4();
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Simple save recovered missing/invalid run_uuid. generated=' . $runUuid);
    }

    $clientResultHash = leCleanHash((string) ($_POST['client_result_hash'] ?? ''));
    $clientHashWasRecovered = false;

    $modeKey = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['mode_key'] ?? 'balanced'), 40);
    $allowedModes = ['balanced', 'mixed', 'ai-forward', 'skip-dominant', 'explorative', 'conservative'];
    if (!in_array($modeKey, $allowedModes, true)) {
        $modeKey = 'balanced';
    }

    $modelVersion = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['model_version'] ?? 'legacy-tfjs-client-v2'), 60);
    if ($modelVersion === '') {
        $modelVersion = 'legacy-tfjs-client-v2';
    }

    $tfjsVersion = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['tfjs_version'] ?? ''), 40);
    $browserEngine = leCleanText((string) ($_POST['browser_engine'] ?? ''), 160);
    // Core AI -> MyLottoExpert technical learning handoff.
    $originSource = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['origin_source'] ?? 'core_ai'), 32);
    if ($originSource === '') { $originSource = 'core_ai'; }

    $saveIntent = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['save_intent'] ?? 'prediction_archive'), 32);
    if ($saveIntent === '') { $saveIntent = 'prediction_archive'; }

    $playStatus = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['play_status'] ?? 'archived'), 32);
    if ($playStatus === '') { $playStatus = 'archived'; }

    $modelFamily = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['model_family'] ?? 'core_ai'), 32);
    if ($modelFamily === '') { $modelFamily = 'core_ai'; }

    $riskProfile = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['risk_profile'] ?? $modeKey), 40);
    $strategyProfile = leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['strategy_profile'] ?? $modeKey), 40);
    $batchType = $postedBatchTypeForIntegrity !== ''
        ? $postedBatchTypeForIntegrity
        : leCleanTechnicalKey((string) ($_POST['batch_type'] ?? 'single_core_ai_run'), 64);
    if ($batchType === '') { $batchType = 'single_core_ai_run'; }

    $batchUuid = leCleanRunUuid((string) ($_POST['batch_uuid'] ?? ''));
    $batchIndex = leClampInt($_POST['batch_index'] ?? null, 0, 999, 0);
    $batchTotal = leClampInt($_POST['batch_total'] ?? null, 0, 999, 0);

    $settingsJson = leCleanJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['settings_json'] ?? ''), 30000);
    $rankedMainJson = leCleanJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['ranked_main_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 30000);
    $rankedExtraJson = leCleanJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['ranked_extra_numbers_json'] ?? ''), 16000);
    $mainDisplayJson = leCleanJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['main_display_json'] ?? ''), 30000);
    $extraDisplayJson = leCleanJsonPayload((string) ($_POST['extra_display_json'] ?? ''), 16000);

    $latestDrawDateForHash = leCleanDateForDbNullable((string) ($_POST['latest_draw_date'] ?? ''));
    $latestDrawDateCanonical = $latestDrawDateForHash ? substr($latestDrawDateForHash, 0, 10) : '';

    $clientCanonicalPayload = [
        'payload_version'      => 'le-client-v2',
        'run_uuid'            => $runUuid,
        'game_id'             => (string) $gameId,
        'lottery_id'          => (string) $lottery,
        'main_numbers'        => $mainNumbers,
        'extra_ball_numbers'  => $extraNumbers,
        'draws_analyzed'      => (string) $count,
        'generated_at'        => $generatedAt,
        'latest_draw_date'    => $latestDrawDateCanonical,
        'mode_key'            => $modeKey,
        'epochs'              => (string) $epochs,
        'batch_size'          => (string) $batchSize,
        'dropout_rate'        => leNormalizeDecimalForHash((float) $dropout, 6),
        'learning_rate'       => leNormalizeDecimalForHash((float) $lr, 8),
        'activation_function' => $activationFunctionSaved,
        'hidden_layers'       => (string) $layers,
        'recency_decay'       => leNormalizeDecimalForHash((float) $recencyDecay, 6),
        'model_version'       => $modelVersion,
        'tfjs_version'        => $tfjsVersion,
    ];

    $serverComputedClientHash = hash('sha256', leBuildClientCanonicalString($clientCanonicalPayload));
    if ($clientResultHash === '') {
        $clientResultHash = $serverComputedClientHash;
        $clientHashWasRecovered = true;
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Simple save recovered missing client hash. run_uuid=' . $runUuid);
    } elseif (!hash_equals($serverComputedClientHash, $clientResultHash)) {
        // Keep save simple: do not block inserts because the async browser hash was
        // prepared before final batch fields changed. Token, entitlement, game match,
        // and number-range validation remain the production safety gates.
        $clientResultHash = $serverComputedClientHash;
        $clientHashWasRecovered = true;
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Simple save replaced mismatched client hash with server hash. run_uuid=' . $runUuid);
    }

    $joomlaSecret = '';
    try {
        $joomlaSecret = (string) Factory::getConfig()->get('secret', '');
    } catch (Throwable $secretError) {
        $joomlaSecret = '';
    }
    if ($joomlaSecret === '') {
        $joomlaSecret = 'lottoexpert-client-integrity-v2';
    }

    $serverValidationHash = hash_hmac('sha256', leBuildClientCanonicalString($clientCanonicalPayload) . '|' . $clientResultHash, $joomlaSecret);

    $nextDraw = getNextDrawDate($postedGameId, $db, $tableName);

    if (empty($nextDraw)) {
        // Log the missing next_draw_date but do NOT block the save.
        // A NULL next_draw_date is preferable to a complete save failure;
        // the prediction is still valid and the administrator can backfill
        // the draw date later.
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] next_draw_date not found for game=' . $postedGameId . ' table=' . $tableName . '. Proceeding with NULL.');
        $nextDraw = null;
    }


    $coreAiTarget = leBuildCoreAiPredictionTarget(
        (int) $lottery,
        (string) $gameId,
        $nextDraw,
        (int) ($foundSpec['pickSize'] ?? 0),
        (int) ($foundSpec['extraBallCount'] ?? 0)
    );

    if ($batchUuid === '' && $batchType === 'single_core_ai_run') {
        $batchUuid = $runUuid;
        $batchIndex = 1;
        $batchTotal = 1;
    }

    $columns = [
        'user_id',
        'lottery_id',
        'main_numbers',
        'extra_ball_numbers',
        'source',
        'label',
        'draws_analyzed',
        'generated_at',
        'date_saved',
        'next_draw_date',
        'epochs',
        'batch_size',
        'dropout_rate',
        'learning_rate',
        'activation_function',
        'hidden_layers',
        'recency_decay',
    ];

    $values = [
        (int) $currUser->id,
        (int) $lottery,
        $db->quote($mainNumbers),
        $db->quote($extraNumbers),
        $db->quote($source),
        $db->quote($label),
        (int) $count,
        $db->quote($generatedAt),
        $db->quote(date('Y-m-d H:i:s')),
        $nextDraw !== null ? $db->quote($nextDraw) : 'NULL',
        (int) $epochs,
        (int) $batchSize,
        (float) $dropout,
        (float) $lr,
        $db->quote($activationFunctionSaved),
        (int) $layers,
        (float) $recencyDecay,
    ];

    // Phase 2 optional metadata columns. These are added only if your table already has them,
    // so this upgraded file remains backward-compatible with your current #__user_saved_numbers schema.
    $availableSaveColumns = leGetTableColumns($db, '#__user_saved_numbers');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'run_uuid', $db->quote($runUuid));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_run_uuid', $db->quote($runUuid));
    // Canonical analysis identity. MyLottoExpert uses these fields first, so Core AI
    // can never be confused with SKAI, MCMC, Skip/Hit, Frequency, or Heatmap.
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_method_key', $db->quote('core_ai'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_engine_label', $db->quote('LottoExpert Core AI'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_track_label', $db->quote('Core AI Precision Lock Track'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_source_page', $db->quote('core_ai'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'analysis_schema_version', $db->quote('1'));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'game_id', $db->quote((string) $gameId));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'latest_draw_date', $latestDrawDateForHash ? $db->quote($latestDrawDateForHash) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'mode_key', $db->quote($modeKey));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'model_version', $db->quote($modelVersion));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'tfjs_version', $db->quote($tfjsVersion));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'browser_engine', $db->quote($browserEngine));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'client_result_hash', $db->quote($clientResultHash));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'client_hash', $db->quote($clientResultHash));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'server_validation_hash', $db->quote($serverValidationHash));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'result_hash', $db->quote($serverValidationHash));
    // Core AI learning/evidence metadata for MyLottoExpert. Every insert is optional-column safe.
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'origin_source', $db->quote($originSource));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'save_intent', $db->quote($saveIntent));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'play_status', $db->quote($playStatus));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'model_family', $db->quote($modelFamily));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'risk_profile', $db->quote($riskProfile));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'strategy_profile', $db->quote($strategyProfile));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_type', $db->quote($batchType));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_uuid', $db->quote($batchUuid));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_index', (int) $batchIndex);
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'batch_total', (int) $batchTotal);

    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'settings_json', $settingsJson !== '' ? $db->quote($settingsJson) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'settings', $settingsJson !== '' ? $db->quote($settingsJson) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'ranked_main_numbers_json', $rankedMainJson !== '' ? $db->quote($rankedMainJson) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'ranked_extra_numbers_json', $rankedExtraJson !== '' ? $db->quote($rankedExtraJson) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'regular_main_numbers_json', $rankedMainJson !== '' ? $db->quote($rankedMainJson) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'regular_extra_numbers_json', $rankedExtraJson !== '' ? $db->quote($rankedExtraJson) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'main_display_json', $mainDisplayJson !== '' ? $db->quote($mainDisplayJson) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'extra_display_json', $extraDisplayJson !== '' ? $db->quote($extraDisplayJson) : 'NULL');

    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'prediction_target_id', $db->quote($coreAiTarget['prediction_target_id']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'prediction_target_key', $db->quote($coreAiTarget['prediction_target_key']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'prediction_target_json', $db->quote((string) $coreAiTarget['prediction_target_json']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_game_id', $db->quote($coreAiTarget['target_game_id']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_lottery_id', (int) $coreAiTarget['target_lottery_id']);
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_draw_date', $coreAiTarget['target_draw_date'] !== '' ? $db->quote($coreAiTarget['target_draw_date']) : 'NULL');
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_draw_session', $db->quote($coreAiTarget['target_draw_session']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_timezone_id', $db->quote($coreAiTarget['target_timezone_id']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_prediction_family', $db->quote($coreAiTarget['target_prediction_family']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_prediction_type', $db->quote($coreAiTarget['target_prediction_type']));
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_pick_size', (int) $coreAiTarget['target_pick_size']);
    leAppendColumnIfExists($columns, $values, $availableSaveColumns, 'target_extra_count', (int) $coreAiTarget['target_extra_count']);


    $insertQuery = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
        ->columns($db->quoteName($columns))
        ->values(implode(',', $values));

    try {
        $db->setQuery($insertQuery);
        $db->execute();

        $savedId = 0;
        try {
            $savedId = (int) $db->insertid();
        } catch (Throwable $idError) {
            $savedId = 0;
        }

        if (leIsAjaxRequest()) {
            leJsonResponse(true, 'Number set saved successfully.', [
                'saved_id'               => $savedId,
                'run_uuid'               => $runUuid,
                'client_result_hash'     => $clientResultHash,
                'server_validation_hash' => $serverValidationHash,
                'client_hash_recovered'  => $clientHashWasRecovered ? 1 : 0,
            ]);
        }

        leSuccessSave($app, 'Number set saved successfully.', $savedId);
    } catch (Throwable $e) {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] Save failed: ' . $e->getMessage());
        leFailSave($app, 'We could not save this number set. Please try again.');
    }
}

// The rest of your file (re-initialization, JSON config read, the full HTML/CSS/JS) stays exactly the same.
// Paste the remainder of your original file here without changes.


// ─── TRAINING PARAMETERS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Use training params from spec when available (dailylotteries.json carries them).
// For games from lottery_skip_config.json, derive safe defaults from game type.

// Lookup the Joomla lotteries.lottery_id by game_id for the save handler.
$queryLottery = $db->getQuery(true)
    ->select($db->quoteName('lottery_id'))
    ->from($db->quoteName('#__lotteries'))
    ->where($db->quoteName('game_id') . ' = ' . $db->quote($gameId));
$db->setQuery($queryLottery);
$lottery_id = (int) $db->loadResult();

function getDefaultTrainingByType($pickSz, $rangeM, $extraCount) {
    // Daily Pick 3 / Pick 4 style - safer production baseline.
    if ($pickSz <= 4 && $rangeM <= 10) {
        return [
            'epochs'             => 90,
            'batchSize'          => 8,
            'dropoutRate'        => 0.20,
            'learningRate'       => 0.0003,
            'activationFunction' => 'tanh',
            'hiddenLayers'       => 2,
            'recencyDecay'       => 0.90,
        ];
    }
    // Pick 5, no extra ball - moderate baseline to reduce overfitting.
    if ($pickSz === 5 && $extraCount === 0) {
        return [
            'epochs'             => 170,
            'batchSize'          => 32,
            'dropoutRate'        => 0.22,
            'learningRate'       => 0.0008,
            'activationFunction' => 'relu',
            'hiddenLayers'       => 3,
            'recencyDecay'       => 0.95,
        ];
    }
    // Multi-extra ball (EuroMillions, Lucky Stars, etc.) - slightly heavier but capped.
    if ($extraCount >= 2) {
        return [
            'epochs'             => 250,
            'batchSize'          => 32,
            'dropoutRate'        => 0.22,
            'learningRate'       => 0.0005,
            'activationFunction' => 'relu',
            'hiddenLayers'       => 3,
            'recencyDecay'       => 0.93,
        ];
    }
    // Jackpot-style default (Powerball, Mega Millions, UK Lotto, Irish Lotto, etc.)
    return [
        'epochs'             => 200,
        'batchSize'          => 32,
        'dropoutRate'        => 0.22,
        'learningRate'       => 0.0008,
        'activationFunction' => 'relu',
        'hiddenLayers'       => 3,
        'recencyDecay'       => 0.95,
    ];
}

$typeDefaults = getDefaultTrainingByType(
    (int) $foundSpec['pickSize'],
    (int) $foundSpec['rangeMain'],
    (int) $foundSpec['extraBallCount']
);

// Spec training values (from dailylotteries.json) override type defaults where present.
$specTraining = (isset($foundSpec['training']) && is_array($foundSpec['training']))
    ? $foundSpec['training']
    : [];
$gameConfig = array_merge($typeDefaults, $specTraining);

// Direct assignment from merged config (type defaults are guaranteed present via array_merge above).
$epochs             = $gameConfig['epochs'];
$batchSize          = $gameConfig['batchSize'];
$dropoutRate        = $gameConfig['dropoutRate'];
$learningRate       = $gameConfig['learningRate'];
$activationFunction = $gameConfig['activationFunction'];
$hiddenLayers       = $gameConfig['hiddenLayers'];

// Guard against any non-numeric values that may have come from the spec's training block.
if (!is_numeric($epochs)       || $epochs <= 0)                        { $epochs             = $typeDefaults['epochs']; }
if (!is_numeric($batchSize)    || $batchSize <= 0)                     { $batchSize          = $typeDefaults['batchSize']; }
if (!is_numeric($dropoutRate)  || $dropoutRate < 0 || $dropoutRate > 1){ $dropoutRate        = $typeDefaults['dropoutRate']; }
if (!is_numeric($learningRate) || $learningRate <= 0)                  { $learningRate       = $typeDefaults['learningRate']; }
if (!in_array($activationFunction, ['relu','sigmoid','tanh'], true))   { $activationFunction = $typeDefaults['activationFunction']; }
if (!is_numeric($hiddenLayers) || $hiddenLayers <= 0)                  { $hiddenLayers       = $typeDefaults['hiddenLayers']; }


// Map the JSON fields into our variables
$mainNumbersMax = (int) $foundSpec['rangeMain'];       // e.g. 70
$pickSize       = (int) $foundSpec['pickSize'];        // e.g. 5 or 6
$numExtraBalls  = (int) $foundSpec['extraBallCount'];   // 0, 1, or 2
$hasExtraBall   = $numExtraBalls > 0;
$extraBallMax   = $hasExtraBall
                    ? (int) $foundSpec['rangeExtra']
                    : 0;                               // e.g. 25

// Derive a SKAI game type for presets (Option B - game-aware)
$skaiGameType = 'jackpot'; // default

// Very small-range daily games (e.g. Pick 3 / Pick 4)
if ($pickSize <= 4 && $mainNumbersMax <= 10) {
    $skaiGameType = 'daily';
}
// Classic Pick 5, no bonus ball
elseif ($pickSize === 5 && !$hasExtraBall) {
    $skaiGameType = 'pick5';
}
// Games with 2 or more extra balls (e.g. EuroMillions style)
elseif ($hasExtraBall && $numExtraBalls >= 2) {
    $skaiGameType = 'multiExtra';
}
// Otherwise, treat as jackpot-style (Powerball, Mega Millions, etc.)

// HARD-CODED COLUMN NAMES & SLICING

// We've locked these in for security; we'll only ever use the first $pickSize
// (plus any extra balls) out of this master list:
$allNumberFields = [
  'first','second','third','fourth','fifth','sixth','seventh',
  'eighth','nineth','tenth','eleventh','twelveth','thirtheenth',
  'fourteenth','fifteenth','sixteenth','seventeenth','eighteenth',
  'nineteenth','twentieth','twenty_first','twenty_second'
];

// pick the columns for the main draw:
$mainFieldNames  = array_slice($allNumberFields, 0, $pickSize);

// pick the columns for any extra-ball(s) (will be empty if none):
$extraFieldNames = $hasExtraBall
    ? array_slice($allNumberFields, $pickSize, $numExtraBalls)
    : [];
// end HARD-CODED COLUMN NAMES

// (A) Helper to compute "n choose k"
function combination($n, $k) {
    if ($k > $n) return 0;
    $res = 1;
    for ($i = 1; $i <= $k; $i++) {
        $res = $res * ($n - $i + 1) / $i;
    }
    return round($res);
}

// (B) Total ways to pick $pickSize from $mainNumbersMax
$totalCombinations = combination($mainNumbersMax, $pickSize);

// DYNAMIC BUCKETS BLOCK START

// 1) grab any custom from GET/POST
$custom = isset($_REQUEST['customCount']) ? (int) $_REQUEST['customCount'] : null;

// 2) build the raw list: always include 1 ticket, stock buckets, and custom
$raw = [
  $pickSize,  // "1 ticket"
  10, 15, 20, // stock buckets
  $custom     // optional custom
];

// 3) filter invalid, dedupe & sort
$options = array_values(array_unique(array_filter(
    $raw,
    function($n) use($pickSize, $mainNumbersMax) {
        return is_int($n)
            && $n >= $pickSize
            && $n <= $mainNumbersMax;
    }
)));
sort($options);

// 4) build stats
$stats = [];
foreach ($options as $opt) {
    $ways = combination($opt, $pickSize);
    $odds = $ways ? round($totalCombinations / $ways) : 0;
    $stats[] = [
        'count' => $opt,
        'ways'  => $ways,
        'odds'  => $odds,
        'pct'   => $ways
                   ? round(100 * $ways / $totalCombinations, 2)
                   : 0
    ];
}

// (E) Grab the "best" (last) row for headlines
$best = end($stats);

// DYNAMIC BUCKETS BLOCK END


// Securely connect to the Joomla database

$dbCol = $db->quoteName($db->replacePrefix($foundSpec['tableName']));


$gameIdCol = $db->quoteName('game_id');
$drawDateCol = $db->quoteName('draw_date');

// Prepare the SQL query securely
$query = $db->getQuery(true)
    ->select('*') // Include the game_name field
    ->from($dbCol)
    ->where($gameIdCol . ' = ' . $db->quote($gameId))
    ->order($drawDateCol . ' ASC');

$db->setQuery($query);
$historicalResults = $db->loadObjectList();

// Extract the lottery name from the database or default to 'Lottery' if not found
$lotteryName = isset($historicalResults[0]->game_name) ? $historicalResults[0]->game_name : 'Lottery';

// Count the total number of database entries
$totalEntryCount = count($historicalResults);

// Initialize variables
$draws = [];
$nearestDrawNumbers = [];
$nearestDrawDate = '';

// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Use the actual last draw_date from the DB instead of today
if (!empty($historicalResults)) {
    // $historicalResults is ordered by draw_date ASC
    $lastRow        = end($historicalResults);
    $latestDrawDate = date('Y-m-d', strtotime($lastRow->draw_date));
} else {
    // Fallback if no history present
    $latestDrawDate = date('Y-m-d');
}
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

if (!empty($historicalResults)) {
    foreach ($historicalResults as $lr) {
        // Collect historical draw numbers and date

// build the numbers array dynamically based on our slices
$numbers = [];
// main balls
foreach ($mainFieldNames as $col) {
  $numbers[] = intval($lr->{$col});
}
// extra ball(s)
foreach ($extraFieldNames as $col) {
  $numbers[] = intval($lr->{$col});
}

        $draws[] = [
            'numbers'   => $numbers,
            'draw_date' => $lr->draw_date
        ];
    }

    // Use the latest draw as the input for Analysis
    $latestDrawData      = end($draws);
    $latestResult        = $latestDrawData['numbers'];
    $latestDrawDateFromDB = date('Y-m-d', strtotime($latestDrawData['draw_date']));

    // Find the draw nearest to the selected date
    $rawSelectedDate  = isset($_POST['latestDrawDate']) ? trim((string) $_POST['latestDrawDate']) : '';
    // Validate the POST date: must be YYYY-MM-DD; fall back to the DB-derived date on any failure.
    if ($rawSelectedDate !== '' && preg_match('/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/', $rawSelectedDate)) {
        $selectedDrawDate = $rawSelectedDate;
    } else {
        $selectedDrawDate = $latestDrawDate;
    }
    // Pre-build the target DateTime once outside the loop (selectedDrawDate is already validated).
    try {
        $selectedDt = new DateTime($selectedDrawDate);
    } catch (Exception $dtEx) {
        error_log('[AI-Lotteries] DateTime parse error on selectedDrawDate: ' . $dtEx->getMessage());
        $selectedDt = null;
    }
    $nearestDraw = null;

    if ($selectedDt !== null) {
        foreach ($draws as $draw) {
            try {
                $drawDt = new DateTime($draw['draw_date']);
            } catch (Exception $dtEx) {
                error_log('[AI-Lotteries] DateTime parse error on draw_date ' . $draw['draw_date'] . ': ' . $dtEx->getMessage());
                continue; // skip this malformed row; do not stop the entire loop
            }
            if ($drawDt <= $selectedDt) {
                $nearestDraw = $draw;
            } else {
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    if ($nearestDraw) {
        $nearestDrawNumbers = $nearestDraw['numbers'];
        $nearestDrawDate    = $nearestDraw['draw_date'];
    }
}

?>

  [[div class="le-inline-evolution-note"]]
    [[strong]]Positioning note:[[/strong]] Core AI explains the foundational method clearly. SKAI expands this by learning from saved runs, scored outcomes, and broader strategy behavior over time.
  [[/div]]

  [[div class="skai-analyzes-grid"]]
    [[div class="skai-analyze-item"]]
      [[h3]]Historical Draw Patterns[[/h3]]
      [[p]]Sequential number behavior, interval consistency, and long-term frequency distributions across all recorded draws.[[/p]]
    [[/div]]
    [[div class="skai-analyze-item"]]
      [[h3]]Number Distribution Balance[[/h3]]
      [[p]]Coverage across hot, neutral, and cold number groups relative to their statistical expectation in random draws.[[/p]]
    [[/div]]
    [[div class="skai-analyze-item"]]
      [[h3]]Clustering Behavior[[/h3]]
      [[p]]Co-occurrence relationships between numbers &mdash; identifying which numbers tend to appear together more frequently.[[/p]]
    [[/div]]
    [[div class="skai-analyze-item"]]
      [[h3]]Volatility Cycles[[/h3]]
      [[p]]Recency-weighted trend analysis measuring how draw behavior has shifted over recent cycles compared to historical norms.[[/p]]
    [[/div]]
  [[/div]]
