  [[p id="skaiModeDescription" class="skai-mode-desc"]]
    Balanced mode uses game-specific defaults for <?php echo htmlspecialchars($lotteryName, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8'); ?> &ndash; a steady choice for most sessions.
  [[/p]]

  [[div class="custom-container"]]
    [[details]]
      [[summary]]Training Parameters Explained[[/summary]]
      [[h4 style="margin-top:10px;"]]Epochs[[/h4]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Definition:[[/strong]] An epoch is one complete pass through the entire dataset.[[/p]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Typical Range:[[/strong]] 10 to 1000. Increasing epochs can help the model learn more patterns but may cause overfitting.[[/p]]
      [[h4]]Batch Size[[/h4]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Definition:[[/strong]] How many samples are processed at once before updating the model (8&ndash;256). Larger batches speed training but may miss finer details.[[/p]]
      [[h4]]Dropout Rate[[/h4]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Definition:[[/strong]] Fraction of neurons randomly ignored during training (0.1&ndash;0.5). Higher dropout reduces overfitting.[[/p]]
      [[h4]]Learning Rate[[/h4]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Definition:[[/strong]] Controls how quickly the model adjusts its knowledge (0.0001&ndash;0.1). Higher rates learn faster but can skip important details.[[/p]]
      [[h4]]Activation Function[[/h4]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Definition:[[/strong]] Non-linear function (ReLU, Sigmoid, Tanh) that lets the network capture complex patterns.[[/p]]
      [[h4]]Hidden Layers[[/h4]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Definition:[[/strong]] Layers between input and output. More layers detect more complex patterns (1&ndash;5).[[/p]]
      [[h4]]Recency Decay[[/h4]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Definition:[[/strong]] Controls how much recent draws matter vs older ones. 1.0 = equal weight for all. Lower values emphasize recent draws.[[/p]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Example:[[/strong]] With 0.8 decay, yesterday's draw counts fully, two days ago counts as 0.8, three days ago as 0.64, and so on.[[/p]]
    [[/details]]
  [[/div]]

  [[div class="skai-step-label"]]
    [[span class="skai-step-badge" style="background:var(--skai-slate);"]]OPTIONAL[[/span]]
    [[span class="skai-step-title"]]Fine-tune AI Parameters[[/span]]
    [[span class="skai-step-hint"]]Skip this if you are new.[[/span]]
  [[/div]]

  [[div class="custom-container"]]
    [[details]]
      [[summary]]Advanced Settings[[/summary]]
      [[form id="predictionForm" onsubmit="return false;"]]
        [[div class="parameter-inputs"]]
          [[div class="parameter-item"]]

              [[input type="number" id="epochs" name="epochs" value="<?php echo htmlspecialchars($epochs); ?>" min="1"]]
            [[/label]]
          [[/div]]
          [[div class="parameter-item"]]
            [[label for="batchSize"]]Batch Size[[br]]

            [[/label]]
          [[/div]]
          [[div class="parameter-item"]]
            [[label for="learningRate"]]Learning Rate[[br]]

            [[/label]]
          [[/div]]

            [[label for="activationFunction"]]Activation Function[[br]]
              [[select id="activationFunction" name="activationFunction"]]
                [[option value="relu" <?php echo $activationFunction === 'relu' ? 'selected' : ''; ?>]]ReLU[[/option]]
                [[option value="sigmoid" <?php echo $activationFunction === 'sigmoid' ? 'selected' : ''; ?>]]Sigmoid[[/option]]
                [[option value="tanh" <?php echo $activationFunction === 'tanh' ? 'selected' : ''; ?>]]Tanh[[/option]]
              [[/select]]
            [[/label]]
          [[/div]]
          [[div class="parameter-item"]]
            [[label for="hiddenLayers"]]Hidden Layers[[br]]

                [[span id="recencyDecayLambdaReadout" style="min-width:48px;text-align:right;font-weight:700;color:var(--skai-navy);" aria-live="polite"]]1.00[[/span]]

      [[p]][[strong]]Run Core AI 9-Batch Precision Lock[[/strong]] runs nine separate LottoExpert Core AI focusing runs. It combines three Focus Profiles with three Signal Blend checkpoints, giving you a controlled comparison field for overlap, disagreement, and narrowing opportunities.[[/p]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Why does it take long?[[/strong]] Each run is a complete neural network training pass through all historical draw data. Nine runs in a row takes patience. You can stop any time and save whatever has finished.[[/p]]
      [[p]][[strong]]How does saving work?[[/strong]] After all nine runs complete, click [[strong]]Save All 9[[/strong]]. The page saves each completed run one at a time using one shared batch identity so MyLottoExpert can recognize the full Precision Lock group.[[/p]]
      [[p]][[strong]]Should I click Save while it runs?[[/strong]] No. Let the batch finish first. When the Save All 9 button appears, click it to save the completed runs one at a time.[[/p]]

    [[p class="skai-section-desc"]]Core AI is designed to produce a structured candidate pool, not a guaranteed ticket. For the strongest workflow, run the [[strong]]9-Batch Precision Lock[[/strong]], let all runs finish, then click [[strong]]Save All 9[[/strong]] so MyLottoExpert can track and score the batch after the official draw.[[/p]]

      [[div style="font-size:.76rem;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.08em;text-transform:uppercase;color:#1C66FF;margin-bottom:8px;"]]1. Review overlap[[/div]]

      [[p style="font-size:.9rem;line-height:1.62;color:#4b5563;margin:0;"]]Look for numbers that keep appearing across Balanced, Explorative, and Conservative Focus runs. Repetition across different blend checkpoints is the main Precision Lock signal.[[/p]]
    [[/article]]
    [[article style="border:1px solid rgba(127,141,170,.22);border-radius:16px;padding:18px;background:linear-gradient(180deg,#ffffff 0%,#f8fbff 100%);box-shadow:0 8px 22px rgba(10,26,51,.07);"]]

    [[/article]]
    [[article style="border:1px solid rgba(127,141,170,.22);border-radius:16px;padding:18px;background:linear-gradient(180deg,#ffffff 0%,#f8fbff 100%);box-shadow:0 8px 22px rgba(10,26,51,.07);"]]

        How Core AI ranks numbers
        [[span style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:500;color:var(--skai-slate);white-space:nowrap;"]]Methodology[[/span]]
      [[/summary]]
      [[div style="padding:0 18px 18px;font-size:.9rem;line-height:1.7;color:#374151;"]]
        [[p]]Core AI starts with verified historical draw data, prepares the records into model-ready features, trains a foundational neural model, and ranks candidate numbers by probability signal.[[/p]]
        [[p]]The [[strong]]Signal Blend[[/strong]] slider is one percentage. Lower values lean toward overdue/gap-pressure behavior; higher values lean toward AI-forward ranking. Center keeps the Core AI output balanced.[[/p]]

        [[p]]Playing <?php echo htmlspecialchars($lotteryName, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8'); ?> means picking [[strong]]<?php echo $pickSize; ?>[[/strong]] numbers from [[strong]]<?php echo $mainNumbersMax; ?>[[/strong]]<?php if ($hasExtraBall): ?> and [[strong]]<?php echo $numExtraBalls; ?> extra ball<?php echo $numExtraBalls > 1 ? 's' : ''; ?>[[/strong]] from [[strong]]<?php echo $extraBallMax; ?>[[/strong]]<?php endif; ?>. The base main-number combination count is [[strong]]<?php echo number_format($totalCombinations); ?>[[/strong]].[[/p]]
        [[p]]When Core AI gives you a larger ranked pool, the goal is not to play every possible combination. The goal is to create a better organized candidate field, then use a focused ticket plan or reduced wheel when appropriate.[[/p]]

          [[strong]]Current coverage guide:[[/strong]] <?php echo $best['count']; ?> numbers creates [[strong]]<?php echo number_format($best['ways']); ?> possible <?php echo $pickSize; ?>-number combinations[[/strong]] inside that pool, representing approximately [[strong]]<?php echo $best['pct']; ?>%[[/strong]] of the full main-number combination space.

        Core AI vs. SKAI
        [[span style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:500;color:var(--skai-slate);white-space:nowrap;"]]Product path[[/span]]
      [[/summary]]
      [[div style="padding:0 18px 18px;font-size:.9rem;line-height:1.7;color:#374151;"]]
        [[p]][[strong]]Core AI[[/strong]] is the polished foundational engine. It produces a clear ranked candidate set, supports single focusing runs, and captures structured evidence from the preferred 9-Batch Precision Lock.[[/p]]
        [[p]][[strong]]SKAI[[/strong]] is the advanced adaptive layer. It goes further by studying saved runs, measuring post-draw performance, comparing batches, and adapting future strategy recommendations over time.[[/p]]

[[script]]
function showSignUpPopup() {
  document.getElementById('signupOverlay').style.display = 'block';
  document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
  var close = document.getElementById('signupModalClose');
  var overlay = document.getElementById('signupOverlay');
  if (close) {
    close.addEventListener('click', function () {
      overlay.style.display = 'none';
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
    });
  }
  if (overlay) {
    overlay.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
      if (e.target === overlay) {
        overlay.style.display = 'none';
        document.body.style.overflow = '';
      }
    });
  }
});
[[/script]]

  
<!-- SKAI Phase 2: Client-Side Integrity Hashing -->
[[script]]
(function () {
  "use strict";

  var PAYLOAD_VERSION = "le-client-v2";
  var MODEL_VERSION = "legacy-tfjs-client-v2";

  function byId(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }
  function setVal(id, value) { var el = byId(id); if (el) { el.value = value == null ? "" : String(value); } }
  function getVal(id) { var el = byId(id); return el ? String(el.value || "") : ""; }

  function uuidV4() {
    if (window.crypto && typeof window.crypto.getRandomValues === "function") {
      var bytes = new Uint8Array(16);
      window.crypto.getRandomValues(bytes);
      bytes[6] = (bytes[6] & 0x0f) | 0x40;
      bytes[8] = (bytes[8] & 0x3f) | 0x80;
      var hex = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < 256; i++) { hex[i] = (i + 0x100).toString(16).substr(1); }
      return hex[bytes[0] ] + hex[bytes[1] ] + hex[bytes[2] ] + hex[bytes[3] ] + "-" +
        hex[bytes[4] ] + hex[bytes[5] ] + "-" + hex[bytes[6] ] + hex[bytes[7] ] + "-" +
        hex[bytes[8] ] + hex[bytes[9] ] + "-" + hex[bytes[10] ] + hex[bytes[11] ] + hex[bytes[12] ] + hex[bytes[13] ] + hex[bytes[14] ] + hex[bytes[15] ];
    }

    return "xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx".replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
      var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0;
      var v = c === "x" ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
      return v.toString(16);
    });
  }

  function normalizeDecimal(value, precision) {
    var n = parseFloat(value);
    if (!isFinite(n)) { n = 0; }
    var out = n.toFixed(precision);
    out = out.replace(/0+$/, "").replace(/\.$/, "");
    return out === "" ? "0" : out;
  }

  function canonicalString(payload) {
    var parts = [
      payload.payload_version, payload.run_uuid, payload.game_id, payload.lottery_id,
      payload.main_numbers, payload.extra_ball_numbers, payload.draws_analyzed,
      payload.generated_at, payload.latest_draw_date, payload.mode_key, payload.epochs,
      payload.batch_size, payload.dropout_rate, payload.learning_rate,
      payload.activation_function, payload.hidden_layers, payload.recency_decay,
      payload.model_version, payload.tfjs_version
    ];
    for (var i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
      parts[i] = String(parts[i] == null ? "" : parts[i]).replace(/\|/g, "/");
    }
    return parts.join("|");
  }

  function fallbackHash(str) {
    // Pure JavaScript SHA-256 fallback for older browsers or non-secure contexts.
    function rightRotate(value, amount) {
      return (value >>> amount) | (value << (32 - amount));
    }

    var mathPow = Math.pow;
    var maxWord = mathPow(2, 32);
    var lengthProperty = "length";
    var i, j;
    var result = "";
    var words = [];
    var asciiBitLength = str[lengthProperty] * 8;
    var hash = [];
    var k = [];
    var primeCounter = 0;
    var isComposite = {};

    for (var candidate = 2; primeCounter < 64; candidate++) {
      if (!isComposite[candidate]) {
        for (i = 0; i < 313; i += candidate) {
          isComposite[i] = candidate;
        }
        hash[primeCounter] = (mathPow(candidate, 0.5) * maxWord) | 0;
        k[primeCounter++] = (mathPow(candidate, 1 / 3) * maxWord) | 0;
      }
    }

    str += "\x80";
    while (str[lengthProperty] % 64 - 56) {
      str += "\x00";
    }

    for (i = 0; i < str[lengthProperty]; i++) {
      j = str.charCodeAt(i);
      if (j >> 8) {
        // Canonical payload is ASCII, but guard anyway.
        j = j & 255;
      }
      words[i >> 2] |= j << ((3 - i) % 4) * 8;
    }

    words[words[lengthProperty] ] = ((asciiBitLength / maxWord) | 0);
    words[words[lengthProperty] ] = (asciiBitLength);

    for (j = 0; j < words[lengthProperty];) {
      var w = words.slice(j, j += 16);
      var oldHash = hash.slice(0);

      for (i = 0; i < 64; i++) {
        var w15 = w[i - 15];
        var w2 = w[i - 2];
        var a = hash[0];
        var e = hash[4];
        var temp1 = hash[7]
          + (rightRotate(e, 6) ^ rightRotate(e, 11) ^ rightRotate(e, 25))
          + ((e & hash[5]) ^ ((~e) & hash[6]))
          + k[i]
          + (w[i] = (i < 16) ? w[i] : (
              w[i - 16]
              + (rightRotate(w15, 7) ^ rightRotate(w15, 18) ^ (w15 >>> 3))
              + w[i - 7]
              + (rightRotate(w2, 17) ^ rightRotate(w2, 19) ^ (w2 >>> 10))
            ) | 0);
        var temp2 = (rightRotate(a, 2) ^ rightRotate(a, 13) ^ rightRotate(a, 22))
          + ((a & hash[1]) ^ (a & hash[2]) ^ (hash[1] & hash[2]));

        hash = [(temp1 + temp2) | 0].concat(hash);
        hash[4] = (hash[4] + temp1) | 0;
      }

      for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
        hash[i] = (hash[i] + oldHash[i]) | 0;
      }
    }

    for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
      for (j = 3; j + 1; j--) {
        var b = (hash[i] >> (j * 8)) & 255;
        result += ((b < 16) ? "0" : "") + b.toString(16);
      }
    }

    return result.toLowerCase();
  }

  function sha256Hex(str) {
    if (window.crypto && window.crypto.subtle && window.TextEncoder) {
      return window.crypto.subtle.digest("SHA-256", new TextEncoder().encode(str)).then(function (buf) {
        var bytes = new Uint8Array(buf);
        var hex = "";
        for (var i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) { hex += ("00" + bytes[i].toString(16)).slice(-2); }
        return hex;
      }).catch(function () { return fallbackHash(str); });
    }
    return Promise.resolve(fallbackHash(str));
  }

  function getSelectedMode() {
    if (typeof window.getSelectedSkaiMode === "function") {
      try { return window.getSelectedSkaiMode(); } catch (_) {}
    }
    var btn = document.querySelector('.skai-mode-btn[aria-pressed="true"]');
    return btn && btn.getAttribute("data-skai-mode") ? btn.getAttribute("data-skai-mode") : "balanced";
  }

  function setSaveButtonLocked(locked) {
    var form = byId("savePredictionForm");
    if (!form) { return; }
    var button = form.querySelector("[type=submit]");
    if (!button) { return; }
    button.disabled = !!locked;
    button.setAttribute("aria-busy", locked ? "true" : "false");
    if (locked) {
      if (!button.getAttribute("data-ready-text")) { button.setAttribute("data-ready-text", button.textContent || "Save Core AI Run"); }
      button.textContent = "Preparing secure save...";
    } else {
      button.textContent = button.getAttribute("data-ready-text") || "Save Core AI Run";
    }
  }

  function coreAiActiveDataValue(selector, fallback) {
    try {
      var el = document.querySelector(selector + '[aria-pressed="true"], ' + selector + '.is-active');
      if (el) {
        return el.getAttribute('data-profile') || el.getAttribute('data-strategy') || el.getAttribute('data-skai-mode') || fallback;
      }
    } catch (_) {}
    return fallback;
  }

  function coreAiBuildEvidenceSettings(modeKey) {
    var riskProfile = getVal('saveRiskProfile') || coreAiActiveDataValue('[data-profile]', modeKey || 'balanced');
    var strategyProfile = getVal('saveStrategyProfile') || coreAiActiveDataValue('[data-strategy]', modeKey || 'balanced');
    setVal('saveRiskProfile', riskProfile);
    setVal('saveStrategyProfile', strategyProfile);

    return {
      model_family: 'core_ai',
      analysis_method_key: 'core_ai',
      analysis_engine_label: 'LottoExpert Core AI',
      analysis_track_label: 'Core AI Precision Lock Track',
      analysis_source_page: 'core_ai',
      analysis_schema_version: '1',
      source: 'ai_prediction',
      origin_source: 'core_ai',
      save_intent: 'prediction_archive',
      mode_key: modeKey || 'balanced',
      risk_profile: riskProfile,
      strategy_profile: strategyProfile,
      signal_blend_ai_pct: (typeof window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct === 'function') ? String(window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct()) : '',
      signal_blend_skip_pct: (typeof window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct === 'function') ? String(100 - window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct()) : '',
      signal_blend_label: (typeof window.coreAiBlendLabelFromPct === 'function' && typeof window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct === 'function') ? window.coreAiBlendLabelFromPct(window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct()) : '',
      batch_type: getVal('saveBatchType') || 'single_core_ai_run',
      batch_uuid: getVal('saveBatchUuid') || '',
      batch_index: getVal('saveBatchIndex') || '1',
      batch_total: getVal('saveBatchTotal') || '1',
      epochs: getVal('saveEpochs'),
      batch_size: getVal('saveBatchSize'),
      dropout_rate: getVal('saveDropoutRate'),
      learning_rate: getVal('saveLearningRate'),
      activation_function: getVal('saveActivationFunction'),
      hidden_layers: getVal('saveHiddenLayers'),
      recency_decay: getVal('saveRecencyDecay'),
      draws_analyzed: (function(){ var form = byId('savePredictionForm'); var el = form ? form.querySelector('[name="draws_analyzed"]') : null; return el ? el.value : ''; })(),
      latest_draw_date: getVal('saveLatestDrawDate'),
      model_version: MODEL_VERSION
    };
  }

  function prepareClientIntegrity() {
    var runUuid = getVal("saveRunUuid");
    if (!runUuid) { runUuid = uuidV4(); setVal("saveRunUuid", runUuid); }

    var tfjsVersion = "";
    try { tfjsVersion = window.tf && window.tf.version && window.tf.version.tfjs ? String(window.tf.version.tfjs) : ""; } catch (_) {}

    var browserEngine = "";
    try { browserEngine = navigator.userAgent || ""; } catch (_) {}

    var existingModeKey = getVal("saveModeKey");
    var modeKey = existingModeKey || getSelectedMode();
    var latestDrawDate = getVal("latestDrawDate") || getVal("saveLatestDrawDate");

    setVal("saveModeKey", modeKey);
    setVal("saveModelVersion", MODEL_VERSION);
    setVal("saveTfjsVersion", tfjsVersion);
    setVal("saveBrowserEngine", browserEngine.substr(0, 160));
    setVal("saveLatestDrawDate", latestDrawDate);
    try {
      setVal("saveSettingsJson", JSON.stringify(coreAiBuildEvidenceSettings(modeKey)));
    } catch (_) {}


    var form = byId("savePredictionForm");
    var lotteryId = "";
    var drawsAnalyzed = "";
    if (form) {
      var lotteryInput = form.querySelector('[name="lottery_id"]');
      var drawsInput = form.querySelector('[name="draws_analyzed"]');
      lotteryId = lotteryInput ? String(lotteryInput.value || "") : "";
      drawsAnalyzed = drawsInput ? String(drawsInput.value || "") : "";
    }

    var payload = {
      payload_version: PAYLOAD_VERSION,
      run_uuid: runUuid,
      game_id: getVal("saveGameId"),
      lottery_id: lotteryId,
      main_numbers: getVal("saveMainNumbers"),
      extra_ball_numbers: getVal("saveExtraBallNumbers"),
      draws_analyzed: drawsAnalyzed,
      generated_at: getVal("saveGeneratedAt"),
      latest_draw_date: latestDrawDate,
      mode_key: modeKey,
      epochs: getVal("saveEpochs"),
      batch_size: getVal("saveBatchSize"),
      dropout_rate: normalizeDecimal(getVal("saveDropoutRate"), 6),
      learning_rate: normalizeDecimal(getVal("saveLearningRate"), 8),
      activation_function: getVal("saveActivationFunction"),
      hidden_layers: getVal("saveHiddenLayers"),
      recency_decay: normalizeDecimal(getVal("saveRecencyDecay"), 6),
      model_version: MODEL_VERSION,
      tfjs_version: tfjsVersion
    };

    setSaveButtonLocked(true);

    return sha256Hex(canonicalString(payload)).then(function (hash) {
      setVal("saveClientResultHash", hash);
      setSaveButtonLocked(false);
      try { window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("skai:integrity:ready", { detail: { run_uuid: runUuid, client_result_hash: hash } })); } catch (_) {}
      return hash;
    });
  }

  window.skaiPrepareClientIntegrity = prepareClientIntegrity;
  window.skaiClientIntegrityCanonicalString = canonicalString;
  window.coreAiBuildEvidenceSettings = coreAiBuildEvidenceSettings;
})();

  [[script defer]]
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      // -- ES5 compatibility helpers ----------------------------------
      // Replaces Array.prototype.fill (ES6)
      function skaiArrayFill(n, val) {
        var arr = [];
        for (var _i = 0; _i < n; _i++) { arr.push(val); }
        return arr;
      }
      // Replaces Array.from (ES6) for array-like objects
      function skaiArrayFrom(arrayLike) {
        var arr = [];
        for (var _i = 0; _i < arrayLike.length; _i++) { arr.push(arrayLike[_i]); }
        return arr;
      }
      // Replaces new Set(arr) (ES6) - returns plain object lookup
      function skaiMakeSet(arr) {
        var obj = {};
        for (var _i = 0; _i < arr.length; _i++) { obj[arr[_i] ] = true; }
        return obj;
      }
      // Replaces Set.prototype.has (ES6)
      function skaiSetHas(obj, val) { return obj[val] === true; }
      var SKAI_LT = String.fromCharCode(60);
      var SKAI_GT = String.fromCharCode(62);
      var SKAI_AMP = String.fromCharCode(38);
      var SKAI_MDASH = String.fromCharCode(8212);
      function skaiHtmlTag(name, attrs, closing) {
        if (closing) {
          return SKAI_LT + '/' + name + SKAI_GT;
        }
        return SKAI_LT + name + (attrs ? ' ' + attrs : '') + SKAI_GT;
      }
      function skaiHtmlFullTag(name, attrs, content) {
        return skaiHtmlTag(name, attrs, false) +
          String(content === null || typeof content === 'undefined' ? '' : content) +
          skaiHtmlTag(name, '', true);
      }
      function skaiEscapeHtml(value) {
        return String(value)
          .replace(/&/g, SKAI_AMP + 'amp;')
          .replace(/</g, SKAI_AMP + 'lt;')
          .replace(/>/g, SKAI_AMP + 'gt;')
          .replace(/"/g, SKAI_AMP + 'quot;')
          .replace(/'/g, SKAI_AMP + '#039;');
      }
      function skaiBuildMatchSpan(value) {
        return skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="match"', skaiEscapeHtml(value));
      }
      // -- end ES5 helpers ---------------------------------------------

        function convertSorcererSyntaxToHTML(str) {
  return str.replace(/\[\[/g, SKAI_LT).replace(/\]\]/g, SKAI_GT);
}

// -- UPDATED renderBacktestResults --
function renderBacktestResults(results) {
  function openTag(name, attrs) {
    return skaiHtmlTag(name, attrs, false);
  }

  function closeTag(name) {
    return skaiHtmlTag(name, '', true);
  }

  function fullTag(name, attrs, content) {
    return skaiHtmlFullTag(name, attrs, content);
  }

  var tableHTML =
    openTag('style') +
    '.backtest-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-top:20px;}' +
    '.backtest-table th,.backtest-table td{border:1px solid #ccc;padding:8px;text-align:center;}' +
    '.backtest-table th{background-color:#3498db;color:#fff;}' +
    closeTag('style') +
    openTag('table', 'class="backtest-table"') +
    openTag('thead') + openTag('tr') +
    fullTag('th', '', 'Draw Date') +
    fullTag('th', '', 'Actual Main Numbers') +
    fullTag('th', '', 'Actual Extra Ball(s)') +
    fullTag('th', '', 'Predicted Main Numbers (Top 20)') +
    fullTag('th', '', 'Predicted Extra Ball(s)') +
    fullTag('th', '', 'Main Match Count') +
    fullTag('th', '', 'Extra Match Count') +
    closeTag('tr') + closeTag('thead') +
    openTag('tbody');

  results.forEach(function(r) {
    tableHTML +=
      openTag('tr') +
      fullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(r.date)) +
      fullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(r.actualMain)) +
      fullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(r.actualExtra.length ? r.actualExtra.join(', ') : '-')) +
      fullTag('td', '', r.predictedMain) +
      fullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(r.predictedExtra.length ? r.predictedExtra.join(', ') : '-')) +
      fullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(r.mainMatchCount)) +
      fullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(r.extraMatchCount)) +
      closeTag('tr');
  });

  tableHTML += closeTag('tbody') + closeTag('table');

  // Proper scoring summary (if present)
  if (results && results.skaiSummary) {
    var summary = results.skaiSummary;
    tableHTML +=
      openTag('div', 'style="margin-top:12px; padding:10px; border:1px solid #ccc; border-radius:6px; text-align:left;"') +
      fullTag('div', 'style="font-weight:700; margin-bottom:6px;"', 'LottoExpert AI Backtest Summary') +
      fullTag('div', '', 'Steps: ' + skaiEscapeHtml(summary.steps)) +
      fullTag('div', '', 'Main: Avg Expected Mass (in picks): ' + skaiEscapeHtml(Number(summary.avgExpectedMassMain).toFixed(4))) +
      fullTag('div', '', 'Main: Avg Brier (lower better): ' + skaiEscapeHtml(Number(summary.avgBrierMain).toFixed(6))) +
      fullTag('div', '', 'Main: Avg LogLoss (lower better): ' + skaiEscapeHtml(Number(summary.avgLogLossMain).toFixed(6))) +
      fullTag('div', '', 'Extra: Avg Expected Mass (in picks): ' + skaiEscapeHtml(Number(summary.avgExpectedMassExtra).toFixed(4))) +
      fullTag('div', '', 'Extra: Avg Brier (lower better): ' + skaiEscapeHtml(Number(summary.avgBrierExtra).toFixed(6))) +
      fullTag('div', '', 'Extra: Avg LogLoss (lower better): ' + skaiEscapeHtml(Number(summary.avgLogLossExtra).toFixed(6))) +
      closeTag('div');
  }

  return tableHTML;
}

      // Normalize data function
      function normalizeData(data) {
        return data.map(function(arr) {
          return arr.map(function(num, index) {

      var skaiBlendReadoutEl = document.getElementById('skaiBlendReadout');

      function skaiFmt2(n) {
        var x = parseFloat(n);
        if (!isFinite(x)) { x = 0; }
        return x.toFixed(2);
      }

      function skaiClamp01(x) {
        var n = parseFloat(x);
        if (!isFinite(n)) { n = 0; }
        return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, n));
      }

      function skaiUpdateBlendReadout(modeKey, lambda, beta, tempT) {
        if (typeof coreAiUpdateSignalBlendReadout === 'function') {
          coreAiUpdateSignalBlendReadout();
          return;
        }
        if (!skaiBlendReadoutEl) { return; }
        var lam = skaiClamp01(lambda);
        var skip = 1 - lam;
        skaiBlendReadoutEl.textContent =
          'Blend: ' + Math.round(lam * 100) + '%';
      }

      function formatLambda(val) {
        var n = parseFloat(val);
        if (isNaN(n)) { n = 1.0; }
        n = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, n));
        return n.toFixed(2);
      }

      function syncLambdaReadout() {
        if (!recencyDecayInput || !recencyDecayLambdaReadout) {
          return;
        }
        recencyDecayLambdaReadout.textContent = formatLambda(recencyDecayInput.value);
      }

      // Initialize and keep in sync while editing
      if (recencyDecayInput) {
        recencyDecayInput.addEventListener('input', syncLambdaReadout);
        recencyDecayInput.addEventListener('change', syncLambdaReadout);
      }
      syncLambdaReadout();

      // Guard so a missing checkbox can't break the whole script (and kill the progress bar)

  // ---- SKAI Mode Presets (Option B - game-aware) ----
  var skaiGameType = <?php echo json_encode((string) $skaiGameType, JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE | JSON_HEX_TAG | JSON_HEX_APOS | JSON_HEX_QUOT | JSON_HEX_AMP); ?>; // jackpot, pick5, daily, multiExtra

  // Capture base values from JSON config as "Balanced" anchors
  function safeNumber(val, fallback) {
    var n = parseFloat(val);
    return isNaN(n) ? fallback : n;
  }

  var baseEpochs      = safeNumber(epochsInput && epochsInput.value,      200);
  var baseBatch       = safeNumber(batchSizeInput && batchSizeInput.value,32);
  var baseDropout     = safeNumber(dropoutRateInput && dropoutRateInput.value,0.2);
  var baseLR          = safeNumber(learningRateInput && learningRateInput.value,0.001);
  var baseLayers      = safeNumber(hiddenLayersInput && hiddenLayersInput.value,2);

  function clamp(val, min, max) {
    return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, val));
  }

  function buildPresetsForGameType(gameType) {
    var presets = {};

    function preset(epochs, batch, dropout, lr, recency, layers) {
      return {
        epochs:  epochs,
        batch:   batch,
        dropout: dropout,
        lr:      lr,
        recency: recency,
        layers:  layers
      };
    }

    if (gameType === 'daily') {
      // Pick 3 / Pick 4 / Big 3 style games.
      // Fast enough to run repeatedly, but not so hot that it chases short-term noise.
      presets.balanced     = preset(90,  8, 0.20, 0.00030, 0.90, 2);
      presets.explorative  = preset(130, 8, 0.15, 0.00040, 0.80, 3);
      presets.conservative = preset(60,  8, 0.28, 0.00020, 0.98, 2);
    } else if (gameType === 'pick5') {
      // Regular Pick 5 games without an extra ball.
      presets.balanced     = preset(170, 32, 0.22, 0.00080, 0.95, 3);
      presets.explorative  = preset(230, 32, 0.18, 0.00100, 0.90, 4);
      presets.conservative = preset(120, 32, 0.28, 0.00060, 0.98, 3);
    } else if (gameType === 'multiExtra') {
      // EuroMillions-style games with two or more extra balls.
      presets.balanced     = preset(250, 32, 0.22, 0.00050, 0.93, 3);
      presets.explorative  = preset(340, 32, 0.18, 0.00070, 0.88, 4);
      presets.conservative = preset(180, 32, 0.28, 0.00035, 0.97, 3);
    } else {
      // Jackpot / regular lottery default: Powerball, Mega Millions, Pick 6, UK Lotto, etc.
      presets.balanced     = preset(200, 32, 0.22, 0.00080, 0.95, 3);
      presets.explorative  = preset(260, 32, 0.18, 0.00100, 0.90, 4);
      presets.conservative = preset(140, 32, 0.28, 0.00060, 0.98, 3);
    }

    return presets;
  }

  }
  return 'Balanced Focus uses steady, game-tuned settings and is the preferred starting point for most Core AI focusing runs.';
}

    if (typeof coreAiUpdateSignalBlendReadout === 'function') { coreAiUpdateSignalBlendReadout(); }

  }

// Utility: build a tensor of recency-decay weights
function buildSampleWeightTensor(numSamples, decay) {
  var weights = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < numSamples; i++) {
    weights.push(Math.pow(decay, (numSamples - 1) - i));
  }
  return tf.tensor1d(weights);
}

// Global skip influence factor (0.0-1.0).
// Higher values make Skip & Hit bias stronger in the final probabilities.
// You can tweak this later (e.g., 0.2 = softer, 0.5 = stronger).
var SKIP_ALPHA = 0.3;

function coreAiClampInt(value, min, max, fallback) {
  var n = parseInt(value, 10);
  if (isNaN(n)) { n = fallback; }
  if (n < min) { n = min; }
  if (n > max) { n = max; }
  return n;
}

function coreAiBlendLabelFromPct(aiPct) {
  aiPct = coreAiClampInt(aiPct, 0, 100, 50);
  if (aiPct <= 35) { return 'Skip-Pattern Heavy'; }
  if (aiPct >= 65) { return 'AI-Forward'; }
  return 'Balanced Mix';
}

function coreAiBlendModeFromPct(aiPct) {
  aiPct = coreAiClampInt(aiPct, 0, 100, 50);
  if (aiPct <= 35) { return 'skip-dominant'; }
  if (aiPct >= 65) { return 'ai-forward'; }
  return 'mixed';
}

function coreAiGetSignalBlendPct() {
  var slider = document.getElementById('coreAiBlendSlider');
  return slider ? coreAiClampInt(slider.value, 0, 100, 50) : 50;
}

function coreAiGetFocusProfile() {
  var btn = document.querySelector('.skai-mode-btn[aria-pressed="true"]');
  return btn && btn.getAttribute('data-skai-mode') ? btn.getAttribute('data-skai-mode') : 'balanced';
}

function coreAiFocusLabel(profile) {
  if (profile === 'explorative') { return 'Explorative Focus'; }
  if (profile === 'conservative') { return 'Conservative Focus'; }
  return 'Balanced Focus';
}

function coreAiBlendStrategyKey(aiPct) {
  aiPct = coreAiClampInt(aiPct, 0, 100, 50);
  return 'blend_' + aiPct;
}

function coreAiBlendDirectionFromPct(aiPct) {
  aiPct = coreAiClampInt(aiPct, 0, 100, 50);
  if (aiPct <= 35) { return 'Skip-Pattern Side'; }
  if (aiPct >= 65) { return 'AI-Forward Side'; }
  return 'Centered';
}

function coreAiUpdateSignalBlendReadout() {
  var blendPct = coreAiGetSignalBlendPct();
  var profile = coreAiGetFocusProfile();
  var label = coreAiBlendLabelFromPct(blendPct);
  var direction = coreAiBlendDirectionFromPct(blendPct);
  var badge = document.getElementById('coreAiBlendBadge');
  var directionEl = document.getElementById('coreAiSkipPct');
  var blendEl = document.getElementById('coreAiAiPct');
  var cls = document.getElementById('coreAiBlendClass');
  var readout = document.getElementById('skaiBlendReadout');
  if (badge) { badge.textContent = label; }
  if (directionEl) { directionEl.textContent = direction; }
  if (blendEl) { blendEl.textContent = blendPct + '%'; }
  if (cls) { cls.textContent = label; }
  if (readout) {
    readout.textContent = 'Focus: ' + coreAiFocusLabel(profile) + ' • Blend: ' + blendPct + '% • Type: ' + label;
  }
  var riskField = document.getElementById('saveRiskProfile');
  var strategyField = document.getElementById('saveStrategyProfile');
  var modeField = document.getElementById('saveModeKey');
  if (riskField) { riskField.value = profile; }
  if (strategyField) { strategyField.value = coreAiBlendStrategyKey(blendPct); }
  if (modeField) { modeField.value = coreAiBlendModeFromPct(blendPct); }
}
