// --- SKAI probabilistic blending helpers (math-correct ensemble) ---
// NOTE: SKIP_ALPHA remains for backwards-compatibility, but SKAI now uses a coherent expert blend.
var SKAI_EPS               = 1e-9;
var SKAI_SKIP_BETA_DEFAULT = 2.0;  // controls how strongly skipScores separate numbers (hoist-safe)
var SKAI_BLEND_DEFAULT     = 0.65; // Balanced-mode default AI weight λ (hoist-safe)

function getSelectedSkaiMode() {
  var pct = (typeof window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct === 'function') ? window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct() : 50;
  return coreAiBlendModeFromPct(pct);
}

// Mode → λ (AI weight). Higher λ = more AI-forward.
function getSkaiBlendLambda(modeKey) {
  if (typeof window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct === 'function') {
    return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct() / 100));
  }
  if (modeKey === 'ai-forward')     { return 0.75; }
  if (modeKey === 'skip-dominant')  { return 0.25; }
  return SKAI_BLEND_DEFAULT;
}

// Jensen-Shannon divergence for two discrete distributions (bounded, symmetric, stable).
function skaiJSDivergence(p, q) {
  var n = Math.min(p.length, q.length);
  var js = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) {
    var pi = Math.max(SKAI_EPS, p[i]);
    var qi = Math.max(SKAI_EPS, q[i]);
    var mi = 0.5 * (pi + qi);
    js += 0.5 * (pi * Math.log(pi / mi) + qi * Math.log(qi / mi));
  }
  // Natural log units; bounded in [0, ln(2)]
  return js;
}

// Mixed mode: λ adapts to how much AI and Skip agree.
// - If they agree (low JSD), lean AI-forward more.
// - If they disagree (high JSD), pull λ toward 0.5 to avoid over-committing.
function skaiAdaptiveLambdaMixed(aiNorm, skipProb) {
  var js = skaiJSDivergence(aiNorm, skipProb);
  var jsMax = Math.log(2); // theoretical maximum
  var agree = 1 - Math.min(1, js / jsMax); // 1=agree, 0=disagree

  // Map agreement into a safe λ band for Mixed:
  // - High agreement → λ up to ~0.80
  // - Low agreement  → λ down to ~0.50
  var lambda = 0.50 + (0.30 * agree);

  // Clamp defensively
  return Math.max(0.35, Math.min(0.90, lambda));
}

// Unified λ getter: fixed for other modes; adaptive for Mixed.
function getSkaiLambda(modeKey, aiNorm, skipProb) {
  var lam = getSkaiBlendLambda(modeKey);
  return (typeof lam === 'number' && isFinite(lam)) ? Math.max(0, Math.min(1, lam)) : SKAI_BLEND_DEFAULT;
}

// Mode-aware skip separation (beta). Higher beta makes Skip expert "sharper".
function getSkaiSkipBeta(modeKey) {
  var aiPct = (typeof window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct === 'function') ? window.coreAiGetSignalBlendPct() : 50;
  var skipShare = (100 - aiPct) / 100;
  return Math.max(1.4, Math.min(3.2, 1.4 + (skipShare * 1.8)));
}

// Temperature for exploration sampling (τ >= 1). τ=1 means no flattening.
function getSkaiExploreTau(modeKey) {
  if (modeKey === 'explorative') { return 1.8; }
  if (modeKey === 'mixed')       { return 1.4; }
  return 1.0;
}

// How many picks should be "explore sampled" instead of strict top-k.
// All modes get at least 1 explore pick to prevent identical outputs across batch runs.
function getSkaiExploreCount(modeKey, pickSize) {
  if (modeKey === 'explorative')   { return Math.max(1, Math.floor(pickSize * 0.40)); }
  if (modeKey === 'mixed')         { return Math.max(1, Math.floor(pickSize * 0.30)); }
  if (modeKey === 'skip-dominant') { return Math.max(1, Math.floor(pickSize * 0.20)); }
  // All other modes (ai-forward, balanced, conservative): 1 exploration pick minimum
  return 1;
}

// Build a tempered mass (flattened) for sampling: p^(1/τ), normalized.
function skaiTemperedMass(probMass, tau) {
  if (!tau || tau <= 1) {
    return normalizePositive(probMass);
  }
  var raw = new Array(probMass.length);
  var inv = 1 / tau;
  for (var i = 0; i < probMass.length; i++) {
    raw[i] = Math.pow(Math.max(SKAI_EPS, probMass[i]), inv);
  }
  return normalizePositive(raw);
}

// Weighted sampling without replacement from a probability mass.
function skaiSampleWithoutReplacement(probMass, count) {
  var picks = [];
  var available = probMass.slice(0);

  for (var k = 0; k < count; k++) {
    // Build CDF
    var sum = 0;
    for (var i = 0; i < available.length; i++) {
      sum += Math.max(0, available[i]);
    }
    if (sum <= 0) {
      break;
    }

    var r = Math.random() * sum;
    var chosen = -1;
    for (var i = 0; i < available.length; i++) {
      r -= Math.max(0, available[i]);
      if (r <= 0) { chosen = i; break; }
    }
    if (chosen < 0) { break; }

    picks.push(chosen);
    available[chosen] = 0; // remove
  }

  return picks;
}

// Select final picks: exploit top-(pickSize-exploreCount), explore sample the rest.
function skaiSelectPicksFromMass(probMass, pickSize, modeKey) {
  var exploreCount = getSkaiExploreCount(modeKey, pickSize);
  var tau = getSkaiExploreTau(modeKey);

  var indices = [];
  // Exploit indices by sorting
  var ranked = probMass.map(function(p, i) { return { i: i, p: p }; }).sort(function(a, b) { return b.p - a.p; });

  var exploitCount = Math.max(0, pickSize - exploreCount);
  for (var k = 0; k < exploitCount && k < ranked.length; k++) {
    indices.push(ranked[k].i);
  }

  if (exploreCount > 0) {
    // Build remaining mass excluding already-picked exploit indices
    var remaining = probMass.slice(0);
    for (var k = 0; k < indices.length; k++) {
      remaining[indices[k] ] = 0;
    }

    var tempered = skaiTemperedMass(remaining, tau);
    var sampled = skaiSampleWithoutReplacement(tempered, exploreCount);
    for (var k = 0; k < sampled.length; k++) {
      indices.push(sampled[k]);
    }
  }

  // Return sorted numeric values (1-based numbers) for stable display (dedup defensive)
  var seen = {};
  var uniq = [];
  for (var m = 0; m < indices.length; m++) {
    var idx = indices[m] + 1;
    if (!seen[idx]) { seen[idx] = true; uniq.push(idx); }
  }
  return uniq.sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; });
}

// Normalize a positive vector into sum-to-1 mass (with epsilon floor).
function normalizePositive(arr) {
  var sum = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
    var v = (typeof arr[i] === 'number' && isFinite(arr[i])) ? Math.max(SKAI_EPS, arr[i]) : SKAI_EPS;
    sum += v;
  }
  var out = new Array(arr.length);
  var denom = (sum > 0) ? sum : (arr.length * SKAI_EPS);
  for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
    var v = (typeof arr[i] === 'number' && isFinite(arr[i])) ? Math.max(SKAI_EPS, arr[i]) : SKAI_EPS;
    out[i] = v / denom;
  }
  return out;
}

// Turn skipScores (0..1) into a proper expert distribution using a softmax-like transform.
function buildSkipExpertProbs(skipScores, beta) {
  var raw = new Array(skipScores.length);
  for (var i = 0; i < skipScores.length; i++) {
    var u = (typeof skipScores[i] === 'number' && isFinite(skipScores[i])) ? skipScores[i] : 0;
    // center at 0.5 to reduce runaway bias; beta controls separation
    raw[i] = Math.exp(beta * (u - 0.5));
  }
  return normalizePositive(raw);
}

// Log-opinion pool (geometric mixture): p ∝ ai^λ * skip^(1-λ)
function logOpinionPool(aiProbs, skipProbs, lambda) {
  var out = new Array(aiProbs.length);
  for (var i = 0; i < aiProbs.length; i++) {
    var a = Math.max(SKAI_EPS, aiProbs[i]);
    var s = Math.max(SKAI_EPS, skipProbs[i]);
    out[i] = Math.exp(lambda * Math.log(a) + (1 - lambda) * Math.log(s));
  }
  return normalizePositive(out);
}
 // --- END SKAI probabilistic blending helpers ---

// --- SKAI backtest proper scoring rules (math-correct evaluation) ---
function skaiClipProb(p) {
  if (typeof p !== 'number' || !isFinite(p)) { return SKAI_EPS; }
  return Math.min(1 - SKAI_EPS, Math.max(SKAI_EPS, p));
}

function skaiBrierScore(probMass, actualSet, maxVal) {
  // probMass: array length maxVal, sum-to-1
  // actualSet: Set of winning numbers in 1..maxVal
  var sum = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < maxVal; i++) {
    var p = skaiClipProb(probMass[i]);
    var y = skaiSetHas(actualSet, i + 1) ? 1 : 0;
    var d = p - y;
    sum += d * d;
  }
  return sum / maxVal;
}

function skaiLogLoss(probMass, actualSet, maxVal) {
  // Strictly proper for Bernoulli marginals; clipped to avoid -Inf
  var sum = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < maxVal; i++) {
    var p = skaiClipProb(probMass[i]);
    var y = skaiSetHas(actualSet, i + 1) ? 1 : 0;
    sum += y ? -Math.log(p) : -Math.log(1 - p);
  }
  return sum / maxVal;
}

function skaiExpectedMassInPicks(probMass, picks) {
  // picks: array of numbers (1..max)
  var s = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < picks.length; i++) {
    var idx = picks[i] - 1;
    if (idx >= 0 && idx < probMass.length) {
      s += skaiClipProb(probMass[idx]);
    }
  }
  return s;
}
// --- END SKAI backtest proper scoring rules ---
// Compute per-draw Skip feature vectors for a chronological series of draws.
// drawsNumbers: [ [n1, n2, ...], ... ] in OLDEST → NEWEST order.
// For each draw t, we compute skipVec[t][k] = draws since number (k+1) last appeared BEFORE draw t.
function computeSkipFeatureSeries(drawsNumbers, pickSize, mainNumbersMax) {
  var lastHitIndex   = skaiArrayFill(mainNumbersMax, null);
  var skipsPerStep   = [];

  for (var t = 0; t < drawsNumbers.length; t++) {
    var skipVec = skaiArrayFill(mainNumbersMax, 0);

    // For each number, how long since last seen?
    for (var k = 0; k < mainNumbersMax; k++) {
      var last = lastHitIndex[k];
      // If we've never seen it, treat skip as t (all previous draws missed it).
      var skip = (last === null) ? t : (t - last - 1);
      skipVec[k] = skip;
    }

    // Now update lastHitIndex using the CURRENT draw's main numbers.
    var draw = drawsNumbers[t];
    for (var j = 0; j < pickSize; j++) {
      var n = draw[j];
      if (n >= 1 && n <= mainNumbersMax) {
        lastHitIndex[n - 1] = t;
      }
    }

    skipsPerStep.push(skipVec);
  }

  // Normalize skips to 0..1 so they play nicely with normalized inputs.
  var maxSkip = 0;
  for (var t = 0; t < skipsPerStep.length; t++) {
    var vec = skipsPerStep[t];
    for (var i = 0; i < vec.length; i++) {
      if (vec[i] > maxSkip) {
        maxSkip = vec[i];
      }
    }
  }

  if (maxSkip > 0) {
    for (var t = 0; t < skipsPerStep.length; t++) {
      var vec = skipsPerStep[t];
      for (var i = 0; i < vec.length; i++) {
        vec[i] = vec[i] / maxSkip;
      }
    }
  }

  return skipsPerStep;
}

// Compute per-number Skip scores (0..1) from a DESC list of draws (most recent first).
// This is a thin wrapper around computeSkipFeatureSeries so older code that calls
// computeSkipScores(...) continues to work.
function computeSkipScores(drawsDesc, pickSize, mainNumbersMax) {
  // Convert DESC draws into ASC array of numbers for computeSkipFeatureSeries.
  var drawsAscNumbers = drawsDesc.slice().reverse().map(function(d) { return d.numbers; });
  if (!drawsAscNumbers.length) {
    return skaiArrayFill(mainNumbersMax, 0);
  }

  var skipSeries = computeSkipFeatureSeries(drawsAscNumbers, pickSize, mainNumbersMax);
  var latestVec  = skipSeries[skipSeries.length - 1] || [];
  var result     = skaiArrayFill(mainNumbersMax, 0);

  for (var i = 0; i < mainNumbersMax; i++) {
    result[i] = (typeof latestVec[i] === 'number') ? latestVec[i] : 0;
  }

  return result;
}

function trainModelForBacktest(trainingDraws, settings, onEpochEndCallback) {
  var pickSize       = settings.PICK_SIZE;
  var mainNumbersMax = settings.MAIN_MAX;
  var extraBallMax   = settings.EXTRA_MAX;
  var hasExtraBall   = settings.HAS_EXTRA;

  // 1) normalize inputs
  var drawsNumbers = trainingDraws.map(function(d) { return d.numbers; });
  var normalized   = drawsNumbers.map(function(arr) {
    return arr.map(function(n, i) {
      return i < pickSize
        ? n / mainNumbersMax
        : (hasExtraBall ? n / extraBallMax : n);
    });
  });

  // 1b) compute Skip feature series (per draw, per main number)
  var skipFeatureSeries = computeSkipFeatureSeries(drawsNumbers, pickSize, mainNumbersMax);

  // 2) build X and Y arrays
  var xs = [], ys_main = [], ys_extra = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < normalized.length - 1; i++) {
    var baseInput    = normalized[i];
    var skipFeatures = skipFeatureSeries[i];
    var inputVec     = baseInput.concat(skipFeatures);
    xs.push(inputVec);

    var nextNums = drawsNumbers[i + 1];

    // Y for main
    var mainVec = skaiArrayFill(mainNumbersMax, 0);
    nextNums.slice(0, pickSize).forEach(function(n) { mainVec[n - 1] = 1; });
    ys_main.push(mainVec);

    // Y for extra (supports 1 or more extra balls)
    if (hasExtraBall) {
      var extraVec = skaiArrayFill(extraBallMax, 0);
      var _numExtra = settings.EXTRA_COUNT || 1;
      for (var _eb2 = 0; _eb2 < _numExtra; _eb2++) {
        var _en = nextNums[pickSize + _eb2];
        if (_en >= 1 && _en <= extraBallMax) {
          extraVec[_en - 1] = 1;
        }
      }
      ys_extra.push(extraVec);
    }
  }

  // 3) create tensors
  var xsTensor     = tf.tensor2d(xs);
  var ysMainTensor = tf.tensor2d(ys_main);
  var ysExtraTensor;
  if (hasExtraBall) {
    ysExtraTensor = tf.tensor2d(ys_extra);
  }

  // 4) recency-decay weights
  var sampleWeightTensor = buildSampleWeightTensor(xs.length, settings.RECENCY_DECAY);

  // 5) build the model
  var input = tf.input({ shape: [xs[0].length] });
  var x = tf.layers.dense({ units: 128, activation: settings.ACTIVATION_FUNCTION }).apply(input);
  x = tf.layers.dropout({ rate: settings.DROPOUT_RATE }).apply(x);
  for (var i = 0; i < settings.HIDDEN_LAYERS; i++) {
    x = tf.layers.dense({ units: 64, activation: settings.ACTIVATION_FUNCTION }).apply(x);
    x = tf.layers.dropout({ rate: settings.DROPOUT_RATE }).apply(x);
  }
  var mainOut = tf.layers.dense({
    units: settings.MAIN_MAX,
    activation: 'sigmoid',
    name: 'main_numbers_output'
  }).apply(x);

  var model, outputs;
  if (hasExtraBall) {
    var extraOut = tf.layers.dense({
      units: settings.EXTRA_MAX,
      activation: 'sigmoid',
      name: 'extra_output'
    }).apply(x);
    outputs = [mainOut, extraOut];
    model = tf.model({ inputs: input, outputs: outputs });
  } else {
    outputs = mainOut;
    model = tf.model({ inputs: input, outputs: outputs });
  }

  // 6) compile
  var optimizer = tf.train.adam(settings.LEARNING_RATE);
  var loss      = hasExtraBall
    ? ['binaryCrossentropy','binaryCrossentropy']
    : 'binaryCrossentropy';
  model.compile({ optimizer: optimizer, loss: loss, metrics: ['accuracy'] });

  // 7) prepare yTrain (no sampleWeight support in this tfjs build)
  var yTrain;
  if (hasExtraBall) {
    yTrain = {
      main_numbers_output: ysMainTensor,
      extra_output: ysExtraTensor
    };
  } else {
    yTrain = ysMainTensor;
  }

  // 8) fit model (recency-weighted)
  // sampleWeightTensor is a per-sample exponential decay weight (newest samples weigh more).
  var fitArgs = {
    epochs:          settings.EPOCHS,
    batchSize:       settings.BATCH_SIZE,
    shuffle:         false,
    validationSplit: 0.2,
    callbacks:       { onEpochEnd: onEpochEndCallback }
  };

          // PATCH: sampleWeight not supported in this TFJS build; disable to avoid runtime error.
          // Recency is still used in backtesting via SKAI blend + skip features; full per-sample weighting requires a TFJS build that supports sampleWeight.
          // fitArgs.sampleWeight = hasExtraBall
          //   ? [sampleWeightTensor, sampleWeightTensor]
          //   : sampleWeightTensor;

  return model.fit(xsTensor, yTrain, fitArgs).then(function() {
    // Dispose training tensors after fit; the trained model is returned for prediction.
    try {
      if (xsTensor && typeof xsTensor.dispose === "function") { xsTensor.dispose(); }
      if (ysMainTensor && typeof ysMainTensor.dispose === "function") { ysMainTensor.dispose(); }
      if (ysExtraTensor && typeof ysExtraTensor.dispose === "function") { ysExtraTensor.dispose(); }
      if (sampleWeightTensor && typeof sampleWeightTensor.dispose === "function") { sampleWeightTensor.dispose(); }
    } catch (btTrainCleanupError) {
      console.warn("Backtest training tensor cleanup warning:", btTrainCleanupError);
    }
    return model;
  });
}


function runBacktesting(sortedDrawsAsc, settings) {
  return new Promise(function(resolveAll, rejectAll) {
  var results      = [];
  var N            = sortedDrawsAsc.length;

  // Proper scoring aggregates (lower is better for Brier/LogLoss)
  var totalBrierMain = 0;
  var totalLogLossMain = 0;
  var totalExpectedMassInPicksMain = 0;

  var totalBrierExtra = 0;
  var totalLogLossExtra = 0;
  var totalExpectedMassInPicksExtra = 0;
  var numBacktests = parseInt(document.getElementById('numDrawsBacktest').value) || 3;
  var backtestIndices = [];
  for (var i = N - numBacktests; i < N; i++) { if (i >= 1) { backtestIndices.push(i); } }

  // progress tracking
  var totalSteps = backtestIndices.length * settings.EPOCHS;
  var completed    = 0;
  function updateBacktestProgress() {
    completed++;
    var pct = Math.round((completed/totalSteps)*100);
    backtestProgressBar.style.width   = pct + '%';
    backtestProgressBar.textContent   = pct + '%';
    progressMessage.innerText         = 'System Status: Backtesting in progress... (' + pct + '%)';
  }

  // ES5-safe recursive Promise chain replaces async for loop
  function processBacktestStep(bi) {
    if (bi >= backtestIndices.length) {
      // All steps done - build summary and resolve
      var steps = results.length || 1;
      results.skaiSummary = {
        steps: steps,
        avgBrierMain: (totalBrierMain / steps),
        avgLogLossMain: (totalLogLossMain / steps),
        avgExpectedMassMain: (totalExpectedMassInPicksMain / steps),
        avgBrierExtra: (steps > 0 ? (totalBrierExtra / steps) : 0),
        avgLogLossExtra: (steps > 0 ? (totalLogLossExtra / steps) : 0),
        avgExpectedMassExtra: (steps > 0 ? (totalExpectedMassInPicksExtra / steps) : 0)
      };
      resolveAll(results);
      return;
    }

    var idx = backtestIndices[bi];
    var nums       = sortedDrawsAsc[idx].numbers;
    var actualMain = nums.slice(0, settings.PICK_SIZE);
    var actualExtra= settings.HAS_EXTRA
      ? nums.slice(settings.PICK_SIZE, settings.PICK_SIZE + settings.EXTRA_COUNT)
      : [];

    // train & predict
    var trainingDraws = sortedDrawsAsc.slice(0, idx);
    trainModelForBacktest(trainingDraws, settings, updateBacktestProgress).then(function(model) {

    // prepare last input (normalized numbers + Skip features)
    var drawsNumbersForBT   = trainingDraws.map(function(d) { return d.numbers; });
    var skipFeatureSeriesBT = computeSkipFeatureSeries(drawsNumbersForBT, settings.PICK_SIZE, settings.MAIN_MAX);
    var lastIndex           = trainingDraws.length - 1;

    var lastBaseNorm = drawsNumbersForBT[lastIndex].map(function(v,i) {
      return i < settings.PICK_SIZE
        ? v / settings.MAIN_MAX
        : (settings.HAS_EXTRA ? v / settings.EXTRA_MAX : v);
    });
    var lastSkipFeatures = skipFeatureSeriesBT[lastIndex];
    var lastInputVec     = lastBaseNorm.concat(lastSkipFeatures);

    var pred = model.predict(tf.tensor2d([ lastInputVec ]));

    var mainArr  = settings.HAS_EXTRA ? pred[0].dataSync() : pred.dataSync();
    var extraArr = settings.HAS_EXTRA ? pred[1].dataSync() : [];

    // Compute Skip scores for this specific backtest window.
    // trainingDraws is ASC (oldest to newest), so we reverse to get DESC for computeSkipScores().
    var skipScoresForBacktest = computeSkipScores(
      trainingDraws.slice().reverse(),
      settings.PICK_SIZE,
      settings.MAIN_MAX
    );

    // Build full blended mass for proper scoring (main)
    var actualMainSet = skaiMakeSet(actualMain);

    var aiRawMain = skaiArrayFrom(mainArr).map(function(v) {
      var p = (typeof v === 'number' && isFinite(v)) ? v : 0;
      return Math.min(1 - SKAI_EPS, Math.max(SKAI_EPS, p));
    });
    var aiNormMain = normalizePositive(aiRawMain);

    var skipArrMain = Array.isArray(skipScoresForBacktest)
      ? skipScoresForBacktest
      : skaiArrayFill(aiNormMain.length, 0);

    // Mode-aware skip expert + adaptive Mixed lambda (agreement-based)
    var modeKeyBT = getSelectedSkaiMode();

    var skipBetaBT = getSkaiSkipBeta(modeKeyBT);
    var skipProbMain = buildSkipExpertProbs(skipArrMain, skipBetaBT);

    var lambdaBT = getSkaiLambda(modeKeyBT, aiNormMain, skipProbMain);

    // PATCH 7B-3B: backtest readout (shows the lambda being used for this run)
    var tBT = (typeof skaiGetStoredTemp === 'function') ? skaiGetStoredTemp(modeKeyBT) : 1.0;
    skaiUpdateBlendReadout(modeKeyBT, lambdaBT, skipBetaBT, tBT);

    var probMassMainNorm = logOpinionPool(aiNormMain, skipProbMain, lambdaBT);

    // Deterministic top-20 ranking for backtest evaluation (no exploration here)
    var mainProbs = probMassMainNorm
      .map(function(p, i) {
        var skipScore = (Array.isArray(skipScoresForBacktest) && skipScoresForBacktest[i] != null)
          ? skipScoresForBacktest[i]
          : 0;

        return {
          number:    i + 1,
          prob:      p,
          baseProb:  aiNormMain[i],
          skipScore: skipScore
        };
      })
      .sort(function(a, b) { return b.prob - a.prob; })
      .slice(0, 20);
    var mainPicks = mainProbs.slice(0, settings.PICK_SIZE).map(function(o) { return o.number; });

    // Proper scoring updates (main)
    totalBrierMain += skaiBrierScore(probMassMainNorm, actualMainSet, settings.MAIN_MAX);
    totalLogLossMain += skaiLogLoss(probMassMainNorm, actualMainSet, settings.MAIN_MAX);
    totalExpectedMassInPicksMain += skaiExpectedMassInPicks(probMassMainNorm, mainPicks);

    var mainMatch=0;
    var predictedMain = mainProbs.map(function(x) {
      if (actualMain.indexOf(x.number) !== -1) { mainMatch++; return skaiBuildMatchSpan(x.number); }
      return x.number;
    });
    // top-extras
    var predictedExtra = [], extraMatch=0;
    if (settings.HAS_EXTRA) {
      var actualExtraSet = skaiMakeSet(actualExtra);

      // Build full normalized mass for extra
      var aiRawExtra = skaiArrayFrom(extraArr).map(function(v) {
        var p = (typeof v === 'number' && isFinite(v)) ? v : 0;
        return Math.min(1 - SKAI_EPS, Math.max(SKAI_EPS, p));
      });
      var probMassExtraNorm = normalizePositive(aiRawExtra);

      var extraProbs = skaiArrayFrom(extraArr)
        .map(function(p,i) { return { number: i+1, prob: p }; })
        .sort(function(a,b) { return b.prob-a.prob; })
        .slice(0, settings.EXTRA_SUGGESTIONS);

      // Picks used for evaluation (top EXTRA_COUNT)
      var extraPicks = extraProbs.slice(0, settings.EXTRA_COUNT).map(function(o) { return o.number; });

      // Proper scoring updates (extra)
      totalBrierExtra += skaiBrierScore(probMassExtraNorm, actualExtraSet, settings.EXTRA_MAX);
      totalLogLossExtra += skaiLogLoss(probMassExtraNorm, actualExtraSet, settings.EXTRA_MAX);
      totalExpectedMassInPicksExtra += skaiExpectedMassInPicks(probMassExtraNorm, extraPicks);
      predictedExtra = extraProbs.map(function(x) {
        if (actualExtra.indexOf(x.number) !== -1) { extraMatch++; return skaiBuildMatchSpan(x.number); }
        return x.number;
      });
    }

    results.push({
      date:             sortedDrawsAsc[idx].draw_date,
      actualMain:       actualMain.join(', '),
      actualExtra:      actualExtra,
      predictedMain:    predictedMain.join(', '),
      predictedExtra:   predictedExtra,
      mainMatchCount:   mainMatch,
      extraMatchCount:  extraMatch
    });

    // Elite TFJS cleanup for each backtest step.
    try {
      if (model && typeof model.dispose === "function") {
        model.dispose();
      }

      if (typeof pred !== "undefined") {
        if (settings.HAS_EXTRA && pred && pred.length) {
          pred[0].dispose();
          pred[1].dispose();
        } else if (pred && typeof pred.dispose === "function") {
          pred.dispose();
        }
      }

      if (typeof tf !== "undefined" && typeof tf.memory === "function") {
        console.log("TFJS memory after backtest step:", tf.memory());
      }
    } catch (btCleanupError) {
      console.warn("Backtest cleanup warning:", btCleanupError);
    }
      // Continue with next step (recursive ES5-safe chain)
      processBacktestStep(bi + 1);
    }).catch(rejectAll);
  } // end processBacktestStep

  // Start the recursive chain
  try {
    processBacktestStep(0);
  } catch (e) {
    rejectAll(e);
  }
  }); // end new Promise
}
// --- END FIXED BACKTEST FUNCTIONS ---


      
      startButton.addEventListener('click', function startAnalysis(event) {
       // Scroll the loading container into center view on start
setTimeout(function() {
  var loadingEl = document.getElementById('loading');
  if (loadingEl && typeof loadingEl.scrollIntoView === 'function') {
    loadingEl.scrollIntoView({
      behavior: 'smooth',
      block: 'center'
    });
  }
}, 100); // slight delay to ensure DOM has time to show the element
 
        event.preventDefault();
        // TensorFlow.js and Chart.js are loaded via <script> tags in the head.
        // We now rely on the global 'tf' and 'Chart' objects.
        loadingDiv.style.display = 'block';
        startButton.style.display = 'none';
        var EPOCHS = parseInt(epochsInput.value);
        var BATCH_SIZE = parseInt(batchSizeInput.value);
        var DROPOUT_RATE = parseFloat(dropoutRateInput.value);
        var LEARNING_RATE = parseFloat(learningRateInput.value);
        var ACTIVATION_FUNCTION = activationFunctionInput.value;
        var HIDDEN_LAYERS = parseInt(hiddenLayersInput.value);
        var recencyDecay = parseFloat(document.getElementById('recencyDecay').value) || 1;
        document.getElementById('saveRecencyDecay').value = recencyDecay;

        if (isNaN(EPOCHS) || EPOCHS <= 0) {
          alert("Please enter a valid number of epochs.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        if (isNaN(BATCH_SIZE) || BATCH_SIZE <= 0) {
          alert("Please enter a valid batch size.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        if (isNaN(DROPOUT_RATE) || DROPOUT_RATE < 0 || DROPOUT_RATE > 1) {
          alert("Please enter a valid dropout rate between 0 and 1.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        if (isNaN(LEARNING_RATE) || LEARNING_RATE <= 0) {
          alert("Please enter a valid learning rate greater than 0.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        if (!ACTIVATION_FUNCTION) {
          alert("Please select an activation function.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        if (isNaN(HIDDEN_LAYERS) || HIDDEN_LAYERS <= 0) {
          alert("Please enter a valid number of hidden layers.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        epochValue.innerText = EPOCHS;
        batchSizeValue.innerText = BATCH_SIZE;
        dropoutRateValue.innerText = DROPOUT_RATE;
        learningRateValue.innerText = LEARNING_RATE;
        activationFunctionValue.innerText = ACTIVATION_FUNCTION;
        hiddenLayersValue.innerText = HIDDEN_LAYERS;
        recencyDecayValue.innerText = recencyDecay;  
        var latestDrawDate = latestDrawDateInput.value;
        if (!latestDrawDate) {
          alert("Please enter a valid latest draw date.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        latestDrawDateValue.innerText = latestDrawDate;
        var filteredDraws = draws.filter(function(draw) { return new Date(draw.draw_date) <= new Date(latestDrawDate); });
        // Sort ascending (OLDEST first) so we can build proper next-draw pairs and Skip features
        filteredDraws.sort(function(a, b) { return new Date(a.draw_date) - new Date(b.draw_date); });
        if (filteredDraws.length < 2) {
          alert("Not enough data before the selected date. Please choose a different date.");
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          startButton.style.display = 'block';
          return;
        }
        var latestDrawData = filteredDraws[filteredDraws.length - 1];
        var latestDraw = latestDrawData.numbers;
        var historicalData = filteredDraws.map(function(draw) { return draw.numbers; });
        // Pre-compute Skip feature series for the full historical sequence
        var skipFeatureSeries = computeSkipFeatureSeries(historicalData, pickSize, mainNumbersMax);
        startTime = Date.now();

        epochStartTime = Date.now();
        var funMessageIndex = 0;
        var funMessageTimer = setInterval(function() {
          funMessageIndex = (funMessageIndex + 1) % funMessages.length;
          funMessageDiv.innerText = funMessages[funMessageIndex];
        }, funMessageInterval);
        countdownDiv.innerHTML = "Estimated time: Calculating...";
        try { window.dispatchEvent(new Event('skai:ml:start')); } catch (_) {}
        // Single-threaded JS guarantees no concurrency; skip re-init if already on CPU
        // to avoid resetting TensorFlow.js internal PRNG state between batch runs.
        var backendReady = (typeof tf.getBackend === 'function' && tf.getBackend() === 'cpu')
          ? Promise.resolve()
          : tf.setBackend('cpu');
        backendReady.then(function() {
          console.log('TensorFlow.js version:', tf.version.tfjs);
          console.log('Backend:', tf.getBackend());
          progressMessage.innerText = messages[0];
    // normalize and build X/Y (with Skip features)
        var normalizedHistoricalData = normalizeData(historicalData);
        var xs = [];
        var ys_main = [];
        var ys_extra = [];

        // PATCH: Medium recency weighting without sampleWeight (TFJS build limitation)
        // Strategy: replicate newest 25% of training pairs 3× (older 75% stay 1×)
        var totalPairs   = historicalData.length - 1;
        var recentStart  = Math.floor(totalPairs * 0.75); // newest 25%

        for (var i = 0; i < totalPairs; i++) {
          var baseInput    = normalizedHistoricalData[i];
          var skipFeatures = skipFeatureSeries[i];
          var inputVector  = baseInput.concat(skipFeatures);

          var nextDraw = historicalData[i + 1];

          // Y: main multi-hot
          var mainNumbers = nextDraw.slice(0, pickSize);
          var mainNumbersVector = skaiArrayFill(mainNumbersMax, 0);
          mainNumbers.forEach(function(num) {
            if (num >= 1 && num <= mainNumbersMax) {
              mainNumbersVector[num - 1] = 1;
            }
          });

          // Y: extra multi-hot (if present, supports 1 or more extra balls)
          var extraVector = null;
          if (hasExtraBall) {
            extraVector = skaiArrayFill(extraBallMax, 0);
            for (var _eb = 0; _eb < numExtraBalls; _eb++) {
              var _extraNum = nextDraw[pickSize + _eb];
              if (_extraNum >= 1 && _extraNum <= extraBallMax) {
                extraVector[_extraNum - 1] = 1;
              }
            }
          }

          // Replication factor: driven by recencyDecay (set by profile preset).
          // Thresholds are chosen to bracket the three standard profile values:
          //   explorative ~0.85 (below 0.88) → 5x  (heavy recent-draw weighting)
          //   balanced    ~0.94 (below 0.95) → 3x  (moderate recent-draw weighting)
          //   conservative ~0.97 (above 0.95) → 2x  (near-uniform weighting)
          var recentReps = (recencyDecay <= 0.88) ? 5 : (recencyDecay <= 0.95) ? 3 : 2;
          var reps = (i >= recentStart) ? recentReps : 1;

          for (var r = 0; r < reps; r++) {
            xs.push(inputVector);
            ys_main.push(mainNumbersVector);
            if (hasExtraBall) {
              ys_extra.push(extraVector);
            }
          }
        }

        // PATCH: sampleWeight disabled (not supported in this TFJS build)
        // const sampleWeightTensor = ...


// -- tensors --
        var xsTensor     = tf.tensor2d(xs);
        var ysMainTensor = tf.tensor2d(ys_main);

          var ysExtraTensor;
          if (hasExtraBall) {
            ysExtraTensor = tf.tensor2d(ys_extra);
          }
          var inputShape = xs[0].length;
          var input = tf.input({ shape: [inputShape] });
          var x = tf.layers.dense({ units: 128, activation: ACTIVATION_FUNCTION }).apply(input);
          x = tf.layers.dropout({ rate: DROPOUT_RATE }).apply(x);
          for (var i = 0; i < HIDDEN_LAYERS; i++) {
            x = tf.layers.dense({ units: 64, activation: ACTIVATION_FUNCTION }).apply(x);
            x = tf.layers.dropout({ rate: DROPOUT_RATE }).apply(x);
          }
          var mainNumbersOutput = tf.layers.dense({ units: mainNumbersMax, activation: 'sigmoid', name: 'main_numbers_output' }).apply(x);
          var outputs, model;
          if (hasExtraBall) {
            var extraOutput = tf.layers.dense({ units: extraBallMax, activation: 'sigmoid', name: 'extra_output' }).apply(x);
            outputs = [mainNumbersOutput, extraOutput];
            model = tf.model({ inputs: input, outputs: outputs });
          } else {
            outputs = mainNumbersOutput;
            model = tf.model({ inputs: input, outputs: outputs });
          }
          var optimizer = tf.train.adam(LEARNING_RATE);
          var loss, metrics;
          if (hasExtraBall) {
            loss = ['binaryCrossentropy', 'binaryCrossentropy'];
            metrics = ['accuracy'];
          } else {
            loss = 'binaryCrossentropy';
            metrics = ['accuracy'];
          }
          model.compile({
            optimizer: optimizer,
            loss: loss,
            metrics: metrics
          });
          var yTrain;
          if (hasExtraBall) {
            yTrain = {
              main_numbers_output: ysMainTensor,
              extra_output: ysExtraTensor
            };
          } else {
            yTrain = ysMainTensor;
          }
		var fitArgs = {
            epochs: EPOCHS,
            batchSize: BATCH_SIZE,
            shuffle: false,
            validationSplit: 0.2,
            // PATCH: sampleWeight disabled (not supported in this TFJS build)
            // Recency weighting is approximated via training-pair replication (newest 25% repeated 3×).
            callbacks: {
              onEpochBegin: function(epoch, logs) {
                epochStartTime = Date.now();
                progressMessage.innerText = messages[3];
              },
              onEpochEnd: function(epoch, logs) {
                var epochEndTime = Date.now();
                var epochDuration = (epochEndTime - epochStartTime) / 1000;
                if (epoch === 0) {
                  smoothedTimePerEpoch = epochDuration;
                } else {
                  smoothedTimePerEpoch = (smoothingFactor * epochDuration) + ((1 - smoothingFactor) * smoothedTimePerEpoch);
                }
                var epochsRemaining = EPOCHS - (epoch + 1);
                var estimatedRemainingTime = epochsRemaining * smoothedTimePerEpoch;
                if (estimatedRemainingTime > 0) {
                  var minutes = Math.floor(estimatedRemainingTime / 60);
                  var seconds = Math.floor(estimatedRemainingTime % 60);
                  var mm = (minutes < 10 ? '0' : '') + minutes;
                  var ss = (seconds < 10 ? '0' : '') + seconds;
                  countdownDiv.innerHTML = 'Estimated time left: ' + mm + ':' + ss;
                } else {
                  countdownDiv.innerHTML = "Main analysis completed! Now running backtesting...";
                }
                var percentage = Math.round(((epoch + 1) / EPOCHS) * 100);
                progressBar.style.width = percentage + '%';
                progressBar.textContent = percentage + '%';
                var msgIndex = Math.floor((percentage / 100) * messages.length);
                if (msgIndex >= messages.length) {
                  msgIndex = messages.length - 1;
                }
                progressMessage.innerText = messages[msgIndex];
              }
            }
          };

          // PATCH: training must run before predict; otherwise results are random + instant
          progressMessage.innerText = messages[3];
          return model.fit(xsTensor, yTrain, fitArgs).then(function() {
          progressMessage.innerText = messages[6];

          // Build prediction input: normalized latest draw + its Skip feature vector
          var latestIndex          = historicalData.length - 1;
          var normalizedLatestDraw = normalizeData([latestDraw])[0];
          var latestSkipFeatures   = skipFeatureSeries[latestIndex];
          var latestInputVector    = normalizedLatestDraw.concat(latestSkipFeatures);

          // Use the latest Skip feature vector as our per-number Skip scores for bias
          var skipScores = latestSkipFeatures;

          var predictionInputTensor = tf.tensor2d([latestInputVector]);
          var prediction = model.predict(predictionInputTensor);
          var mainNumbersPrediction, extraPrediction;

          if (hasExtraBall) {
            mainNumbersPrediction = prediction[0].dataSync();
            extraPrediction = prediction[1].dataSync();
          } else {
            mainNumbersPrediction = prediction.dataSync();
          }

          // Dispose prediction tensors immediately after dataSync copies values into TypedArrays.
          try {
            predictionInputTensor.dispose();

            if (hasExtraBall && prediction && prediction.length) {
              prediction[0].dispose();
              prediction[1].dispose();
            } else if (prediction && typeof prediction.dispose === "function") {
              prediction.dispose();
            }
          } catch (disposePredictionError) {
            console.warn("Prediction tensor cleanup warning:", disposePredictionError);
          }
          // Apply mathematically coherent SKAI blend:
          // 1) normalize AI marginals into a mass function
          // 2) convert skipScores into a skip-expert distribution
          // 3) combine via log-opinion pool (geometric mixture)
          var modeKey = getSelectedSkaiMode();

          // 1) AI marginals → normalized mass
          var aiRaw = skaiArrayFrom(mainNumbersPrediction).map(function(v) {
            var p = (typeof v === 'number' && isFinite(v)) ? v : 0;
            return Math.min(1 - SKAI_EPS, Math.max(SKAI_EPS, p));
          });
          var aiNorm = normalizePositive(aiRaw);

          // 2) Skip scores → skip-expert distribution
          var skipArr = Array.isArray(skipScores)
            ? skipScores
            : skaiArrayFill(aiNorm.length, 0);

          var skipBetaLocal = getSkaiSkipBeta(modeKey);
          var skipProbLocal = buildSkipExpertProbs(skipArr, skipBetaLocal);

          // 3) Blend weight λ (adaptive in Mixed)
          var lambdaLocal = getSkaiLambda(modeKey, aiNorm, skipProbLocal);

          // Live blend readout (single Signal Blend percentage, plus β and T)
          var tLive = (typeof skaiGetStoredTemp === 'function') ? skaiGetStoredTemp(modeKey) : 1.0;
          skaiUpdateBlendReadout(modeKey, lambdaLocal, skipBetaLocal, tLive);

          var finalProbNorm = logOpinionPool(aiNorm, skipProbLocal, lambdaLocal);

          // PATCH: removed duplicate (older) SKAI blend block to prevent redeclarations

          // Live readout already updated above with actual adaptive λ.

          // PATCH: removed duplicate finalProbNorm declaration; reuse the earlier finalProbNorm
          var mainNumbersProbabilities = finalProbNorm.map(function(p, i) {
            var number    = i + 1;
            var skipScore = (Array.isArray(skipScores) && skipScores[i] != null) ? skipScores[i] : 0;

            return {
              number:          number,
              probability:     p,
              baseProbability: aiNorm[i],
              skipScore:       skipScore
            };
          });
          mainNumbersProbabilities.sort(function(a, b) { return b.probability - a.probability; });
          // Populate batch-runner capture globals
          try {
            window.skaiSaveMainOrdered = mainNumbersProbabilities.slice(0, 20).map(function (item) { return item.number; });
            window.skaiSaveExtraOrdered = [];
            window.coreAiLastResultPayload = {
              mainNumbers: window.skaiSaveMainOrdered.slice(),
              extraNumbers: [],
              rankedMain: mainNumbersProbabilities.slice(0, 20).map(function(item, idx) {
                return {
                  rank: idx + 1,
                  number: item.number,
                  probability: Number((item.probability || 0).toFixed(8)),
                  base_probability: Number((item.baseProbability || 0).toFixed(8)),
                  skip_score: Number((item.skipScore || 0).toFixed(8))
                };
              }),
              rankedExtra: [],
              generatedAt: (new Date()).toISOString(),
              source: 'core_ai_batch_snapshot'
            };
            try {
              var snapFieldEarly = document.getElementById('saveCoreAiSnapshotJson');
              if (snapFieldEarly) { snapFieldEarly.value = JSON.stringify(window.coreAiLastResultPayload); }
              if (typeof window.coreAiActiveBatchIndex !== "undefined") {
                if (!window.coreAiBatchSnapshots) { window.coreAiBatchSnapshots = {}; }
                window.coreAiBatchSnapshots[window.coreAiActiveBatchIndex] = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(window.coreAiLastResultPayload));
              }
            } catch (_) {}
          } catch (_) {}
          try { window.dispatchEvent(new Event('skai:score:done')); } catch (_) {}
          // Final selection: exploit + controlled exploration (Explorative/Mixed), strict top-k otherwise
          var pickedNumbers = skaiSelectPicksFromMass(finalProbNorm, pickSize, modeKey);

          // Map pickedNumbers back to objects (for display wiring that expects {number,...})
          var pickedSet = skaiMakeSet(pickedNumbers);
          var predictedMainNumbers = mainNumbersProbabilities
            .filter(function(item) { return skaiSetHas(pickedSet, item.number); })
            .sort(function(a, b) { return a.number - b.number; });
          // Display top 20 numbers in order of likelihood (highest probability first)
          var numbersHTML = '';
          var top20Nums = mainNumbersProbabilities.slice(0, 20);
          for (var rankIdx = 0; rankIdx < top20Nums.length; rankIdx++) {
            var rankItem = top20Nums[rankIdx];
            numbersHTML +=
              skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="skai-rank-wrap"',
                skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="skai-rank-label"', '#' + (rankIdx + 1)) +
                skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="number-ball"', skaiEscapeHtml(rankItem.number))
              ) + '\n';
          }

          // For hasExtraBall games, show top 5 extra balls in order of likelihood.
          // extraSorted is computed once per prediction render (small array, O(n log n) is negligible).
          if (hasExtraBall && extraPrediction) {
            var extraSorted = skaiArrayFrom(extraPrediction)
              .map(function(prob, eIdx) { return { number: eIdx + 1, probability: prob }; });
            extraSorted.sort(function(a, b) { return b.probability - a.probability; });
            var top5Extra = extraSorted.slice(0, 5);
            if (top5Extra.length > 0) {
              var extraDividerLabel = numExtraBalls > 1 ? 'Extra Balls' : 'Extra Ball';
              numbersHTML += skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="skai-extra-divider"',
                SKAI_MDASH + ' ' + skaiEscapeHtml(extraDividerLabel) + ' ' + SKAI_MDASH
              ) + '\n';
              for (var eRankIdx = 0; eRankIdx < top5Extra.length; eRankIdx++) {
                numbersHTML +=
                  skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="skai-rank-wrap"',
                    skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="skai-rank-label"', '#' + (eRankIdx + 1)) +
                    skaiHtmlFullTag('span', 'class="number-ball powerball"', skaiEscapeHtml(top5Extra[eRankIdx].number))
                  ) + '\n';
              }
            }
          }

          predictedNumbersDiv.innerHTML = numbersHTML;
          predictedNumbersDiv.style.display = "block";

          var breakdownHTML =
            skaiHtmlFullTag('h3', '', 'Top 20 Main Numbers Breakdown') +
            skaiHtmlTag('table', '', false) +
            skaiHtmlTag('thead', '', false) +
            skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', false) +
            skaiHtmlFullTag('th', '', 'Number') +
            skaiHtmlFullTag('th', '', 'Probability (%)') +
            skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', true) +
            skaiHtmlTag('thead', '', true) +
            skaiHtmlTag('tbody', '', false);
          mainNumbersProbabilities.slice(0, 20).forEach(function(item) {
            var probabilityPercentage = (item.probability * 100).toFixed(2);
            breakdownHTML +=
              skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', false) +
              skaiHtmlFullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(item.number)) +
              skaiHtmlFullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(probabilityPercentage + '%')) +
              skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', true);
          });
          breakdownHTML += skaiHtmlTag('tbody', '', true) + skaiHtmlTag('table', '', true);
          if (hasExtraBall) {
            var extraProbabilities = skaiArrayFrom(extraPrediction)
              .map(function(prob, index) { return { number: index + 1, probability: prob }; });
            extraProbabilities.sort(function(a, b) { return b.probability - a.probability; });
            breakdownHTML +=
              skaiHtmlFullTag('h3', '', 'Top 5 Extra Numbers Breakdown') +
              skaiHtmlTag('table', '', false) +
              skaiHtmlTag('thead', '', false) +
              skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', false) +
              skaiHtmlFullTag('th', '', 'Number') +
              skaiHtmlFullTag('th', '', 'Probability (%)') +
              skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', true) +
              skaiHtmlTag('thead', '', true) +
              skaiHtmlTag('tbody', '', false);
            extraProbabilities.slice(0, 5).forEach(function(item) {
              var probabilityPercentage = (item.probability * 100).toFixed(2);
              breakdownHTML +=
                skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', false) +
                skaiHtmlFullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(item.number)) +
                skaiHtmlFullTag('td', '', skaiEscapeHtml(probabilityPercentage + '%')) +
                skaiHtmlTag('tr', '', true);
            });
            breakdownHTML += skaiHtmlTag('tbody', '', true) + skaiHtmlTag('table', '', true);
          }
          numberBreakdownTableDiv.innerHTML = breakdownHTML;
          
          progressMessage.innerText = messages[8];
          var predictionDate = new Date();
          var predictionDateString = predictionDate.toLocaleString();
          predictionDateValue.innerText = predictionDateString;
 
   
        
        // (1) capture your PHP lotteryName into JS input
var lotteryName = <?php echo json_encode((string) $lotteryName, JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE | JSON_HEX_TAG | JSON_HEX_APOS | JSON_HEX_QUOT | JSON_HEX_AMP); ?>;

// (2) update the hidden generated_at if you haven't already
document.getElementById('saveGeneratedAt').value =
  predictionDateString; // or use your formatDateForDB() if you need YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS

// (3) now push the same timestamp into your label field
document.getElementById('saveLabel').value =
  lotteryName + ' Prediction - ' + predictionDateString;

        
        
        //  -  format to YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS for our DB  - 
function formatDateForDB(d) {
  function pad2(n) { return (n < 10 ? '0' : '') + n; }
  return d.getFullYear() + '-' + pad2(d.getMonth()+1) + '-' + pad2(d.getDate()) + ' ' +
         pad2(d.getHours()) + ':' + pad2(d.getMinutes()) + ':' + pad2(d.getSeconds());
}

      // populate hidden field with DB-formatted timestamp
        var now = new Date();
        var dbTimestamp = formatDateForDB(now);
        document.getElementById('saveGeneratedAt').value = dbTimestamp;
        // label can still show human-friendly time
        document.getElementById('saveLabel').value =
          lotteryName + ' Prediction - ' + now.toLocaleString();


// Save AI analysis specs to hidden fields
document.getElementById('saveEpochs').value              = EPOCHS;
document.getElementById('saveBatchSize').value           = BATCH_SIZE;
document.getElementById('saveDropoutRate').value         = DROPOUT_RATE;
document.getElementById('saveLearningRate').value        = LEARNING_RATE;
document.getElementById('saveActivationFunction').value  = ACTIVATION_FUNCTION;
document.getElementById('saveHiddenLayers').value        = HIDDEN_LAYERS;
var _saveModeKey = (typeof getSelectedSkaiMode === 'function') ? getSelectedSkaiMode() : 'balanced';
document.getElementById('saveModeKey').value            = _saveModeKey;
document.getElementById('saveLatestDrawDate').value     = latestDrawDate;

 
           // After generating the predictions, populate the hidden fields in the save form
          // For MAIN numbers, use all predicted main numbers instead of just the first "pickSize".
          var mainPredictionNumbers = mainNumbersProbabilities
  .slice(0, 20)
  .map(function(item) { return item.number; })
  .join(',');

      
          // For the EXTRA ball predictions, if applicable, compute the entire sorted list
          var extraPredictionNumbers = "";
          if (hasExtraBall) {
            var extraProbabilities = skaiArrayFrom(extraPrediction).map(function(prob, index) { return { number: index + 1, probability: prob }; });
            extraProbabilities.sort(function(a, b) { return b.probability - a.probability; });
           extraPredictionNumbers = extraProbabilities
  .slice(0, 5)
  .map(function(item) { return item.number; })
  .join(',');
          }
      
          // Populate the hidden form fields with the entire list of predicted values.
          document.getElementById('saveMainNumbers').value = mainPredictionNumbers;
          document.getElementById('saveExtraBallNumbers').value = extraPredictionNumbers;
          // Core AI technical learning payload for MyLottoExpert scoring and batch comparison.
          try {
            var rankedMainPayload = mainNumbersProbabilities.slice(0, 20).map(function(item, idx) {
              return {
                rank: idx + 1,
                number: item.number,
                probability: Number((item.probability || 0).toFixed(8)),
                base_probability: Number((item.baseProbability || 0).toFixed(8)),
                skip_score: Number((item.skipScore || 0).toFixed(8))
              };
            });
            var rankedExtraPayload = [];
            if (hasExtraBall) {
              rankedExtraPayload = extraProbabilities.slice(0, 5).map(function(item, idx) {
                return {
                  rank: idx + 1,
                  number: item.number,
                  probability: Number((item.probability || 0).toFixed(8))
                };
              });
            }
            document.getElementById('saveRankedMainNumbersJson').value = JSON.stringify(rankedMainPayload);
            document.getElementById('saveMainDisplayJson').value = JSON.stringify({
              renderer_hint: 'ranked_main_top20',
              numbers: rankedMainPayload.map(function(item) { return item.number; }),
              ranked: rankedMainPayload
            });
            document.getElementById('saveRankedExtraNumbersJson').value = JSON.stringify(rankedExtraPayload);
            document.getElementById('saveExtraDisplayJson').value = JSON.stringify({
              renderer_hint: hasExtraBall ? 'ranked_extra_top5' : 'none',
              numbers: rankedExtraPayload.map(function(item) { return item.number; }),
              ranked: rankedExtraPayload
            });
            try {
              window.coreAiLastResultPayload = {
                mainNumbers: rankedMainPayload.map(function(item) { return item.number; }),
                extraNumbers: rankedExtraPayload.map(function(item) { return item.number; }),
                rankedMain: rankedMainPayload,
                rankedExtra: rankedExtraPayload,
                generatedAt: (new Date()).toISOString(),
                source: 'core_ai_final_result_snapshot'
              };
              var snapFieldFinal = document.getElementById('saveCoreAiSnapshotJson');
              if (snapFieldFinal) { snapFieldFinal.value = JSON.stringify(window.coreAiLastResultPayload); }
              if (typeof window.coreAiActiveBatchIndex !== "undefined") {
                if (!window.coreAiBatchSnapshots) { window.coreAiBatchSnapshots = {}; }
                window.coreAiBatchSnapshots[window.coreAiActiveBatchIndex] = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(window.coreAiLastResultPayload));
              }
            } catch (_) {}
            if (typeof window.coreAiBuildEvidenceSettings === 'function') {
              document.getElementById('saveSettingsJson').value = JSON.stringify(window.coreAiBuildEvidenceSettings(_saveModeKey));
            }
          } catch (_coreEvidenceErr) {
            console.warn('Core AI evidence payload warning:', _coreEvidenceErr);
          }


          // Phase 2: prepare client-side integrity hash for the server-validated save.
          try {
            if (typeof window.skaiPrepareClientIntegrity === 'function') {
              window.skaiPrepareClientIntegrity().then(function(hash) {
                console.log('SKAI client integrity ready:', hash);
              }).catch(function(err) {
                console.warn('SKAI client integrity warning:', err);
              });
            }
          } catch (_integrityErr) {
            console.warn('SKAI client integrity setup warning:', _integrityErr);
          }

          // Elite TFJS memory cleanup for the main model.
          // At this point, output values have already been copied into plain JS arrays/strings.
          try {
            if (xsTensor && typeof xsTensor.dispose === "function") {
              xsTensor.dispose();
            }

            if (ysMainTensor && typeof ysMainTensor.dispose === "function") {
              ysMainTensor.dispose();
            }

            if (typeof ysExtraTensor !== "undefined" && ysExtraTensor && typeof ysExtraTensor.dispose === "function") {
              ysExtraTensor.dispose();
            }

            if (model && typeof model.dispose === "function") {
              model.dispose();
            }

            if (typeof tf !== "undefined" && typeof tf.memory === "function") {
              console.log("TFJS memory after main cleanup:", tf.memory());
            }
          } catch (cleanupError) {
            console.warn("TFJS cleanup warning:", cleanupError);
          }
          // Persist extra ball picks for batch-runner capture
          try {
            if (hasExtraBall && extraPredictionNumbers) {
              var _extraArr = extraPredictionNumbers.split(',').map(function (n) { return parseInt(n, 10); }).filter(function (n) { return !isNaN(n); });
              window.skaiSaveExtraOrdered = _extraArr;
            }
          } catch (_) {}
      
          // BEGIN BACKTESTING STEP (if user enabled it)
          if (enableBacktestCheckbox.checked) {
            backtestNoticeDiv.style.display = 'block';
            backtestProgressContainer.style.display = 'block';
            countdownDiv.innerHTML = "Running backtesting on previous draws...";
      
            var sortedDrawsAsc = filteredDraws.slice().sort(function(a, b) { return new Date(a.draw_date) - new Date(b.draw_date); });
            var settings = {
              EPOCHS: EPOCHS,
              BATCH_SIZE: BATCH_SIZE,
              DROPOUT_RATE: DROPOUT_RATE,
              LEARNING_RATE: LEARNING_RATE,
              ACTIVATION_FUNCTION: ACTIVATION_FUNCTION,
              HIDDEN_LAYERS: HIDDEN_LAYERS,
              RECENCY_DECAY:   recencyDecay,
              PICK_SIZE:       pickSize,
              MAIN_MAX:        mainNumbersMax,
              EXTRA_COUNT:     numExtraBalls,
              EXTRA_MAX:       extraBallMax,
              HAS_EXTRA:       hasExtraBall,
              EXTRA_SUGGESTIONS: topExtraSuggestions
            };
            // ES5-safe: return the Promise so the outer chain waits for backtest to finish
            return runBacktesting(sortedDrawsAsc, settings).then(function(backtestResults) {
              var backtestHTML = renderBacktestResults(backtestResults);
              backtestResultsDiv.innerHTML = backtestHTML;
              backtestResultsDiv.style.display = 'block';
              backtestNoticeDiv.innerHTML =
                skaiHtmlFullTag('h4', '', 'Backtesting Complete') +
                skaiHtmlFullTag('p', '', 'Backtesting has finished processing all draws.');
              backtestProgressContainer.style.display = 'none';
              countdownDiv.innerHTML = "Done! Analysis is complete.";
            });
          }
          // END BACKTESTING STEP
          return null; // no backtest - signal success to outer .then()
        }); // end model.fit().then()
      }).then(function() {
        // Final cleanup runs after tf.setBackend + model.fit (+ optional backtest) all complete
        setTimeout(function() {
          loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
          predictionDiv.style.display = 'block';
          numberBreakdownDiv.style.display = 'block';
          document.getElementById('parameterDisplay').style.display = 'block';
          document.getElementById('skai-step4-label').style.display = 'flex';
          document.getElementById('saveFormContainer').style.display = 'block';
          var _hs = document.getElementById('skai-help-strip');
          if (_hs) { _hs.style.display = 'flex'; }
        }, 1000);
        clearInterval(funMessageTimer);
        startButton.style.display = 'block';
        try { window.dispatchEvent(new Event('skai:done')); } catch (_) {}
      }).catch(function(error) {
        console.error('Error during model training or Analysis:', error);
        loadingDiv.innerText = 'An error occurred during model training or Analysis: ' + error.message;
        startButton.style.display = 'block';
        clearInterval(funMessageTimer);
      });
      });
    });
  [[/script]]

[[script defer]]
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
  var canvas1 = document.getElementById('coverageChart');
  var canvas2 = document.getElementById('ticketsChart');
  var ctx1 = canvas1 ? canvas1.getContext('2d') : null;
  var ctx2 = canvas2 ? canvas2.getContext('2d') : null;

  if (!ctx1 || !ctx2 || typeof Chart === 'undefined') {
    console.error("Chart.js not ready or canvas not found.");
    return;
  }

  var rootStyles = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement);
  var primaryBlue = rootStyles.getPropertyValue('--primary-blue').trim();
  if (!primaryBlue) {
    primaryBlue = rootStyles.getPropertyValue('--skai-blue').trim() || '#1C66FF';
  }

  function commonOptions(label) {
    return {
      responsive: true,
      maintainAspectRatio: false,
      plugins: {
        legend: { display: false }
      },
      scales: {
        y: {
          beginAtZero: true,
          title: { display: true, text: label, color: '#333' },
          ticks: {
            color: '#333',
            callback: function (val) {
              if (label.indexOf('Coverage') !== -1) return val + '%';
              if (val >= 1000) return (val / 1000).toFixed(1) + 'k';
              return val;
            }
          },
          grid: { color: '#ccc' }
        },
        x: {
          ticks: { color: '#333' },
          grid: { display: false }
        }
      }
    };
  }

  new Chart(ctx1, {
    type: 'bar',
    data: {
      labels: <?php echo json_encode(array_column($stats, 'count'), JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE | JSON_HEX_TAG | JSON_HEX_APOS | JSON_HEX_QUOT | JSON_HEX_AMP); ?>,
      datasets: [{
        data: <?php echo json_encode(array_column($stats, 'pct'), JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE | JSON_HEX_TAG | JSON_HEX_APOS | JSON_HEX_QUOT | JSON_HEX_AMP); ?>,
        backgroundColor: primaryBlue,
        borderRadius: 4
      }]
    },
    options: commonOptions('Coverage %')
  });

  new Chart(ctx2, {
    type: 'bar',
    data: {
      labels: ['Full Wheel', 'Reduced Wheel'],
      datasets: [{
        data: [11628, 28],
        backgroundColor: primaryBlue,
        borderRadius: 4
      }]
    },
    options: commonOptions('Tickets')
  });
});
