[[script]]
(function () {
  "use strict";

  function showSaveToast(msg, type) {
    try {
      var old = document.getElementById("skai-save-toast");
      if (old && old.parentNode) {
        old.parentNode.removeChild(old);
      }

      var isError = type === "error";
      var t = document.createElement("div");
      t.id = "skai-save-toast";
      t.setAttribute("role", "status");
      t.setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
      t.style.cssText =
        "position:fixed;bottom:28px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);" +
        "background:" + (isError ? "#991b1b" : "#065f46") + ";" +
        "color:#fff;padding:10px 22px;border-radius:999px;font-size:0.92rem;" +
        "font-weight:600;box-shadow:0 4px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.18);" +
        "z-index:99999;pointer-events:none;opacity:1;transition:opacity 0.4s;" +
        "max-width:92vw;text-align:center;";

      t.textContent = msg;
      document.body.appendChild(t);

      setTimeout(function () {
        try {
          t.style.opacity = "0";
        } catch (_) {}

        setTimeout(function () {
          try {
            if (t.parentNode) {
              t.parentNode.removeChild(t);
            }
          } catch (_) {}
        }, 450);
      }, 3200);
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  function showInlineSaveStatus(form, message) {
    try {
      var existing = form.querySelector("[data-skai-inline-saved]");
      if (existing && existing.parentNode) {
        existing.parentNode.removeChild(existing);
      }

      var now = new Date();
      var hh = ("0" + now.getHours()).slice(-2);
      var mm = ("0" + now.getMinutes()).slice(-2);
      var ss = ("0" + now.getSeconds()).slice(-2);

      var span = document.createElement("span");
      span.setAttribute("data-skai-inline-saved", "1");
      span.style.cssText =
        "display:block;margin-top:10px;color:#065f46;font-size:0.85rem;" +
        "font-weight:600;vertical-align:middle;";

      span.textContent = (message || "Saved successfully.") + " Saved at " + hh + ":" + mm + ":" + ss;
      form.appendChild(span);
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  function formToEncodedBody(form) {
    var data = [];
    var inputs = form.elements;

    for (var i = 0; i < inputs.length; i++) {
      var el = inputs[i];

      if (!el.name) {
        continue;
      }

      var tag = el.tagName.toUpperCase();

      if (tag === "INPUT") {
        if ((el.type === "checkbox" || el.type === "radio") && !el.checked) {
          continue;
        }

        data.push(encodeURIComponent(el.name) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(el.value || ""));
      } else if (tag === "TEXTAREA" || tag === "SELECT") {
        data.push(encodeURIComponent(el.name) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(el.value || ""));
      } else if (tag === "BUTTON" && el.type === "submit" && el.name) {
        data.push(encodeURIComponent(el.name) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(el.value || "1"));
      }
    }

    try {
      if (form && form.id === 'savePredictionForm' && window.coreAiLastResultPayload) {
        var payloadJson = JSON.stringify(window.coreAiLastResultPayload);
        var hasSnapshot = false;
        for (var si = 0; si < data.length; si++) {
          if (data[si].indexOf('core_ai_snapshot_json=') === 0) { hasSnapshot = true; break; }
        }
        if (!hasSnapshot) { data.push('core_ai_snapshot_json=' + encodeURIComponent(payloadJson)); }
      }
    } catch (_) {}

    return data.join("&");
  }

  function setButtonState(button, saving) {
    if (!button) {
      return;
    }

    button.disabled = saving;
    button.setAttribute("aria-busy", saving ? "true" : "false");

    if (saving) {
      if (!button.getAttribute("data-original-text")) {
        button.setAttribute("data-original-text", button.textContent || "Save");
      }

      button.textContent = "Saving...";
    } else {
      button.textContent = button.getAttribute("data-original-text") || "Save Core AI Run";
    }
  }

  function interceptSaveForm(form) {
    if (!form || form.__skaiSaveIntercepted) {
      return;
    }

    form.__skaiSaveIntercepted = true;

    form.addEventListener("submit", function (ev) {
      try {
        ev.preventDefault();
        ev.stopPropagation();
      } catch (_) {}

      var submitBtn = form.querySelector("[type=submit]");
      var hashField = form.querySelector("[name='client_result_hash']");
      if (hashField && !hashField.value) {
        // For Core AI batch saves the server recovers a missing hash; only
        // block when this is a regular single save where the hash is mandatory.
        var batchTypeEl = form.querySelector("[name='batch_type']");
        var batchTypeVal = batchTypeEl ? String(batchTypeEl.value || '') : '';
        var isBatchSave = batchTypeVal === 'core_ai_precision_lock_9_batch' ||
                          batchTypeVal === 'core_ai_range_test_9_batch'     ||
                          batchTypeVal === 'core_ai_batch'                  ||
                          batchTypeVal === 'core_ai_precision_lock_batch';
        if (!isBatchSave) {
          showSaveToast("Secure save is still preparing. Please wait one moment and try again.", "error");
          return false;
        }
        // Batch path: log and continue; server will generate hash server-side.
        try { console.warn("[SKAI save] client hash missing for batch save — server recovery path will be used."); } catch (_) {}
      }

      setButtonState(submitBtn, true);

      var body = formToEncodedBody(form);
      var url = form.getAttribute("action") || window.location.href.split("#")[0];

      var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
      xhr.open("POST", url, true);
      xhr.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8");
      xhr.setRequestHeader("X-Requested-With", "XMLHttpRequest");

      xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
        if (xhr.readyState !== 4) {
          return;
        }

        setButtonState(submitBtn, false);

        var parsed = null;

        try {
          parsed = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText || "{}");
        } catch (e) {
          parsed = null;
        }

        if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 400 && parsed && parsed.success === true) {
          showSaveToast(parsed.message || "Saved successfully.", "success");
          showInlineSaveStatus(form, parsed.message || "Saved successfully.");
          try { window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("skai:save:ajax:complete", { detail: { ok: true, parsed: parsed, message: parsed.message || "Saved successfully." } })); } catch (_) {}
          return;
        }

        var message = "Save failed. Please refresh the page and try again.";

        if (parsed && parsed.message) {
          message = parsed.message;
        }

        showSaveToast(message, "error");
        try { window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("skai:save:ajax:complete", { detail: { ok: false, parsed: parsed, message: message, status: xhr.status } })); } catch (_) {}
      };

      xhr.onerror = function () {
        setButtonState(submitBtn, false);
        showSaveToast("Network error while saving. Please try again.", "error");
        try { window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("skai:save:ajax:complete", { detail: { ok: false, parsed: null, message: "Network error while saving. Please try again." } })); } catch (_) {}
      };

      try {
        xhr.send(body);
      } catch (e) {
        setButtonState(submitBtn, false);
        showSaveToast("Could not send the save request. Please try again.", "error");
        try { window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("skai:save:ajax:complete", { detail: { ok: false, parsed: null, message: "Could not send the save request. Please try again." } })); } catch (_) {}
      }

      return false;
    }, true);
  }

  function wireSaveForms() {
    var forms = document.querySelectorAll("form");

    for (var i = 0; i < forms.length; i++) {
      if (forms[i].querySelector("[name='save_set']")) {
        interceptSaveForm(forms[i]);
      }
    }
  }

  if (document.readyState === "loading") {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", wireSaveForms, { once: true });
  } else {
    wireSaveForms();
  }

  window.skaiInterceptSaveForm = interceptSaveForm;
  window.skaiShowSaveToast = showSaveToast;
})();
[[/script]]

<!-- SKAI Feature A: Run Core AI 9-Batch Precision Lock -->
[[script]]
(function () {
  "use strict";

  var DEFAULT_BATCH_COMBOS = [
    { profile: "balanced",     strategy: "blend_25", blend_ai_pct: 25, label: "Balanced Focus x Blend 25%" },
    { profile: "balanced",     strategy: "blend_50", blend_ai_pct: 50, label: "Balanced Focus x Blend 50%" },
    { profile: "balanced",     strategy: "blend_75", blend_ai_pct: 75, label: "Balanced Focus x Blend 75%" },
    { profile: "explorative",  strategy: "blend_25", blend_ai_pct: 25, label: "Explorative Focus x Blend 25%" },
    { profile: "explorative",  strategy: "blend_50", blend_ai_pct: 50, label: "Explorative Focus x Blend 50%" },
    { profile: "explorative",  strategy: "blend_75", blend_ai_pct: 75, label: "Explorative Focus x Blend 75%" },
    { profile: "conservative", strategy: "blend_25", blend_ai_pct: 25, label: "Conservative Focus x Blend 25%" },
    { profile: "conservative", strategy: "blend_50", blend_ai_pct: 50, label: "Conservative Focus x Blend 50%" },
    { profile: "conservative", strategy: "blend_75", blend_ai_pct: 75, label: "Conservative Focus x Blend 75%" }
  ];

  function coreAiCleanProfile(value) {
    value = String(value || "").toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9_-]/g, "");
    if (value === "explorative" || value === "conservative" || value === "balanced") { return value; }
    return "balanced";
  }

  function coreAiClampBlend(value) {
    var n = parseInt(value, 10);
    if (isNaN(n)) { n = 50; }
    if (n < 0) { n = 0; }
    if (n > 100) { n = 100; }
    return n;
  }

  function coreAiStrategyFromBlend(blendPct) {
    return "blend_" + coreAiClampBlend(blendPct);
  }

  function coreAiBlendLabel(blendPct) {
    blendPct = coreAiClampBlend(blendPct);
    if (blendPct <= 30) { return "Skip-Pattern Heavy"; }
    if (blendPct >= 70) { return "AI-Forward"; }
    return "Balanced Mix";
  }

  function coreAiDecodeBase64Url(value) {
    try {
      value = String(value || "").replace(/-/g, "+").replace(/_/g, "/");
      while (value.length % 4) { value += "="; }
      return decodeURIComponent(escape(window.atob(value)));
    } catch (_) { return ""; }
  }

  function coreAiNormalizeBatchPlan(items) {
    if (!items || !items.length) { return null; }
    var out = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < items.length && out.length < 9; i++) {
      var item = items[i] || {};
      var profile = coreAiCleanProfile(item.profile || item.focus || item.risk_profile || "balanced");
      var blend = coreAiClampBlend(item.blend_ai_pct || item.blend_pct || item.blend || item.ai_pct || item.value || 50);
      var strategy = coreAiStrategyFromBlend(blend);
      var label = String(item.label || (coreAiFocusLabelSafe(profile) + " x Blend " + blend + "%"));
      label = label.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9 %_+().,|:-]/g, "").substring(0, 120);
      out.push({ profile: profile, strategy: strategy, blend_ai_pct: blend, label: label, handoff: true });
    }
    return out.length ? out : null;
  }

  function coreAiFocusLabelSafe(profile) {
    if (typeof window.coreAiFocusLabel === "function") {
      try { return window.coreAiFocusLabel(profile); } catch (_) {}
    }
    if (profile === "explorative") { return "Explorative Focus"; }
    if (profile === "conservative") { return "Conservative Focus"; }
    return "Balanced Focus";
  }

  function coreAiReadExternalBatchPlan() {
    try {
      var params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search || "");
      var rawPlan = params.get("core_ai_batch_plan") || params.get("le_core_ai_batch_plan") || "";
      if (rawPlan) {
        var decoded = coreAiDecodeBase64Url(rawPlan) || rawPlan;
        var parsed = JSON.parse(decoded);
        var plan = coreAiNormalizeBatchPlan(Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : (parsed.runs || parsed.batch || []));
        if (plan && plan.length) { return plan; }
      }

      var blendText = params.get("core_ai_batch_blends") || params.get("core_ai_blends") || "";
      if (blendText) {
        var blends = blendText.split(",").map(function(v){ return coreAiClampBlend(v); });
        var profiles = (params.get("core_ai_batch_profiles") || params.get("core_ai_profiles") || params.get("core_ai_batch_profile") || "balanced").split(",").map(coreAiCleanProfile);
        var items = [];
        if (profiles.length === 1) {
          for (var b = 0; b < blends.length && items.length < 9; b++) {
            items.push({ profile: profiles[0], blend_pct: blends[b] });
          }
        } else {
          for (var p = 0; p < profiles.length && items.length < 9; p++) {
            for (var j = 0; j < blends.length && items.length < 9; j++) {
              items.push({ profile: profiles[p], blend_pct: blends[j] });
            }
          }
        }
        return coreAiNormalizeBatchPlan(items);
      }
    } catch (_) {}
    return null;
  }

  var BATCH_COMBOS = coreAiReadExternalBatchPlan() || DEFAULT_BATCH_COMBOS.slice();
  var CORE_AI_HANDOFF_BATCH = !!(BATCH_COMBOS.length && BATCH_COMBOS[0] && BATCH_COMBOS[0].handoff);

  var STORAGE_KEY = "skai_batch_results_v1";
  var REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT = <?php echo (int) $pickSize; ?>;
  var AUTO_SAVE_DELAY_MS = 700;
  var batchResults = [];
  var batchRunning = false;
  var batchStopped = false;
  var batchIndex = 0;
  var batchDoneCount = 0;
  var batchUuid = '';

  function coreAiBatchUuid() {
    if (batchUuid) { return batchUuid; }
    try {
      var params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search || "");
      var externalUuid = String(params.get("core_ai_batch_uuid") || params.get("le_core_ai_batch_uuid") || "").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_.-]/g, "").substring(0, 64);
      if (externalUuid) { batchUuid = externalUuid; return batchUuid; }
    } catch (_) {}
    try {
      if (window.crypto && window.crypto.getRandomValues) {
        var buf = new Uint8Array(16);
        window.crypto.getRandomValues(buf);
        buf[6] = (buf[6] & 15) | 64;
        buf[8] = (buf[8] & 63) | 128;
        var hex = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < buf.length; i++) { hex.push(('00' + buf[i].toString(16)).slice(-2)); }
        batchUuid = hex.slice(0,4).join('') + '-' + hex.slice(4,6).join('') + '-' + hex.slice(6,8).join('') + '-' + hex.slice(8,10).join('') + '-' + hex.slice(10,16).join('');
        return batchUuid;
      }
    } catch (_) {}
    batchUuid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
      var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0;
      var v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 3 | 8);
      return v.toString(16);
    });
    return batchUuid;
  }


  function persistResults() {
    try {
      var slim = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < batchResults.length; i++) {
        var r = batchResults[i];
        slim.push({ combo: r.combo, text: r.text || "", done: !!r.done, saved: !!r.saved, savedId: r.savedId || 0, saveError: r.saveError || "", mainNumbers: r.mainNumbers || [], extraNumbers: r.extraNumbers || [] });
      }
      sessionStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(slim));
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  function loadPersistedResults() {
    try {
      var raw = sessionStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      if (!raw) { return []; }
      return JSON.parse(raw) || [];
    } catch (_) { return []; }
  }

  function qs(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }

  function setCell(profile, strategy, content, className) {
    var cell = qs("skai-cell-" + profile + "-" + strategy);
    if (!cell) { return; }
    cell.innerHTML = "";
    if (content && typeof content === "object" && content.nodeType === 1) {
      cell.appendChild(content);
    } else {
      cell.textContent = String(content === null || typeof content === "undefined" ? "" : content);
    }
    cell.style.background = className === "running" ? "#eff6ff" :
                            className === "done"    ? "#f0fdf4" :
                            className === "warning" ? "#fff7ed" :
                            className === "error"   ? "#fef2f2" : "";
  }

  function updateProgress() {
    var pt = qs("skai-batch-progress-text");
    if (pt) { pt.textContent = "Completed " + batchDoneCount + " of " + BATCH_COMBOS.length; }
  }

  function setCurrentLabel(label) {
    var cl = qs("skai-batch-current-label");
    if (cl) { cl.textContent = label; }
  }

  function showPanel() {
    var anchor = qs("core-ai-batch-monitor-anchor");
    if (anchor) { anchor.style.display = "block"; }
    var p = qs("skai-batch-panel");
    if (p) { p.style.display = "block"; }
    try { if (anchor) { anchor.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" }); } } catch (_) {}
  }

  function hideModal() {
    var m = qs("skai-batch-modal");
    if (m) { m.style.display = "none"; }
  }

  function selectProfile(profile) {
    try {
      var btns = document.querySelectorAll("[data-profile]");
      for (var i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) {
        var b = btns[i];
        var isTarget = (String(b.getAttribute("data-profile")).toLowerCase() === profile);
        b.setAttribute("aria-pressed", isTarget ? "true" : "false");
        if (isTarget) {
          b.className = (b.className || "").replace(/\bis-active\b/g, "").trim() + " is-active";
        } else {
          b.className = (b.className || "").replace(/\bis-active\b/g, "").trim();
        }
      }
      if (typeof window.coreAiSetFocusProfile === "function") { window.coreAiSetFocusProfile(profile); }
      var riskField = qs("saveRiskProfile");
      if (riskField) { riskField.value = profile; }
      var inp = qs("skai-risk-profile") || qs("skai-ai-risk-profile");
      if (inp) { inp.value = profile; }
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  function selectStrategy(strategy) {
    try {
      var btns = document.querySelectorAll("[data-strategy]");
      for (var i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) {
        var b = btns[i];
        var isTarget = (String(b.getAttribute("data-strategy")).toLowerCase() === strategy);
        b.setAttribute("aria-pressed", isTarget ? "true" : "false");
        if (isTarget) {
          b.className = (b.className || "").replace(/\bis-active\b/g, "").trim() + " is-active";
        } else {
          b.className = (b.className || "").replace(/\bis-active\b/g, "").trim();
        }
      }
      var inp = qs("skai-strategy") || qs("skai-ai-strategy");
      if (inp) { inp.value = strategy; }
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  function captureResult() {
    try {
      var containers = [
        "prediction",
        "numberBreakdown",
        "aiMainPredictionContainer",
        "aiExtraPredictionContainer",
        "skai-ai-results",
        "skai-results",
        "skaiResultsContainer",
        "skai-output"
      ];
      var html = "";
      var text = "";
      for (var i = 0; i < containers.length; i++) {
        var el = qs(containers[i]);
        if (el && el.innerHTML && el.innerHTML.trim().length > 20) {
          html += el.outerHTML;
          text += (el.textContent || el.innerText || "").trim().substring(0, 2000);
        }
      }
      if (!html) {
        var picks = document.querySelectorAll(".number-ball, .skai-number-ball, .skai-pick, [class*='ball'], [class*='pick-number']");
        if (picks.length > 0) {
          var tmp = document.createElement("div");
          for (var j = 0; j < picks.length && j < 30; j++) {
            tmp.appendChild(picks[j].cloneNode(true));
          }
          html = tmp.innerHTML;
          text = tmp.textContent || "";
        }
      }
      var mainNums  = (window.skaiSaveMainOrdered  && window.skaiSaveMainOrdered.length)
        ? window.skaiSaveMainOrdered.slice()  : [];
      var extraNums = (window.skaiSaveExtraOrdered && window.skaiSaveExtraOrdered.length)
        ? window.skaiSaveExtraOrdered.slice() : [];

      // v15: batch snapshot recovery, Save All 9 uses old working form-submit behavior.
      // During a 9-run batch, each prediction stores its ranked numbers into
      // window.coreAiBatchSnapshots[batchIndex] at the moment numbers are created.
      // This prevents the next run from overwriting the previous run's save fields.
      try {
        var activeCaptureIdx = (typeof window.coreAiActiveBatchIndex !== "undefined") ? window.coreAiActiveBatchIndex : null;
        var snap = (window.coreAiBatchSnapshots && activeCaptureIdx !== null) ? window.coreAiBatchSnapshots[activeCaptureIdx] : null;
        if (snap && snap.mainNumbers && snap.mainNumbers.length) {
          mainNums = snap.mainNumbers.slice();
        }
        if (snap && snap.extraNumbers && snap.extraNumbers.length) {
          extraNums = snap.extraNumbers.slice();
        }
      } catch (_) {}

      try {
        if (mainNums.length < REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT && window.coreAiLastResultPayload && window.coreAiLastResultPayload.mainNumbers && window.coreAiLastResultPayload.mainNumbers.length) {
          mainNums = window.coreAiLastResultPayload.mainNumbers.slice();
        }
        if ((!extraNums || !extraNums.length) && window.coreAiLastResultPayload && window.coreAiLastResultPayload.extraNumbers && window.coreAiLastResultPayload.extraNumbers.length) {
          extraNums = window.coreAiLastResultPayload.extraNumbers.slice();
        }
      } catch (_) {}

      // Core AI batch capture gate:
      // Use captured prediction numbers as the primary proof of a completed run.
      // Completion events are helpful, but they can fire before the batch listener catches them.
      // If the hidden save fields already contain valid numbers, recover from those fields.
      function parseCsvNumbers(value) {
        var out = [];
        String(value || "").split(",").forEach(function (part) {
          var n = parseInt(String(part).replace(/[^0-9]/g, ""), 10);
          if (n > 0 && out.indexOf(n) === -1) { out.push(n); }
        });
        return out;
      }
      if (mainNums.length < REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
        var hiddenMain = document.getElementById("saveMainNumbers");
        var hiddenMainNums = hiddenMain ? parseCsvNumbers(hiddenMain.value) : [];
        if (hiddenMainNums.length >= REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
          mainNums = hiddenMainNums.slice(0, Math.max(REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT, hiddenMainNums.length));
        }
      }
      if (!extraNums.length) {
        var hiddenExtra = document.getElementById("saveExtraBallNumbers");
        var hiddenExtraNums = hiddenExtra ? parseCsvNumbers(hiddenExtra.value) : [];
        if (hiddenExtraNums.length) { extraNums = hiddenExtraNums; }
      }

      // Final relaxed recovery: read the rendered ranked balls if globals/hidden fields lag.
      if (mainNums.length < REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
        try {
          var renderedMain = [];
          var renderedExtra = [];
          var balls = document.querySelectorAll('#predictedNumbers .number-ball');
          for (var bi = 0; bi < balls.length; bi++) {
            var bn = parseInt(String(balls[bi].textContent || balls[bi].innerText || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, ''), 10);
            if (!bn) { continue; }
            if ((balls[bi].className || '').indexOf('powerball') >= 0) {
              if (renderedExtra.indexOf(bn) === -1) { renderedExtra.push(bn); }
            } else if (renderedMain.indexOf(bn) === -1) {
              renderedMain.push(bn);
            }
          }
          if (renderedMain.length >= REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
            mainNums = renderedMain;
          }
          if (!extraNums.length && renderedExtra.length) {
            extraNums = renderedExtra;
          }
        } catch (_) {}
      }

      return {
        html: html || "(no picks captured)",
        text: text || "(no picks captured)",
        mainNumbers:  mainNums,
        extraNumbers: extraNums
      };
    } catch (_) {
      return { html: "(capture error)", text: "(capture error)", mainNumbers: [], extraNumbers: [] };
    }
  }

  function runCombo(combo, onDone) {
    try {
      var mappedStrategy = (combo.blend_ai_pct <= 30) ? "skip" : (combo.blend_ai_pct >= 70 ? "ai" : "hybrid");
      if (typeof window.skaiApplyCombo === "function") {
        window.skaiApplyCombo(combo.profile, mappedStrategy);
      } else {
        selectProfile(combo.profile);
        selectStrategy(mappedStrategy);
      }
      if (typeof window.coreAiSetSignalBlendPct === "function") {
        window.coreAiSetSignalBlendPct(coreAiClampBlend(combo.blend_ai_pct));
      }
    } catch (_) {}

    try {
      var _gvLog = function (id, def) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id) || document.getElementById(id + "_ui");
        var v = (el && el.value != null) ? String(el.value).trim() : "";
        return v !== "" ? v : def;
      };
      var _ep  = _gvLog("epochs",         _gvLog("skaiadv_epochs",   "?"));
      var _bs  = _gvLog("batchSize",      _gvLog("skaiadv_batch",    "?"));
      var _dr  = _gvLog("dropoutRate",    _gvLog("skaiadv_dropout",  "?"));
      var _lr  = _gvLog("learningRate",   _gvLog("skaiadv_lr",       "?"));
      console.log("[SKAI batch] Running combo:", combo.label,
        "| profile=" + combo.profile + ", strategy=" + combo.strategy,
        "| epochs=" + _ep, "batchSize=" + _bs, "dropout=" + _dr, "lr=" + _lr
      );
      setCell(combo.profile, combo.strategy,
        "Running... (" + _ep + " ep, " + combo.profile + ", Blend " + coreAiClampBlend(combo.blend_ai_pct) + "%)", "running");
    } catch (_) {}

    var finished = false;
    var timeout = null;
    var _doneFired      = false;
    var _scoreDoneFired = false;
    var _onMlStart = null;

    function finish() {
      if (finished) { return; }
      finished = true;
      try { clearTimeout(timeout); } catch (_) {}
      if (_onMlStart) {
        try { window.removeEventListener("skai:ml:start", _onMlStart, false); } catch (_) {}
        _onMlStart = null;
      }
      try { console.log("[SKAI batch] combo done: " + combo.label +
        " | doneFired=" + _doneFired + " scoreDoneFired=" + _scoreDoneFired); } catch (_) {}
      // Simple production rule:
      // The batch is not save-ready until prediction numbers are actually visible
      // to the save layer. Older working code saved after fields were populated;
      // this keeps that behavior and avoids posting empty main_numbers.
      function captureWhenNumbersReady(attempt) {
        attempt = attempt || 0;
        var res = captureResult();
        res.verifiedCompletion = !!(_doneFired && _scoreDoneFired);
        res.completionSignals = { done: !!_doneFired, scoreDone: !!_scoreDoneFired };

        if (res.mainNumbers && res.mainNumbers.length >= REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
          onDone(res);
          return;
        }

        // Give the UI/save hidden fields time to populate after the model fires
        // completion events. This is the exact timing gap that caused empty saves.
        if (attempt < 80) {
          setTimeout(function () { captureWhenNumbersReady(attempt + 1); }, 250);
          return;
        }

        onDone(res);
      }
      setTimeout(function () { captureWhenNumbersReady(0); }, 500);
    }

    function checkAllDone() {
      if (_doneFired && _scoreDoneFired) { finish(); }
    }

    function registerCompletionListeners() {
      if (finished) { return; }
      window.addEventListener("skai:done", function onSkaiDone() {
        try { window.removeEventListener("skai:done", onSkaiDone, false); } catch (_) {}
        _doneFired = true;
        checkAllDone();
      }, false);
      window.addEventListener("skai:score:done", function onScoreDone() {
        try { window.removeEventListener("skai:score:done", onScoreDone, false); } catch (_) {}
        _scoreDoneFired = true;
        checkAllDone();
      }, false);
    }

    _onMlStart = function onMlStart() {
      try { window.removeEventListener("skai:ml:start", _onMlStart, false); } catch (_) {}
      _onMlStart = null;
      registerCompletionListeners();
    };
    window.addEventListener("skai:ml:start", _onMlStart, false);

    timeout = setTimeout(finish, 300000); /* 5-minute max wait per combo run */

    var runBtn = qs("startPrediction") || qs("runPrediction");
    if (!runBtn) {
      onDone({ html: "(run button not found)", text: "(run button not found)", mainNumbers: [], extraNumbers: [] });
      return;
    }
    try {
      window.__SKAI_RUNNING__ = false;
    } catch (_) {}
    try {
      if (typeof runBtn.click === "function") { runBtn.click(); }
      else {
        var ev = document.createEvent("MouseEvents");
        ev.initEvent("click", true, true);
        runBtn.dispatchEvent(ev);
      }
    } catch (_) {
      finish();
    }
  }

  function runNext() {
    if (batchStopped || batchIndex >= BATCH_COMBOS.length) {
      onBatchEnd();
      return;
    }
    var combo = BATCH_COMBOS[batchIndex];
    setCell(combo.profile, combo.strategy, "Running...", "running");
    setCurrentLabel(combo.label);
    var idx = batchIndex;
    batchIndex += 1;

    try {
      window.coreAiActiveBatchIndex = idx;
      window.coreAiActiveBatchCombo = combo;
      if (!window.coreAiBatchSnapshots) { window.coreAiBatchSnapshots = {}; }
    } catch (_) {}

    runCombo(combo, function (res) {
      if (batchStopped) {
        onBatchEnd();
        return;
      }

      var mainNums = res.mainNumbers || [];
      var extraNums = res.extraNumbers || [];
      var completionSignalOk = !!res.verifiedCompletion;

      /*
       * Core AI batch capture gate:
       * Capture completed run data without posting a save during the batch.
       *
       * Why:
       * - The run may finish correctly, but the batch capture can happen before
       *   window.skaiSaveMainOrdered or visible number balls are fully ready.
       * - The save form and ranked JSON may already contain the real prediction.
       * - The save step later uses the normal save form path, including the
       *   same client-integrity preparation as the older working file.
       *
       * Save proof order:
       * 1. Captured ordered main numbers.
       * 2. Hidden saveMainNumbers field.
       * 3. Ranked main JSON evidence.
       */
      function coreAiParseCsvNumbersForSave(value) {
        var out = [];
        String(value || "").split(",").forEach(function (part) {
          var n = parseInt(String(part).replace(/[^0-9]/g, ""), 10);
          if (n > 0 && out.indexOf(n) === -1) {
            out.push(n);
          }
        });
        return out;
      }

      function coreAiNumbersFromRankedJsonField(fieldId) {
        var field = document.getElementById(fieldId);
        var raw = field ? String(field.value || "") : "";
        var out = [];

        if (!raw) {
          return out;
        }

        try {
          var parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
          if (!Array.isArray(parsed)) {
            return out;
          }

          for (var i = 0; i < parsed.length; i++) {
            var n = parseInt(parsed[i] && parsed[i].number, 10);
            if (n > 0 && out.indexOf(n) === -1) {
              out.push(n);
            }
          }
        } catch (_) {}

        return out;
      }

      function coreAiRecoverMainNumbersForSave(existing) {
        var recovered = existing && existing.length ? existing.slice() : [];

        if (recovered.length >= REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
          return recovered;
        }

        var hiddenMain = document.getElementById("saveMainNumbers");
        var hiddenNums = hiddenMain ? coreAiParseCsvNumbersForSave(hiddenMain.value) : [];

        if (hiddenNums.length >= REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
          return hiddenNums;
        }

        var rankedNums = coreAiNumbersFromRankedJsonField("saveRankedMainNumbersJson");

        if (rankedNums.length >= REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT) {
          return rankedNums;
        }

        return recovered;
      }

      function coreAiRecoverExtraNumbersForSave(existing) {
        var recovered = existing && existing.length ? existing.slice() : [];

        if (recovered.length) {
          return recovered;
        }

        var hiddenExtra = document.getElementById("saveExtraBallNumbers");
        var hiddenExtraNums = hiddenExtra ? coreAiParseCsvNumbersForSave(hiddenExtra.value) : [];

        if (hiddenExtraNums.length) {
          return hiddenExtraNums;
        }

        return coreAiNumbersFromRankedJsonField("saveRankedExtraNumbersJson");
      }

      mainNums = coreAiRecoverMainNumbersForSave(mainNums);
      extraNums = coreAiRecoverExtraNumbersForSave(extraNums);

      var hasValidNumbers = mainNums.length >= REQUIRED_MAIN_COUNT;

      /*
       * v15 restore: wait-until-finished, then user saves.
       * This copies the older working behavior requested by the user:
       * - Each batch run is only captured while the batch is running.
       * - Nothing is posted to PHP during the batch.
       * - When all runs are finished, the Save All 9 / Save Selected buttons appear.
       * - Those buttons write each captured run into the normal save form and submit it.
       */
      var verified = !!hasValidNumbers;

      batchResults[idx] = {
        combo: combo,
        html: res.html,
        text: res.text,
        done: verified,
        verified: verified,
        completionSignalOk: completionSignalOk,
        saveProof: hasValidNumbers
          ? (completionSignalOk ? "numbers_and_completion_events" : "valid_number_capture")
          : "incomplete_numbers",
        completionSignals: res.completionSignals || {},
        saved: false,
        savedId: 0,
        saveError: "",
        mainNumbers: mainNums,
        extraNumbers: extraNums
      };

      persistResults();

      batchDoneCount += 1;
      updateProgress();

      if (verified) {
        setCell(combo.profile, combo.strategy, buildBatchCellNode(idx, "Complete", "#16a34a", true), "done");
        setCurrentLabel(combo.label + " complete. Continuing batch...");
      } else {
        setCell(combo.profile, combo.strategy, "Complete - save check needed", "warning");
        setCurrentLabel(combo.label + " finished, but Core AI did not expose numbers to the batch snapshot. Continuing...");
      }

      setTimeout(runNext, AUTO_SAVE_DELAY_MS);
    });
  }

  function onBatchEnd() {
    batchRunning = false;
    setCurrentLabel(batchStopped ? "Batch stopped." : "All runs complete.");
    try { console.log("[SKAI batch] onBatchEnd: " + batchDoneCount + "/" + BATCH_COMBOS.length + " combos done, stopped=" + batchStopped); } catch (_) {}
    var saveRow = qs("skai-batch-save-row");
    if (saveRow && batchDoneCount > 0 && (batchStopped || batchDoneCount >= BATCH_COMBOS.length)) {
      saveRow.style.display = "flex";
    }
    if (!batchStopped && batchDoneCount >= BATCH_COMBOS.length) {
      setBatchSaveNote("Batch complete. Click Save All 9 to save every completed result, or Save Selected to choose specific runs.", "success");
    }
    var stopBtn = qs("skai-batch-stop");
    if (stopBtn) { stopBtn.disabled = true; }
  }

  function coreAiHtmlEscape(value) {
    return String(value == null ? "" : value)
      .replace(/&/g, "\u0026amp;")
      .replace(/</g, "\u0026lt;")
      .replace(/>/g, "\u0026gt;")
      .replace(/"/g, "\u0026quot;")
      .replace(/'/g, "\u0026#039;");
  }

  function coreAiUniqueBatchProfiles() {
    var seen = {}, out = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < BATCH_COMBOS.length; i++) {
      var p = coreAiCleanProfile(BATCH_COMBOS[i].profile);
      if (!seen[p]) { seen[p] = true; out.push(p); }
    }
    return out;
  }

  function coreAiUniqueBatchBlends() {
    var seen = {}, out = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < BATCH_COMBOS.length; i++) {
      var b = coreAiClampBlend(BATCH_COMBOS[i].blend_ai_pct);
      if (!seen[b]) { seen[b] = true; out.push(b); }
    }
    out.sort(function(a, b){ return a - b; });
    return out;
  }

  function coreAiFindComboIndex(profile, blend) {
    profile = coreAiCleanProfile(profile);
    blend = coreAiClampBlend(blend);
    for (var i = 0; i < BATCH_COMBOS.length; i++) {
      if (coreAiCleanProfile(BATCH_COMBOS[i].profile) === profile && coreAiClampBlend(BATCH_COMBOS[i].blend_ai_pct) === blend) {
        return i;
      }
    }
    return -1;
  }

  function coreAiMakeEl(tag, text, attrs) {
    var el = document.createElement(tag);
    if (typeof text !== "undefined" && text !== null) {
      el.textContent = String(text);
    }
    if (attrs) {
      for (var k in attrs) {
        if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(attrs, k)) { continue; }
        if (k === "style") { el.setAttribute("style", attrs[k]); }
        else if (k.indexOf("data-") === 0) { el.setAttribute(k, attrs[k]); }
        else { el.setAttribute(k, attrs[k]); }
      }
    }
    return el;
  }

  function coreAiClearNode(node) {
    while (node && node.firstChild) { node.removeChild(node.firstChild); }
  }

  function renderDynamicBatchGrid() {
    var grid = qs("skai-batch-grid");
    if (!grid) { return; }

    coreAiClearNode(grid);

    var profiles = coreAiUniqueBatchProfiles();
    var blends = coreAiUniqueBatchBlends();
    var useMatrix = (BATCH_COMBOS.length === 9 && profiles.length === 3 && blends.length === 3);
    var headStyle = "padding:6px 8px;background:#f3f4f6;border:1px solid #e5e7eb;";
    var cellStyle = "padding:6px 8px;border:1px solid #e5e7eb;text-align:center;";

    var thead = document.createElement("thead");
    var tbody = document.createElement("tbody");

    if (useMatrix) {
      var trHead = document.createElement("tr");
      trHead.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("th", "Focus / Blend", { style: headStyle + "text-align:left;" }));
      for (var hb = 0; hb < blends.length; hb++) {
        trHead.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("th", blends[hb] + "%", { style: headStyle + "text-align:center;" }));
      }
      thead.appendChild(trHead);

      var profileOrder = ["balanced", "explorative", "conservative"];
      var orderedProfiles = [];
      for (var op = 0; op < profileOrder.length; op++) {
        if (profiles.indexOf(profileOrder[op]) !== -1) { orderedProfiles.push(profileOrder[op]); }
      }
      for (var rp = 0; rp < profiles.length; rp++) {
        if (orderedProfiles.indexOf(profiles[rp]) === -1) { orderedProfiles.push(profiles[rp]); }
      }

      for (var pr = 0; pr < orderedProfiles.length; pr++) {
        var profile = orderedProfiles[pr];
        var tr = document.createElement("tr");
        tr.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("td", coreAiFocusLabelSafe(profile), {
          style: "padding:6px 8px;border:1px solid #e5e7eb;font-weight:700;background:#f9fafb;"
        }));
        for (var bc = 0; bc < blends.length; bc++) {
          var blend = blends[bc];
          var comboIdx = coreAiFindComboIndex(profile, blend);
          if (comboIdx >= 0) {
            var c = BATCH_COMBOS[comboIdx];
            var id = "skai-cell-" + c.profile + "-" + c.strategy;
            tr.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("td", "Pending", {
              id: id,
              style: cellStyle + "min-width:112px;",
              "data-profile": c.profile,
              "data-strategy": c.strategy,
              "data-run-index": String(comboIdx)
            }));
          } else {
            tr.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("td", "-", {
              style: cellStyle + "background:#f9fafb;color:#9ca3af;"
            }));
          }
        }
        tbody.appendChild(tr);
      }
    } else {
      var trHead2 = document.createElement("tr");
      trHead2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("th", "Run", { style: headStyle + "text-align:center;" }));
      trHead2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("th", "Focus", { style: headStyle + "text-align:left;" }));
      trHead2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("th", "Blend", { style: headStyle + "text-align:center;" }));
      trHead2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("th", "Status", { style: headStyle + "text-align:center;" }));
      thead.appendChild(trHead2);

      for (var i = 0; i < BATCH_COMBOS.length; i++) {
        var c2 = BATCH_COMBOS[i];
        var id2 = "skai-cell-" + c2.profile + "-" + c2.strategy;
        var tr2 = document.createElement("tr");
        tr2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("td", String(i + 1), {
          style: cellStyle + "font-weight:700;background:#f9fafb;"
        }));
        tr2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("td", coreAiFocusLabelSafe(c2.profile), {
          style: "padding:6px 8px;border:1px solid #e5e7eb;font-weight:600;background:#f9fafb;"
        }));
        tr2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("td", coreAiClampBlend(c2.blend_ai_pct) + "%", {
          style: cellStyle + "font-weight:700;"
        }));
        tr2.appendChild(coreAiMakeEl("td", "Pending", {
          id: id2,
          style: cellStyle,
          "data-profile": c2.profile,
          "data-strategy": c2.strategy,
          "data-run-index": String(i)
        }));
        tbody.appendChild(tr2);
      }
    }

    grid.appendChild(thead);
    grid.appendChild(tbody);
  }

  function resetGrid() {
    var cells = document.querySelectorAll("#skai-batch-grid td[data-profile]");
    for (var i = 0; i < cells.length; i++) {
      cells[i].textContent = "Pending";
      cells[i].style.background = "";
    }
  }

  function openDetail(idx) {
    var r = batchResults[idx];
    if (!r) { return; }
    var detail = qs("skai-batch-detail");
    var title = qs("skai-batch-detail-title");
    var body = qs("skai-batch-detail-body");
    if (!detail || !body) { return; }
    if (title) { title.textContent = r.combo.label; }
    body.textContent = r.text || "(no result text)";
    detail.style.display = "block";
  }

  function buildBatchCellNode(idx, statusText, color, includeView) {
    var wrap = document.createElement("span");
    var status = document.createElement("span");
    wrap.className = "core-ai-batch-cell-status";
    status.style.color = color || "#16a34a";
    status.style.fontWeight = "700";
    status.textContent = statusText;
    wrap.appendChild(status);
    if (includeView) {
      var viewLink = document.createElement("a");
      viewLink.href = "#";
      viewLink.className = "core-ai-batch-view-link";
      viewLink.style.fontSize = "0.8rem";
      viewLink.style.marginLeft = "4px";
      viewLink.setAttribute("data-batch-view", String(idx));
      viewLink.textContent = "View";
      wrap.appendChild(document.createTextNode(" "));
      wrap.appendChild(viewLink);
    }
    return wrap;
  }

  function renderCompletedCell(idx, saveOk, saveMessage) {
    var r = batchResults[idx];
    if (!r || !r.combo) { return; }
    if (saveOk) {
      setCell(r.combo.profile, r.combo.strategy, buildBatchCellNode(idx, "Saved", "#16a34a", true), "done");
      return;
    }
    setCell(r.combo.profile, r.combo.strategy, buildBatchCellNode(idx, "Save failed", "#dc2626", true), "error");
  }

  function setBatchSaveNote(message, tone) {
    var note = qs("skai-batch-save-note");
    if (!note) { return; }
    note.textContent = message || "";
    if (tone === "success") {
      note.style.color = "#065f46";
      note.style.background = "#ecfdf5";
      note.style.borderColor = "#a7f3d0";
    } else if (tone === "error") {
      note.style.color = "#991b1b";
      note.style.background = "#fef2f2";
      note.style.borderColor = "#fecaca";
    } else {
      note.style.color = "#1e3a5f";
      note.style.background = "#eff6ff";
      note.style.borderColor = "#bfdbfe";
    }
  }

  function encodeFormForBatchSave(form) {
    var pairs = [];
    var els = form ? form.elements : [];
    for (var i = 0; i < els.length; i++) {
      var el = els[i];
      if (!el || !el.name || el.disabled) { continue; }
      var type = (el.type || "").toLowerCase();
      if ((type === "checkbox" || type === "radio") && !el.checked) { continue; }
      if (type === "submit" || type === "button" || type === "file") { continue; }
      pairs.push(encodeURIComponent(el.name) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(el.value || ""));
    }
    pairs.push("save_set=1");
    return pairs.join("&");
  }

  /* v15: direct/post batch auto-save helpers removed. Save All 9 now uses the old working normal form-submit flow below. */

  function saveAllSequential(indices, doneCallback, saveCount, totalCount) {
    if (saveCount === undefined) { saveCount = 0; }
    if (totalCount === undefined) { totalCount = indices.length; }
    if (!indices || indices.length === 0) {
      if (doneCallback) { doneCallback(); }
      return;
    }
    var idx = indices[0];
    var rest = indices.slice(1);
    var r = batchResults[idx];
    if (!r || !r.done) {
      saveAllSequential(rest, doneCallback, saveCount, totalCount);
      return;
    }

    try { selectProfile(r.combo.profile); } catch (_) {}
    try { selectStrategy(r.combo.strategy); } catch (_) {}

    var form = qs("savePredictionForm");
    if (!form) {
      saveAllSequential(rest, doneCallback, saveCount, totalCount);
      return;
    }

    try {
      if (r.mainNumbers && r.mainNumbers.length) {
        window.skaiSaveMainOrdered  = r.mainNumbers.slice();
        window.skaiSaveExtraOrdered = (r.extraNumbers && r.extraNumbers.length)
          ? r.extraNumbers.slice() : [];
        var mainField = document.getElementById("saveMainNumbers");
        if (mainField) { mainField.value = r.mainNumbers.join(","); }
        var extraField = document.getElementById("saveExtraBallNumbers");
        if (extraField) { extraField.value = (r.extraNumbers || []).join(","); }
      }
      /* Update label to include combo name so each save is distinct */
      var LABEL_DELIMITER = " | ";
      var labelField = document.getElementById("saveLabel");
      if (labelField && r.combo && r.combo.label) {
        var baseLbl = labelField.value || "Prediction";
        /* Strip any previous combo suffix (format: "... | Combo Name") */
        var pipeIdx = baseLbl.indexOf(LABEL_DELIMITER);
        if (pipeIdx >= 0) { baseLbl = baseLbl.substring(0, pipeIdx); }
        labelField.value = baseLbl + LABEL_DELIMITER + r.combo.label;
      }
    } catch (_) {}

    /* Show saving progress: Saving 1 of 9, 2 of 9 ... */
    var currentSaveNum = saveCount + 1;
    if (window.skaiShowSaveToast) {
      window.skaiShowSaveToast("Saving " + currentSaveNum + " of " + totalCount + "...");
    }

    try {
      var batchUuidField = document.getElementById("saveBatchUuid");
      var batchIndexField = document.getElementById("saveBatchIndex");
      var batchTotalField = document.getElementById("saveBatchTotal");
      var batchTypeField = document.getElementById("saveBatchType");
      var riskField = document.getElementById("saveRiskProfile");
      var strategyField = document.getElementById("saveStrategyProfile");
      if (batchUuidField) { batchUuidField.value = coreAiBatchUuid(); }
      if (batchIndexField) { batchIndexField.value = String(idx + 1); }
      if (batchTotalField) { batchTotalField.value = String(BATCH_COMBOS.length); }
      if (batchTypeField) { batchTypeField.value = (CORE_AI_HANDOFF_BATCH ? "core_ai_range_test_9_batch" : "core_ai_precision_lock_9_batch"); }
      if (riskField && r.combo) { riskField.value = r.combo.profile || ""; }
      if (strategyField && r.combo) { strategyField.value = "blend_" + (r.combo.blend_ai_pct || 50); }
    } catch (_) {}

    var modeField = document.getElementById("saveModeKey");
    if (modeField && r.combo) {
      modeField.value = (r.combo.blend_ai_pct <= 30) ? "skip-dominant" : (r.combo.blend_ai_pct >= 70 ? "ai-forward" : "mixed");
    }
    if (typeof window.coreAiSetSignalBlendPct === "function" && r.combo && r.combo.blend_ai_pct) {
      window.coreAiSetSignalBlendPct(r.combo.blend_ai_pct);
    }
    var runField = document.getElementById("saveRunUuid");
    if (runField) { runField.value = ""; }
    var hashField = document.getElementById("saveClientResultHash");
    if (hashField) { hashField.value = ""; }

    function submitPreparedBatchSave() {
      var ev = document.createEvent("Event");
      ev.initEvent("submit", true, true);
      form.dispatchEvent(ev);

      setTimeout(function () {
        saveAllSequential(rest, doneCallback, currentSaveNum, totalCount);
      }, 2500); /* 2.5-second delay between sequential saves */
    }

    if (typeof window.skaiPrepareClientIntegrity === "function") {
      window.skaiPrepareClientIntegrity().then(submitPreparedBatchSave).catch(function () {
        if (window.skaiShowSaveToast) {
          window.skaiShowSaveToast("Could not prepare secure save for this batch run.", "error");
        }
        setTimeout(function () {
          saveAllSequential(rest, doneCallback, currentSaveNum, totalCount);
        }, 1200);
      });
    } else {
      submitPreparedBatchSave();
    }
  }

  function wireButtons() {
    var launchBtn = qs("skai-batch-launch");
    var modal = qs("skai-batch-modal");
    var confirmBtn = qs("skai-batch-confirm");
    var cancelBtn = qs("skai-batch-cancel");
    var stopBtn = qs("skai-batch-stop");
    var clearBtn = qs("skai-batch-clear");
    var detailClose = qs("skai-batch-detail-close");
    var saveAllBtn = qs("skai-batch-save-all");
    var saveSelBtn = qs("skai-batch-save-selected");

    if (launchBtn) {
      launchBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        if (modal) { modal.style.display = "flex"; }
      }, false);
    }

    if (cancelBtn) {
      cancelBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        if (modal) { modal.style.display = "none"; }
      }, false);
    }

    if (modal) {
      modal.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
        if (e.target === modal) { modal.style.display = "none"; }
      }, false);
    }

    if (confirmBtn) {
      confirmBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        hideModal();
        if (batchRunning) { return; }
        batchRunning = true;
        batchStopped = false;
        batchIndex = 0;
        batchDoneCount = 0;
        batchResults = [];
        var saveRow = qs("skai-batch-save-row");
        if (saveRow) { saveRow.style.display = "none"; }
        var stopBtn2 = qs("skai-batch-stop");
        if (stopBtn2) { stopBtn2.disabled = false; }
        var detailEl = qs("skai-batch-detail");
        if (detailEl) { detailEl.style.display = "none"; }
        renderDynamicBatchGrid();
        resetGrid();
        showPanel();
        updateProgress();
        setCurrentLabel("Starting...");
        setTimeout(runNext, 400);
      }, false);
    }

    if (stopBtn) {
      stopBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        batchStopped = true;
        batchRunning = false;
        setCurrentLabel("Stopping...");
      }, false);
    }

    if (clearBtn) {
      clearBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        batchStopped = true;
        batchRunning = false;
        batchResults = [];
        batchDoneCount = 0;
        batchIndex = 0;
        try { sessionStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY); } catch (_) {}
        renderDynamicBatchGrid();
        resetGrid();
        updateProgress();
        setCurrentLabel("Ready");
        var detail2 = qs("skai-batch-detail");
        if (detail2) { detail2.style.display = "none"; }
        var saveRow2 = qs("skai-batch-save-row");
        if (saveRow2) { saveRow2.style.display = "none"; }
        var monitorAnchor = qs("core-ai-batch-monitor-anchor");
        if (monitorAnchor) { monitorAnchor.style.display = "none"; }
      }, false);
    }

    if (detailClose) {
      detailClose.addEventListener("click", function () {
        var d = qs("skai-batch-detail");
        if (d) { d.style.display = "none"; }
      }, false);
    }

    var grid = qs("skai-batch-grid");
    if (grid) {
      grid.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
        var t = e.target;
        if (t && t.getAttribute("data-batch-view") !== null) {
          try { e.preventDefault(); } catch (_) {}
          openDetail(parseInt(t.getAttribute("data-batch-view"), 10));
        }
      }, false);
    }

    if (saveAllBtn) {
      saveAllBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        if (!window.confirm("Save all completed runs to your dashboard?")) { return; }
        var indices = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < batchResults.length; i++) {
          if (batchResults[i] && batchResults[i].done && !batchResults[i].saved) { indices.push(i); }
        }
        if (indices.length === 0) {
          alert("No completed runs are available to save.");
          return;
        }
        var totalRuns = indices.length;
        saveAllSequential(indices, function () {
          if (window.skaiShowSaveToast) { window.skaiShowSaveToast("All " + totalRuns + " " + (totalRuns === 1 ? "run" : "runs") + " saved to your dashboard."); }
        });
      }, false);
    }

    if (saveSelBtn) {
      saveSelBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        var available = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < batchResults.length; i++) {
          if (batchResults[i] && batchResults[i].done && !batchResults[i].saved) { available.push(i); }
        }
        if (available.length === 0) {
          alert("No completed runs are available to save.");
          return;
        }
        var labels = [];
        for (var j = 0; j < available.length; j++) {
          labels.push((j + 1) + ". " + batchResults[available[j] ].combo.label);
        }
        var input = window.prompt(
          "Enter the numbers (comma-separated) of the runs you want to save:\n\n" + labels.join("\n"),
          "1"
        );
        if (!input) { return; }
        var chosen = [];
        var parts = input.split(",");
        for (var k = 0; k < parts.length; k++) {
          var n = parseInt(parts[k].trim(), 10);
          if (!isNaN(n) && n >= 1 && n <= available.length) {
            chosen.push(available[n - 1]);
          }
        }
        if (chosen.length === 0) { alert("No valid selections."); return; }
        saveAllSequential(chosen, function () {
          if (window.skaiShowSaveToast) { window.skaiShowSaveToast("Selected runs saved."); }
        });
      }, false);
    }
  }

  function init() {
    renderDynamicBatchGrid();
    wireButtons();
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY); } catch (_) {}
    try {
      var params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search || "");
      if ((params.get("core_ai_autorun") || "") === "1") {
        var launchBtn = qs("skai-batch-launch");
        if (launchBtn && typeof launchBtn.click === "function") { setTimeout(function(){ launchBtn.click(); }, 600); }
      }
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  if (document.readyState === "loading") {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", init, {once: true});
  } else {
    init();
  }
})();
[[/script]]
